et la moille en oile, et l’emprens au feu, et cauterize I cautere entre la forcele et lou col, et II petis cauteres un poc en dessendant en la partie qui est desoz la barbe;	and anoint it in oil, and heat it in embers, and cauterize the large cautery between the armpit and the neck, and two small cauteries a little lower down on the part that is under the beard;
et II cauteres entre la quinte coste et la sisime, en declinant derrier un poc;	and perform cauterization between the fifth and sixth ribs, inclining slightly backward.
et I cautere emmi le pis, et I autre sus l’estomac, et I entre II espaules, et II as II costez dou pis defuers le cautere qui est entre II espaules;	and one cautery in the groin, and one above the stomach, and one between the shoulders, and two at either side of the groin below the cautery between the shoulders;
et ne presser mie ta main, ains fai apertement ausi com en odorant.	and do not press your hand, but do it plainly as in perfumery.
Et dirent aucun ancien que aucun home usent de cautere de feir semblant a I raseur, et l’eschaufent et le mettent entre les costes, tant qu’il vient a cel aposteme;	And some ancient ones said that one should use an iron cautery like a razor, heat it and place it between the ribs, until it reaches that abscess.
et saut fuers li dolor, si com nos avons dit en l’aposteme dou foie.	and jump out of the pain, as we have said about the abscess in the liver.
Mais en cestui ovraige est paour ou li malaides muert maintenant, ou fistule i vient qui ne puet estre sanee.	But in this operation there is fear of death for the patient, or a fistula occurs which cannot be healed.
de la mice	of the mouse
Quant tu cures la maladie de la mice de ceu que nos avons dit as divisions des cures, et il ne profite mie, adonques i afierent .iij. manieres de cautere que tuit sont boin.	When you treat the disease of warts with what we have said about the divisions of treatment, and it does not help, then they resort to three methods of cauterization, all of which are good.
Desquelz li une maniere si est que tu faices III cauteres, ou IIII, en lignant selonc la longor de la mice, selonc la figure dou cautere dou foie que nos avons dit devant;	Of these, one method is that you make three or four cauteries, aligning them according to the length of the mouse, and according to the shape of the cautery of the liver which we have described before.
et n’apresser mie ta main a tout le cautere, et soit li malaides sovins sor son dos;	and do not press your hand to the entire cautery, and let the patient lie on his back;
et une autre maniere de cautere si est que tu eschaufe le cautere qui a II ners, si com nos l’avons mostreit en la dislocation de l’espaule;	and another way of cauterization is to heat the cautery which has the nerve, as we have shown in the dislocation of the shoulder;
et lieve le keur qui est endroit la mice, ou li coutes dou malaide vient devers senestre, et soit li elevations dont tu lieves le keur selonc la keur, selonc la longesce dou cors, et li cautere soient selonc la largesce dou cors.	and lift the skin where the mouse is, or the wound comes from the left side, and let the elevation be according to the skin, according to the length of the body, and the cautery according to the width of the body.
Aprés i boute les II ners enflamez tant que li keurs soit perciez de l’autre part, et puis trai fuers le cautere, et ensi en i avra IIII.	Afterwards, push the heated cautery into the nerve until it pierces through to the other side, and then pull out the cautery, and in this way there will be four holes.
Et se tu vues, si cauterize a tot le cautere a III ners.	And if you see that it is necessary, then cauterize with the entire cautery at three nerves.
Aprés le cure quant il a geteit porriture par lonc tens, et ce vaut mues que li autre des cures devant dites.	After the ulcer has healed for a long time, it is worth more than the other ulcers mentioned earlier.
de ydropisie	of dropsy
Cautere ne vaut a ydropique, fors c’a la maniere qui est apelee «asclytes».	A cautery is not suitable for an epidenitis, except in the manner that is called "asclytes.
Quant tu la cures selonc les manieres que nos avons dit en divisions, et ta cure ne profite mie, adonques covient il que tu li faices IIII cauteres entor la boude, et I sus l’estomac, et un sus le foie, et I sus la mice, et II derrier le dos sus l’espinee, et I endroit le pis;	When you treat it according to the methods we have described in divisions, and your treatment is not helping, then you must make four cauteries around the armpit, one on the stomach, one on the liver, one on the mouse, two behind the back on the spine, and one on the buttock;
et soit li cauteres bien pres de l’espés dou keur.	and the cautery should be applied close to the thick part of the heart.
Aprés laisse le cautere aovert por giter porriture lonc tens, et ne lassier mie la cure dou malaide aprés le cautere;	Afterwards, let the cautery remain open for a long time, and do not stop treating the disease after the cautery;
et sanation se hasterait, et seront ensamble les II ententions avec l’aide de Deu.	and healing will be hastened, and the two intentions with the help of God will come together.
Li forme dou cautere por le ventre soit li clavile que nos avons devant mostreit;	The shape of the cautery for the belly should be like the key that we have shown before;
et cil por le dos soit olivaire, selonc ceu qu’il est ci devant mis.	and that for the back should be olive-shaped, according to what is shown there.
de l’enfleure des piez	of foot swelling
Quant li piez sont enflez a celui qui est ydropique, et sont plain d’awe citrine, il covient que tu cauterizes sus le dos dou piet entre l’auriculaire et l’anulaire;	When the feet are swollen in the case of dropsy, and they are full of yellow water, you should cauterize on the back of the foot between the little toe and the ring finger;
et lieve ta main avec le cautere sens torner.	and move your hand with the cautery without turning it.
Et n’entrer mie trop em parfont, ensi sarrait fuers li awe citrine, et soit li cauteres selonc cest forme:	And do not go too deep, thus one will avoid the yellow awl, and let the cautery follow this form:
Aprés fai sus II jambes II cauteres en chescune jambe a la pointe dou cutellaire;	Afterwards, make two cauteries on each leg at the point of the tibia;
et soit li cauteres dou lonc, l’un desoz le genoil devant et l’autre defuers, enmi la jambe;	and let the cautery be long, one below the knee in front and the other behind, in the middle of the leg;
et laisse les cauteres aovers longement sens curer, que li awe en isse;	and leave the cauteries for a long time without curing, until the evil comes out;
aprés le cure des autres cures que nos avons dit.	after the other cures that we have spoken of.
de la menoison	of menstruation
Quant solution de ventre vient de froidor et de moistor, tant que li vertus retentive et digestive qui est ou stomac et en l’intestine est afleboie, et ne puet estre curez par manieres de cures;	When a distension of the belly comes from cold and moisture, as long as the retentive and digestive power which is in the stomach and intestines is impaired, and cannot be cured by any means of curing;
et tu vois le malaide bien soffrant et de fort vertut, si fai I grant cautere sus l’estomac selonc ceu qu’il en a parleit ci devant ou cautere de l’estomac, au cautere circule;	and you see the patient suffering greatly and very weak, then make a large cautery on the stomach according to what has been spoken of before about the cautery of the stomach, with a circulating cautery;
et IIII cauteres entor la boude subtilz a tout I cautere clavile subtil, et II cauteres sus les hainches.	and make 4 cauteries around the belly subtle and within each cautery a subtle cautery-needle, and 2 cauteries on the hips;
Et se tu vois les moistors habundans et le malaide soffrant, se li fai cautere sus le poignil, et .i. cautere sus chaicun yle, et .ij. petis cauteres sus l’estomac delez le grant, car li cure est profitans quant il i a bone aide.	And if you see abundant moisture and the patient suffering, make a cautery on the shoulder, and one cautery on each elbow, and two small cauteries on the stomach below the large one, for the treatment is beneficial when there is good support.
de la cure des emorroydes	on the treatment of hemorrhoids
Quant les emorroydes sont ou fondement, ou une ou plusors, et sont ancienes et sont de grosses humors froides et moistes corrumpues, et sont curees si com nos avons dit en divisions, et il ne profite mie, si fai cauteres:	When the hemorrhoids are in the anus, one or more, and are old and consist of large amounts of cold and moist corrupted humors, and they are treated as we have said by division, and it does not help to make cauteries:
III sus l’espine dou dos, celi qui est tout defuers desoz almecdate poc et poc en triangulant, et I cautere desoz la boude II dois;	III on the spine of the back, that which is all out of alignment below, tap and tap in a triangular shape, and I cauterize below the armpit II times;
et se tu penses que ses estomac soit refroidiez, et li viande ne cuise, et on voit enfler la faice, adonques li faice on I grant cautere sus le stomac, si com il est devant dit, et I autre sus le foie, et I autre sus la mice a tout le cautere clavile;	and if you think his stomach is cold, and the meat is not digesting, and one sees the face swell, then on the face we make the great cautery on the stomach, as it was said before, and another on the liver, and another on the mouse with the whole cauterization of the clavicle;
et laisse le cautere overt lonc tens.	and let the cautery remain open a long time.
Aprés cure le leu tant qu’il soit sanez.	After cleaning the wound until it heals.
de la charnositeit qui est nommee «thelul»	of the carnosity which is named "thelul"
Quant tu copes althelul, si eschaufe le cautere qui semble I raseur, et puis le met tout embraseit sus cel althelul copeit;	When you cut the skin, heat the cauterizer which resembles a razor, and then place it all ablaze on the copped skin;
et i laisse tant ta main que li cauteres viegne a la naissance de la voine, de coi li sans cort;	and leave your hand so that the cautery comes to the origin of the vein, from which the blood flows.
fai ceu une fois ou II, et s’il i a mout d’althelul, si cauterize chaicun si com nos avons dit;	Do this once or twice, and if there is much inflammation, then cauterize each one as we have said.
aprés les cure d’oignemens profitans tant qu’il soient sanez;	After the treatment of the wounds with beneficial ointments until they are healed.
et se tu cauterizes d’un cautere grant sus alchatim, si avra plus grant aide.	And if you cauterize with a large cautery on the ulcer, it will have greater benefit.
de plaie mal curee	of a badly cured wound
Quant li malaides ne puet soffrir tailleure ne overture, que nos raconterons en son leu, si vient teil maladie que ne puet estre sanee fuer que par cautere.	When the patient cannot endure cutting or opening, which we will discuss in its place, such a disease comes that it cannot be healed except by cautery.
Quant a aucun vient fistule, et est enveillie et giete porriture et moistors corrumpues, si la doies prover a tot une tente subtil, et garde que tu saiches a tot la tente combien elle a de parfont.	When there is a fistula, and it becomes suppurating and oozing corrupted moisture, then you must probe it with a thin rod, and be careful that you know how deep the rod goes into the tent.
Aprés eschaufe le cautere qui semble I raseur, et le boute en la fistule selonc la quantiteit que li tente i est entrée, et rencomence lou cautere tant que cil cors porris et corrumpus soient ars, une fois, ou II ou III, selonc la quantiteit de som besoing;	After heating the cautery which seems right to the surgeon, insert it into the fistula according to the amount that the pus has entered, and repeat the cautery until the infected and rotten flesh is burnt, once, or twice or three times, according to the amount of its need.
et te warde d’ardre lé nerf qui sunt enqui, et des grans voinnes.	And be careful not to burn any nerve that is there, and the large veins.
se li fistule vait au cors de la vesie et a l’intestine, si te warde de ces leus, et ne faire ceu fuers que en leu charnut, et pense qu’ele n’est mie persans;	If the fistula goes into the bladder and intestine, then be careful of those places, and do not push too hard, and think that it is not a sensitive spot.
aprés cure le leu tant qu’il soit sanez, et se li leus est saielez, et les matieres sont ostees lonc tens, adonc saiches que li leus est sanez entierement;	after curing the wound until it is healed, and if the wound is suppurating and the matter has been discharged for a long time, then once you see that the wound is completely healed;
et se les matieres ne sont ostees, saiche que li leus est troez, et corrumpus li os au font;	and if the matter has not been discharged, know that the wound is infected and the bone at the bottom is rotten;
et ensi com un de ces que nos dirons en son leu.	and thus according to one of those we will say in their place.
de la maladie des reins	of kidney disease
Quant dolor de froit vient as rains, et de grosse ventositeit, et ne prent talant de femme, adonc covient il que tu li fais cautere sus les rains d’une part et d’autre au cautere clavile que nos avons devant dit;	When cold pain comes with heavy rains and strong winds, and does not take hold of a woman, then you should make a cautery on the breasts on both sides using the claw-shaped cautery instrument we described earlier;
et se nos le cauterizons em mileu, si avra III cauteres en ligne, et se feront plus grant aide.	and if we cauterize it in the middle, then there should be three cauteries in a line, and they will be of greater help.
de la vessie	of the bladder
Quant li vessie est mole et foible de froit et de moistor, si que li malaides retient l’urine, adonc li fai cautere en la partie defuers sus la vessie, la ou encomencent li poil dou poignil, et I a destre et I a senestre, et soit chescuns cauteres si lons com li nous d’un poce;	When the bladder is soft and weak due to cold and moisture, and the patient retains urine, then make a cautery on the underside of the penis, where the hairs begin at the base, one on the right and one on the left, and each cautery should be as long as the tip of a finger;
et li fais I cautere defuers le dos, ou II se tu en as besoing;	and make a fire cautery on his back, or wherever you need it.
et soit li cauteres clavile selon la forme devant dite.	and the cautery should be made in the shape described above.
de la marris	of the mare
Quant li marrix est froide et moiste, et ne laisse mie por ceu a concevoir, et les flors sont corrumpues et lor termines tarde;	When the body is cold and moist, and fails to conceive, and the flowers are corrupt and their termini late;
et quant elles vienent, si sent grant dolor:	and when they come, there is great pain;
adonques covient il c’on li faice III cauteres entor la boude, si com nos avons dit ou cautere de la vessie, et II cauteres defuers le dos;	therefore, one must make three cauteries around the womb, as we have said in the cautery for the bladder, and two fire cauteries on the back;
et soit li cauteres clavile, si com nos avons dit.	and the cautery should be made in the shape described above.
de la hainche	of the hip
Quant les moistors viscouses dessendent a la boiste de la hainche, et por ceste cause si se muet de son leu, et li signes est que li cuisse est plus longe que li autre quant on le mesure ensamble;	When viscous moistures descend into the box of the hip, and because of this, it dislocates from its place, and the sign is that the thigh is longer than the other when one measures them together;
et est trovez li leus dou departement vuis, si covient que tu cauterizes le malaide sus la boiste de la hainche a I cautere semblant au cercle, et seigne devant le leu entor la boiste si com elle torne, si que li boiste soit dedens le cercle;	and the place of the dislocation is found hollow, then one must cauterize the patient on the hip at one cautery similar to a circle, and mark around the hip in front of the location as it turns, so that the hip is within the circle;
et si soit li cauteres telz com cil dont on a cauterizeit le stomac.	and if it is such a cautery as that with which one cauterizes the stomach.
Et se cist cauteres ne t’est presens, se li fai III cauteres de l’olivaire grans, et soit li cauteres ausi parfont com tous li keurs;	And if this cautery is not present, make three large olive-stone cauteries, and let the cauteries be as deep as all the ulcers.
et le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	and cure it until it is healed.
de la dolor de la hainche	of hip pain
Quant dolor vient en la boiste de la hainche, et c’est de froidor et de moistor, et li malaides est curez de ceu que nos avons dit en la division et li cure ne vaut, et li maladie est anciene:	When pain comes in the hip joint, and it is from coldness and moisture, and the disease is cured of what we have said in the section and the cure does not work, and the disease is old:
adonc covient il que tu purges le malaide des grosses humors de pilules fetides, ou autres pilules bones semblans.	then you must purge the disease of the gross humors with stinking pills, or other good-smelling pills like them.
Aprés li fai cautere;	After that, make a cautery:
et li maniere dou cautere si est selonc II manieres:	and the way of the cautery is according to two ways:Car il faut adonc prendre le fu de l’olivaire et li fai III cauteres
c’est a savoir ensamble medicines ardans, et cautere de feu.	That is to say, together with burning medicines, and fire cauteries.
Cautere de feu si est selonc mout de manieres, desquelz li uns est telz:	Fire cautery can be performed in many ways, one of which is as follows:
que tu cauterize sus la boiste de la hainche III cauteres triangulalz selonc ceste forme, et i fai bone profunditeit et grant, et ait entre chaicun cautere d’espaice la groissece d’un doi, et soit li cauteres olivaire;	that you cauterize on the hip joint in a triangular shape according to this pattern, and make each cautery deep and large, with the distance between each cautery the thickness of a thumb, and let the cauteries be olive-shaped.
aucune fois fait on cautere en mileu sus lou chief de la hainche, por coi il en i a IIII selonc ceste forme:	sometimes cauterization is performed in the middle of the hip joint, with four cauteries according to this pattern:
Et se tu vues, si le cauterize au cautere dou cercle que nos avons devant dit en la dislocation de la hainche;	And if you wish, cauterize it with a circular cautery as we have described before for dislocation of the hip.
mais fai en teil maniere que li cercles conteigne toute la hainche, et tous li espés dou keur soit ars.	But do it in such a way that the circle contains all of the hip, and all of the soft tissue is burned.
Et c’est li maniere c’on fait en sciatique, quant li dolor tient en la hainche, et ne parvient mie jusc’a la cuisse ne jusc’a la jambe.	And that is the way they do it in sciatica when the pain is in the hip and does not reach the thigh or leg.
Et s’ele vient jusc’a la cuisse et la jambe, se li fai II cauteres lai ou li malaides dit que li dolor li tient, et I cautere desus la cheville IIII dois, a la partie senestre un poc;	And if it extends to the thigh and leg, make two cauteries where the patient says the pain is, and one cautery above the ankle on both sides.
et soit li cauteres cutellaire, et soit arse li espesseté dou keur;	and let the cautery be with a hot iron, and burn the thickness of the skin;
et se li malaides sent que li dolor s’estende jusc’a dois dou piet ou pres d’enqui, se le cauterize la ou il sent la dolor III poins ou IIII au cautere qui est apelez «poins».	and if the pain extends to the top of the foot or near there, cauterize where they feel the pain three points or four with the cautery that is called a "point.
Et se mestiers est, se li en fai plus;	And if need be, do more.
et se il seit que li dolor soit desoz le genoil vers la cuisse, se li fais cautere au cautere cutellaire ou circulaire, et te done bien garde en tous tes cauteres que tu n’i lassier mie tant le cautere que tu brules les ners et les grans arteres, et que tu ne faices au malaide plus grant nuisance et contraction.	And if it seems that the pain is beneath the knee toward the thigh, cauterize with the flat or circular cautery; and be careful in all your cauteries not to let the iron stay so long as to burn the nerves and large arteries, nor to cause greater harm and contraction to the patient.
Et je meisme ai veus plusors qui ont fait cautere sus la cheville dou piet, et li lasserent tant que li jambe fut toute enflee, et li piez ausi, et fut perciez et corrumpus toz li piez.	And I myself have seen many who had cautery on the ankle of the foot, and they left it until the leg was completely swollen, and the foot as well, and it became pierced and all the feet were corrupted.
Aprés une solution de ventre dont il ot la mort.	After a stomach ache which caused his death.
Et se li dolors est en II parties ensamble, fai cautere en l’une et en l’autre, selonc ceste maniere.	And if the pain is in two places together, do cautery in one and then the other, according to this method.
Et li saige dirent en la cautere de la hainche, de coi ci est li maniere, fai I tel fer et soit au chief ausi gros com uns nauvillon de dacte, ou un poc moins, et soit par entrechetres et soit des l’un entrechetres jusc’a l’autre d’espaice la quantiteit d’un nou de poce;	And the wise men say about the cautery of the hip, from which this is the way: make such an iron and let it be as wide at the tip as a little finger, or a bit less, and let it be serrated on both edges with the space between each serration being the thickness of a finger joint;
et soient li entrechetres aovers de II pars, et soient aussi comme noez, et i ait I mainche de fer bien fait;	and let the tongs be divided into two parts, and also be like noses, and let it have one handle of well-made iron;
et c’est li forme:	and this is the form:
Et soit eschaufez tant qu’il soit toz rouges et giete senteles, et puis le mette on sus la boiste de la hainche malaide, et soit tornez sus lou sain costeit;	And let it be heated until it is all red and glowing, and then place it on the box of the diseased hip, and then turn it over to the healthy side;
et lou cauterize une fois I cautere reont et lou laisse III jors;	and cauterize it once with the cautery and leave it for three days;
et puis fai emplaustre de burre, et laisse la plaie aoverte lonc tens;	and then make an ointment from suet, and let the wound remain open for a long time;
aprés la cure d’oignement tant qu’il soit sanez.	after the treatment with ointment until it is healed.
Albucasim dit que nos usons poc de cest cautere por la paor de son regart, et se voions poc qui en usent;	Albucasim says that we use this cautery sparingly due to the fear of its appearance, and those who use it sparingly see little success;
et toutevoie ceu est des boins cauteres, qui le puet soffrir, et lai ou il s’afiert.	Nevertheless, it is one of the good cauteries that can be endured by those who are able to tolerate it and in the places where it is effective.
Li cauteres de medicine ardant si est que tu faices I estrument a entrechetres en coi dessende li marge de la porte, et soit d’arain ou de fer a une paroit longe, et en la hautece ait II nous, et ait entre chaicun la quantiteit de la groissece d’un doi;	The cautery of medicine burns if you make the instrument to interlace in such a way that the edge of the door descends, and it is made of bronze or iron with one side long, and in the thickness it has 2 nuts, and between each there is the quantity of the thickness of a finger.
et soient overt defuer et desus, et se joignent ensamble selonc ceste forme:	and they are open below and above, and join together according to this form:
Aprés met sus la boiste de la hainche au malaide gisant sor suin costeit sain, et apresse ta main mout sus la boiste de la hainche;	Afterwards place the box of the hip on the patient lying on his healthy side, and then press your hand firmly on the box of the hip.
aprés giete entre les II cercles de l’awe chaude qui soit chaufee au feu I poc, et li laisse une houre dou tens, et soffre li malaides la chalor et l’arsure de li.	Afterwards pour between the two circles of the hot awe which is heated in the fire for one hour, and let the patient endure the heat and scorching.
Car il i trueve mordication ausi com de feu;	For he will find relief as from fire;
et quant li mordications iert passee, se lieve ta main avec l’estrument et leve la hainche d’awe douce, et laisse ensi III jors, et met sus burre tant que ceu qui est noir de l’eschaudure soit osteit;	And when the burning is passed, lift your hand with the instrument and raise the hip gently, and leave it thus for three days, and put on butter until that which was scorched is healed.
et lou laisse III jors que porriture en istrait;	and let him for three days until the swelling goes down;
et ceu serait li derriene aide aprés le cure d’oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez.	and this would be the last remedy after treating with ointments until it is healed.
Et se li dolor s’est estendue jusc’a la cuisse ou jusc’a la jambe, se li fai I estrument que teigne awe selonc ceu que tu as fait en la hainche igaument;	And if the pain extends to the thigh or leg, then make the instrument that colors red according to how you made it in the hip dislocation;
et c’est li maniere de l’awe chaude, et je l’ai escripte ou traitier de la rectification de medicine.	and this is the manner of the hot color, and I have written it in the treatise on the rectification of medicines.
Pren alcali et chaulz vive, autant de l’une com de l’autre, et les broie ensamble, et les met en I nuef pot.	Take alkali and quicklime, as much of each, and grind them together, and put them in a nine-pot.
ou il ait I petit pertuis defuer se que li pointe d’un raisor i puisse entreir;	where there is a small hole so that the point of a needle can enter;
et met desor celui pot I autre pot bien plombeit, et met sus alcali et chalz et awe douce sus, tant qu’il en i ait I doi desus les poudres cant tu l’avras bien preingte a ta main;	and then put another pot well-plumbed on top of it, and place an alkali and heat and the red dye on top, until there is two fingers' worth of powder above the liquids, after you have mixed it well with your hand;
et le laisse ensi tant qu’il en dessende awe ague et chiece ou pot plombeit, puis pren toute cele awe, et la giete sus chalz et sus alcali si com devant.	and let it be thus until dye water and pieces fall into the plumbed pot; then take all that dye, and pour it over heat and alkali as before.
Et lors si sera mout ague et est aministree en mou d’ovraiges de medicine et en cauteres d’autres membres.	And then there will be a fever, which is treated with various medical remedies and cauteries on other limbs.
Car elle fait auteil oevre com feus, et si a autres medicines dont on cauterize bien la hainche ensi com tesisie et miel anacardi et chalz avec savon, toutes ces choses mellees ensamble.	Because it does the same harm as fire, and there are other remedies with which one can cauterize the hip just like this: theriac, and honey of aniseed, and chalk mixed with soap. All these things mixed together.
Et Galiens nos raconte une cure dont uns hons fut curez de la dolor de la hainche et de la voine sciatique, et lou loe mout, et dit que on n’i fist autre cure, et qu’il en fut sanez a une soule fois quant on ot fait ceste cure, et il se fut baigniez si com il l’enseigne ci aprés.	And Galen tells of a remedy by which a man was cured of sciatic pain and a vein in his hip, and he praises it highly, saying that nothing else was done to him, and that he was healed in one go after this treatment, and that he then bathed as instructed below.
Et dist en teil maniere que tu preignes dou litargire vert fres et sec, et le broie mout avec I poc de graisse, et met sus la hainche et sus la cuisse et sus la jambe ou la dolor tient, et la lie;	And you should prepare it in this way: take litarge in powder, dry and green, and grind it a lot with a little grease, and apply it to the hip and thigh and leg where the pain is located, and leave it there;
et li laisse III houres et par la quantiteit que li malaides ne sente plus l’arsure.	and leave it for three hours until the patient no longer feels the burning sensation. Then, take off the litarge and wash the area with wine, and if the pain still remains, repeat the process again.
Et puis le fai entrer ou bain tant que li cors li soit un poc arousez, et lou fai entrer ou lit, et li dolor s’en ira toute et sera sanez.	And then he enters the bath until his body is somewhat warmed, and he enters the bed, and the pain will go away completely and he will be healed.
Et saiches que nuls ne doit user de cautere de telz medicines, se ceu n’est aprés l’evacuation de cors.	And know that no one should use such medicine with cautery unless after the evacuation of the body's fluids.
Et Dyascorides dist que quant li voine sciatique est cauterizee de fiens de chievre, si i aide mout;	And Dioscorides says that when the sciatic vein is cauterized with goat's dung, it helps a lot;
et doit estre fais li cauteres en teil maniere.	and the cautery must be done in such a way.
Prenez lainne et la beurez d’oile vielz, et metez sus la fossete qui est entre le pouce dou piez et l’autre qui est apelez foscile.	Take lamb's wool and grease it with old oil, and place it in the hollow between the big toe of the foot and the one next to it, which is called the 'foscile'.
Aprés pren fiens de chievre sec, et l’empren a feu tant qu’il soit charbons, et lou met sus la laine, et le laisse tant qu’il soit estains;	Take dry goat's hair, and take it to the fire until it is charcoal, and place it on the wool, and let it be until it turns ash;
et refai encor ensi, et ne cesser de faire ensi tant que tu penses par sens qu’il viegne jusc’a la hainche, et que li dolor soit cessee;	And do this again, and do not stop doing this until you feel through sensation that it has reached the hip, and the pain has ceased;
et cist manieres de cautere est apelez «cautere de chievre».	and this method of cautery is called "goat's hair cautery".
de la dolor dou dos	of the pain in the back
Quant dolor vient au dos, ou par cheoir ou de percussion ou par trop grant evacuation, ou par semblans de matiere espandue froide, a nule de ces semblances ne vaut cauteres, fuer que a celi qui vient de infusion de froide matiere.	When pain comes in the back, whether from falling or impact or from excessive evacuation, or from similar appearances of cold matter, none of these appearances are worth cauterizing for, except for that which comes from the diffusion of cold matter.
Il covient c’aprés ceu que li malaides est voidiez de pilules fetides ou d’autres semblans, que on li faice sus lou dos, lai ou li dolor tient, trois lignes signies d’enche, et en chescune ligne V cauteres ou plus selonc la vertut et la quantiteit que li malaides puet soffrir;	After this, the patient should be bled with foul pills or similar, applied to their back where the pain is located, drawing three lines across, and in each line making V cauteries or more depending on the strength and amount that the patient can endure;
et soit fait li cauteres selonc le cautere qui est apelez «poins»;	and the cautery should be done according to the cautery called "points";
et se tu vues, fai III cauteres ou IIII au cautere clavile moien selonc ceste forme:	and if you see, make three cauteries or four with the clave cautery tool according to this form:
Maintes fois vient ceste maladie as petis enfans, et li signes de l’encomencement si est qu’il ont estroite alainne quant il se lievent, et paor;	This disease often affects young children, and the signs of its onset are that they have a narrow throat when they wake up, and fear.
et tu trueves en la derriene espinee dou dos et en nous l’apparance qui vient sus les autres espinees.	You will find it in the spine at the back, and the appearance of the others that come above the spine.
Quant tu vois ceu et tu le vues curer, si le cauterize au cautere de celcle selonc ceste forme.	When you see this and you cure it, then cauterize it with a silver cautery according to this form.
Si que li cautere porpreigne chescune partie de l’espinee egaument.	So that the purple cautery evenly affects each part of the spine.
Et se tu vues, si cauterize entor l’espinee au cautere poignant II lignes ou III, et soient li poins pres l’uns de l’autre.	And if you see, cauterize around the spine with a pointed cautery 2 or 3 lines apart, and have the points close to each other.
Aprés cure le leu tant qu’il soit sanez selonc ceu que nos avons dit, et warde que tu n’amenistrer cautere en gilbositeit qui soit en spame de nerf.	Afterwards, heal the site until it is healthy according to what we have said, and be careful not to apply cautery to any area that is swollen with pus and is affecting a nerve.
de la dolor des jointes	of the pain of the joints
Quant dolor de jointes sunt de moistors que sont espandues a chaicun membre dou cors, et quant dolor vient em piez, que li mire apelent «podagre» proprement, et quant elle est de froide cause et cures de medicines ne la puent curer, si est curez par cauteres en teil maniere:	When joint pain is caused by moistors that are expanded in each part of the body, and when it comes from the feet, which they call "podagre" properly, and when it is from a cold cause and does not heal with medicines, then it is healed with cauteries in such a way:
fai li mout de cauteres entor la jointure dou piet, et soit li cauteres olivaire selonc ceste forme:	Make the mouth of cauteries around the joint of the foot, and let the cautery be olive-shaped according to this form:
Et s’il i a besoigne que tu poignes sus la faice dou piet, se li fai cautere a tot le cautere c’on claime «point».	And if there is a need to prick on the sole of the foot, do so with the entire cautery that one calls «point».
Et se les dolors viegnent jusc’a genous et as autres jointures, et ceu avient maintes fois, se li fai cautere sus chaicun genoil III cauteres ou IIII de chescunne partie, a tout le cautere olivaire;	And if the pains come up to the knees and the other joints, and this happens many times, then do cautery on each knee with three cauteries or four of each part, all in the olive-shaped cautery;
et se tu as mestier de plus, si en fai plus, mais n’i tenir mie ta main fuers que tant que li espés dou keur soit ars.	And if you need more, then do more, but don't hold your hand against it any longer than the thick of your heart is burnt.
Et se les dolors dessendent jusc’a genoil et au dos, se li aministre le cautere que nos avons dit en son chapistre.	And if the pains descend to the knee and back, administer the cautery we have described in its chapter.
Et se les dolors sunt as mains, si fai poins entor le foscile II lignes;	And if the pains are in the hands, then make points around the wrist two lines;
et s’il remaint point de dolor as dois, si fai poins sus chescune jointe et sus lou poil de la main;	and if there remains no pain in the fingers, then make points on every joint and on the hair of the hand;
et se les dolors vienent jusc’as coutes ou jusc’as espaules, si cauterize chescune partie, et fai boin governement au malaide et penre medicines.	and if the pains come up to the elbows or shoulders, then cauterize every part and make good government for the patient and take medicine.
Car se tu li fais boin governement et tu purges fleume, si sera saneis a l’aide de Deu.	For if you give him good treatment and purge the phlegm, he will be healed with God's help.
de la routure dou syfac	from the root of the eye socket
Quant routure vient en angres, et li bouelz dessendent as coions et c’est novelement, si covient que quant tu lou vues curer, qu’il ne menjuce mie celui jor;	When a hernia comes in the groin and the intestines descend into the scrotum, and it is new, then when you want to cure it, let him not eat that day;
et qu’il use choses qui laichent lou ventre, si que li fiens dessende de son ventre;	and let him use things that loosen the belly so that the feces descends from his belly;
aprés le fai seoir sus son dos entre tes mains, et li comande qu’il teigne son alaine tant que li boueil soient repairiet, et les ramoinne a tes dois, et seigne d’enche desoz la routure sus l’os dou poignil, et a tout un signe que soit semblans a la moitiet d’un cercle a desus dou cors;	after making him lie on his back between your hands, instruct him to tense his abdomen so that the bowels are drawn up, and bring them towards your fingers, and sign from under the navel over the bone of the wrist, and throughout a sign that is similar to half a circle above the body;
puis eschaufe le cautere de coi ci est li forme:	then heat the cautery with which there is the shape:
tant qu’il soit blans et qu’il giete senteles.	until it is white and dripping blood.
Puis ramoine les bouels a lor leu;	then bring the bowels back to their place;
et li ministres teigne sa main sus qu’il ne retornent arrier;	and the assistant holds his hand so that they do not return;
et oevre bien les cuisses au malaide, et met desoz lui I cussin et I serjant sus les cuisses, et I autre sus lou pis qui li teigne les mains;	and open the thighs for the patient, and put a pillow under his hips and a servant on each thigh pressing down, and another on the feet holding his hands down;
puis met le cautere sus lou signe a tout ta main, et lou tien droit et lou tien tant que tu ateignes l’os, et se tu ne l’ateins la premiere fois, si le rencomence encor une autre tant que tu viegnes jusc’a l’os;	then place the cautery on the sign all around your hand, and hold it straight and press until you reach the bone, and if you don't reach it the first time, do it again until you reach the bone;
et te warde subtilment que li boueil ne saille quant tu fais lou cautere;	and be careful that the blister does not burst when you apply the cautery;
que tu ne le brulasses;	that you do not burn yourself;
et que par ceu li malaides ne muere, ou autre malz.	and that the patient does not die, or suffer some other harm.
Et saiches que quant tu ne viens jusc’a l’os au cautere, tes ovraiges ne vaut rien.	And know that when you do not come to the bone with the cautery, your work is worth nothing.
Et covient que li cauteres des enfans soit subtilz selonc la mesure d’ous, et des grans gens aussi grans selonc lor mesure;	And one must make the cauteries for children small according to their ears, and for large people also large according to their size;
aprés III jors cure lou leu dou cautere de burre tant que li eschaudure soit ostee;	after 3 days, clean the site of the cautery with butter until the scald is healed;
aprés le cure d’autres oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez, et gise li malaides XL jors sus son dos tant que li plaie soit bien soudee;	afterwards, apply other ointments until it is healed, and have the patient lie on his back for 40 days until the wound is well-healed;
et covient que ses norrissemens soit lassatis longement, si que li boueil ne saillent quant il se preigdra d’aler en chambres.	and one must let the hair grow long enough that the blister does not burst when he is getting up and moving around.
Et aprés XL jors, quant il se voudra lever, se li amenistre une faixe bien faite, et la porse XL autres jors;	And after 40 days, when he wants to get up, let him be given a well-made brace, and wear it for another 40 days;
et ait boin repos, qu’il se travaille poc et se warde de trop grant repletion de boivre et de mengier, et de trop haut braire;	and has good rest, works little and guards against too much eating and drinking and too much sexual activity;
et quant il fait cest enseignement si est sanez entierement.	and when he follows this instruction, he will be completely healed.
Et je dirai ci aprés la cure de taillier en son chapistre.	And I will say hereafter about the treatment of cutting in his shoulder.
de la routure dou ventre	of stomach ulcers
Quant routures vienent en autres ventres et sont connisans, et tu vues qu’elles ne croissent plus, se li fai I cautere dou cautere reont selonc sa quantiteit, et soit ars li tiers dou keur;	When ulcers come in other bellies and are known, and you see that they are not growing anymore, then do the cautery with fire according to its quantity, and burn the third of the heart;
aprés le cure selonc ceu que nos avons dit;	after the cautery according to what we have said;
et aucun des anciens ont dit c’on le doit cauterizer au cautere a III angles selonc ceste forme:	and some of the ancients say that one should cauterize it with a three-pointed cautery according to this form:
mais signe premier le leu d’enche et fai une ligne per la largesce desus la routure, et une autre defuers, et main ta main emmi a tout le cautere clavile.	but first sign the site of entry and make a line along its width above the ulcer, and another across, and hold your hand still all over during the cautery.
Mais li premiers cauteres est plus legiers et muedres.	But the first cauteries are lighter and milder.
de dolor anciene en aucun membre	of old pain in any limb
Quant dolor vient en aucun membre, ou de cheoir ou de ferir, et cele dolor tient lonc tens, et li cure de medicine n’i vaut, adonc covient qu’il soit cauterizeis au cautere qui est apelez «poins», et soit li cauteres selonc la longesce dou membre et la petitece et sa foibleteit et sa vertut et sa location de torcions et de sa dolor.	When pain comes in a limb, either from falling or from injury, and that pain lasts a long time, and the treatment of medicine does not help, then it must be cauterized with the cautery called 'sharp', and the cautery should be according to the length of the limb, its smallness and weakness, and its torture and pain.
s’il est sanez dou premier cautere, c’est bien;	if he is healed by the first cautery, that is good;et s’il n’est pas sanez, tu le remets a son leu et tu le
se ceu nom, recomence I autre cautere sus celui, car teilz costume est qu’il se doit muer au membre que li est prochiens, por coi il covient que tu faices les cauteres tant que li malaides soit saneis.	and if he is not healed, you reset it to its place and you repeat the cautery on that one, for such is the custom that it should move to the member that is nearest to it, so you must do the cauteries until the patient is healed.et s’il est sanez dou premier cautere, c’est bien; et s’il n’est pas sanez, tu le remets a son leu et tu le recomences I autre cautere sus celui, car teilz costume est qu’il se doit muer
de meselerie	of mixing
Li meseil sont aidiet aucune fois par cautere par grant aide, et meismement li maladie que vient de la putrefaction de fleume et de melancolie.	Some diseases are aided by cautery with great benefit, especially those that arise from putrefied humours and melancholy.
Cant tu la vues cauterizer, pren warde se li maladie est au comencement, et s’ele est curee selonc ceu que nos avons dit en la division, et ne dessent ne ne demoure, et tu doutes que li corruption ne porpreigne tout le malaide, adonques li fai V cauteres sus lou chief:	When you see it cauterized, be careful if the disease is in its early stages, and if it is healed according to what we have said in the division, neither decreasing nor lingering, and you doubt that corruption will spread throughout the disease, then do V cauteries on the head:
I emmi le chief a nouf, et l’autre vers lou front a la fin des chevous;	and I emmi the head to the back of the neck, and the other towards the forehead at the end of the hairline;
et II sus les II cornes, et I derrierre sus le haiterel;	and two on either side of the head, and one behind the neck;De la quare conme il est necesser que li cauteres soit fait sus li chef, adonques covient qu’
et i laise tant ta main que li cauteres viegne jusc’a l’os, et tant que les escorces en issent fors si que les vapors des grosses humors s’en puissent issir;	and leave your hand so that the cautery reaches the bone and comes to the surface so that the vapors of the gross humors can escape;Si tu veies qu’il ne se peut tros bien, adonques covient que li fai a la fine II cauteres sus les lombris de lor ciefs, et li enveie tant que ele vienne sus li chief,
et le cauterize sus la mice selonc ce qu’il est devant.	and cauterize it on the mole according to its appearance.
Et se li meselerie est partout esparse;	And if the mange is spread everywhere;
et elle pert manifestement, si covient que tu lou cauterizes de ces cauteres que nos avons dit ou chief, et I cautere en som lou neis, et II cauteres sus l’espinee dou col, et VI cauteres sus l’espinee dou dos, et I grant sus la crupie et I autre delez, et II sus les II espaules;	and she is losing her hair, then you must cauterize her with the cauteries that we have described earlier: one cautery on the head, two cauteries on the spine of the neck, six cauteries on the spine of the back, one large cautery on the groin, and one smaller one, two cauteries on both shoulders;
et II sus les coutes, et II sus les tendrons dou pis, et I sus chascune jointe des mains et des piez, et sus les fosses des mains;	two cauteries on the inside of the elbows, two cauteries on the tendons of the feet, one cautery on each joint of the hands and feet, and on the knuckles of the hands;
et te warde des ners que sunt sus lou derrien calcant, que tu ne les bruler;	and be careful not to burn the nerves that are on the lower back;
et aucune fois fait om cautere sus l’os dou poignil, et I autre sus l’os de l’estomac, et I autre sus lou foie.	sometimes you will make a cautery on the bone of the elbow, one on the bone of the stomach, and one on the liver.
Et saiches que quant plus i fais de cautere, plus li fais d’aide, et mues li profite;	And know that when you make more cauterizations, you help him more, and move him to profit.
et saiches que li malaides ne sent point de dolor au cautere si com li sain le sentent, por ce que li cors est ja toz corrumpus.	and know that the patient feels no pain from the cautery as the healthy man does, because his body is already entirely corrupted.
Et covient ke li cautere soient grant et petit selonc les membres et les jointures, selonc ceu que vos lou troverez en manieres des fers.	And it is necessary that the cautery be large and small according to the members and joints, according to what you will find in the manner of the irons.
Aprés cure lou leu de farine de veces avec miel et autres cures tant qu’il soit saneis.	Afterwards, treat the site with a poultice of wheat flour with honey and other remedies until it is healed.
Quant enfleure vient en aucun membre et est curee par medicines et oiles et emplastres, et il n’est mie sanez, adonques li fai cauteres sus le membre selonc la grandour et la petitece dou membre;	When swelling comes to a limb and is cured by medicines and oils and poultices, but it is not healed, then he should make cauterizations on the limb according to the size and smallness of the limb;
et soit li cauteres un poc entrans en l’espés dou keur;	and let the cautery be a little into the depth of the heart;
puis le cure d’oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez.	then cure it with ointments until it is healed.
Et aucune fois fait on cautere et a la main et au piet et au dos, a l’issue dou nerf que muet le membre, et ensi si est ostee li enfleure;	And sometimes cauterizations are made on the hand and foot and back, at the exit of the nerve that paralyzes the limb, and thus is removed the swelling;
et toutevoie ne s’en entremette nuls s’il n’est conoissans des membres et des issues des ners movans lou cors.	and yet one should not intermeddle with this unless he understands the limbs and the exits of the nerves moving the body.
de albaras	of albaras
Quant li maladie qui est apelee «albaras» est enveillie, et li engien de medicine n’i valent rien, adonques le cauterize d’un cautere un poc parfont, selonc la quantiteit de l’espés dou keur, tant que li blenchour soit ostee, et soit muee sa color;	When the disease called "albaras" is woke up, and medicine's art is of no use, then cauterize it with a cautery tool slightly deeply, according to the amount of thickness of the skin, so that the whiteness is removed, and its color changes.
puis le cure de farine de veces et de lentilles avec oile roset et foilles de plantain, et sanc de colon et sanc d’alondre, de chescun une partie;	Then treat it with a poultice of wheat flour and lentils, with rose oil and plantain leaves, and blood from the gut and blood from the almond, each in equal parts.
et soit mellez tout ensamble, et soit liiez d’un drapel, et soit aers au leu tant qu’il soit sanez.	Mix it all together, then bind it with a cloth, and keep it in place until it is healed.
li cure de chancre par cautere	the treatment of sores by cautery
Quant chancre vient au comencement, et tu lou vues arrester, si le cauterize au cautere qui semble I cercle, tout entor au tour dou chancre.	When a chancre appears at its beginning, and you see it stopping, then cauterize it with a cautery that looks like a circle, all around the perimeter of the chancre.
Et toutevoie li saige dirent que on faice cautere ausi au mileu dou chancre;	And nonetheless, the wise say that one should also cauterize in the middle of the ulcer:
et toutevoie ceu ne me semble mie boin, car je redous que il ne soit ulcerez et corrumpus, et je l’ai ja veut avenir aucune fois;	And I do not think this is good, for I fear that it may be burned and damaged, and indeed, I have seen this happen.
et plus droituriere chose est qu’il soit cauteriés entor, au cautere qui est apelez «circule», si com nos avons dit en mout de cauteres.	and a better way is to cauterize around it with the cautery called "circle", as we have said in many cauteries.
de l’enfleure qui ne puet meurer	of the swelling that cannot subside
Quant aucuns ait une maladie qui est apelee «adubelati», et elle tarde de meurer ou por la superfluiteit qu’ele fait ou por l’eaige dou malaide quant il est decrepites (c’est a dire trop vielz) et il a poc de sanc, ou por lou tens;	When someone has a disease called "adubelati", and it delays death either due to the excess fluid it creates or because of the age of the patient when they are decrepit (that is, very old) and they have little blood, or because of time;
et tu la vues haster de meurer:	and you see them hastening to die:
adonques le cauterize entor de mout de petis cauteres en poignant;	then cauterize them around with many small cauteries by pricking;
aprés le laisse ensi.	afterwards, leave it as is.
Car elle se hastera de meureir.	Because it will hasten its death.
Et se tu la vues percier a tout le cautere, si chaufe le cautere de coi ci est li forme:	And if you see it piercing all around with the cautery, then heat the cautery from which the form comes:
Et met ta main en mileu de cele maladie qui est apellee «adubelati» tant que li cauteres ait perciet lou keur, et soit telz li cauteres que li malaides lou sente defuers en teil maniere que li cours de la porriture soit alegis.	And put your hand in the middle of the disease called  "adubelati" until the cauteries have pierced the skin, and let the cauteries be such that the patient feels them throughout his body in such a way that the flow of the pus is relieved.
Aprés le cure tant qu’il soit sanez parfaitement.	Afterwards, heal it perfectly.Si li saingne ne vult point curer ou si il demoure longuement en la meureir: adonques tu le remets a leu et covient que li fies 10 cauteres entor de l’esgoutte, et estraigne li keur par les eculz qui sont sus le piez, ou s’il ne veult point aler par les piés, adonques tu le traites a la maniere qu’adibele.
li cure dou feu par fer	the fire cautery by iron
Une autre maniere de maladie i a qui est apelee «corrodens», et n’est autre chose que une mengeson de membre, car ele menjut les membres ausi com li feus les leignes seches.	Another kind of disease is called "corroding", and it is nothing other than a melting of the member, for it melts the members as fire melts dry wood.
Se tu vois ceste maladie en leu qui puisse soffrir cautere ensamble feu, adonques eschaufe les cauteres clavile mout petit et grant, selonc ceu qu’il covient au leu ou li maladie est;	If you see this disease in a place that can withstand fire cautery, then heat the cauteries small and large according to what is appropriate for the location of the disease;
aprés le cauterize de toutes pars tant que tu erraiche toute la corruption, et nen remaigne rien de li, que tout ceu qui est corrumpus ne soit osteit.	afterwards, cauterize it all over until you reach all the corruption and none of it remains, so that all that is corrupted is removed.Se il a grant dolor sus li leu qui tu cauterise, adonques tu prendras un petit trefon que tu aschaufes en la flamme del fuo et li laves li oucis de leu ou il a dolor, si com il
Et puis le laisse III jors, et met sus les leus cauterizez soffre broiet avec oile tant que les eschaudures dou feu soient ostees, et toute li corruption.	And then leave it for 3 days, and apply soft poultices with oil upon the cauterized places until the burns from the fire are healed, and all the corruption is removed.Et si li cauteres feuz ne puissent osteit toute la corruption, adonques covient qu’il soit remede par eschaudures de leus.
Aprés lou cure d’oignemens engendrans char.	After the treatment of inflammations caused by humidity.
Et se tu vois aprés III jors que chars saine ne naisse, c’est boin;	And if you see after three days that no hair grows, that is good.
et se ceu non, si rencomence le cautere sus ceu qui est demoreit des leus corrumpus.	and if not, then restart the cautery on what is left of the corrupted hair.
Et ceste mengeson est aucune fois esteit curee de medicine ague en leu de cautere de feu;	And this baldness has sometimes been cured with medicine in place of fire cautery;
mais toutevoie cautere de feu est de plus grant aide, et j’ai ja dit la cure de la medicine ague en la division:	but nonetheless fire cautery is of greater aid, and I have already described the cure for medicine baldness in the division:
pren la quant tu en as mestier.	take as much as you need.
des porrelz qui vienent as piez	of warts that come on the feet
Mout de fois avient que as piez par defuers naist une maladie qui est apelee «clos» selonc nostre entencion, et est une grosse chose fautree qui blece lou piet.	Many times it happens that on different feet a disease called "clos" according to our understanding occurs, and is a large, hard lump that affects the foot.Et si li pies sont trots, et ne peut aller en son office, que il soit eslongeant de la foyt que il doit; et si li pies de la main sunt trots, qu’il ne peut faire aucun ofis de main: et est li pies de la main et le pied trots, selonc la nassance.
Et li cauteres de ceste maladie si est selonc II manieres.	And the cauteries for this disease are according to two methods.
C’est a savoir cautere de feu, et cautere d’aigue chaude.	That is, fire cautery and hot water cautery.
Cautere de feu si est que tu eschaufe I cautere cheveit ausi com est une penne de vouteul, et soit fait de boin fer a la mesure qu’il puisse porpenre le clou de toutes pars, et qu’il i ait subtilz marges;	Fire cautery is made so that you heat the cautery iron as hot as an oven, and it is made of good steel to the size that it can pierce the claw all around, and it has fine edges;
aprés le met tout chaut sus lou clou, et torne ta main tot entor le clou tant qu’il viegne au font dou clou;	afterwards place it directly on the claw, and rotate your hand all around the claw until it reaches the bottom of the claw;
et lou laisse ensi III jors tant qu’il encomence giter porriture;	and let him leave it for three days until it begins to ooze pus;
puis li fai un emplaustre de malves savaiges broiies avec seil, et laisse l’emplaustre sus toute la nuit, et li clous cherra et sera desracinez de ses racines.	then make a poultice of wild mallows crushed with salt, and leave the poultice on all night; the nail will come loose and be pulled out by the roots.
Puis cure le leu d’oignement enjanrant char tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then heal the wound with an ointment until it is cured.Cautere d’aigue chaude si est que tu prends de l’aigue boullante et la mets sus li clou tant qu’il fieent giter, et le remuers tot entor, et le remuers tot entor; puis li fai un emplaustre come celuy del cautere de feu.
Et s’il sont convertit par defuers lou cors, et maintes fois avient et en mains et em piez, si covient que tu i amenistres cautere d’aigue chaude;	And if they are turned around in the body, and often occur in hands and feet, then you must apply hot water cautery;
et est en teil maniere:	and it is done in this way:
pren une cainne d’arain ou de fer, ou une penne de vouteul, et met sus lou clou et l’althelul, c’est asavoir porrelz verrues;	take a brass or iron rod, or a pen of reed, and place it on the nail and the warts, that is to say, calluses;
et met la cainne sus si qu’ele porpreigne tout entor, puis i met un poc d’awe chaude, et retien bien ta main, et presse ta main en tornant si que li marge de la cainne viegne a la racine dou clou, et puisse trover l’aigue chaude voie parfonde jusc’a la racine;	and place the rod so that it wraps around the nail, then put a little hot water on it, and hold your hand steady, and press your hand as you turn the rod so that the edge of the rod comes to the root of the nail, and can find the hot water a deep path all the way to the root;
et soffre li malaides un poc la mordication de l’aigue chaude une houre;	and let the patient endure the biting of hot water for an hour;
puis le laisse ensi, et il se derracinera tous a tout ses racines.	then let it be, and it will all come out by its roots.
Ensi fai un aprés autre, tant que tu esraiches toz ces qui sont au cors, puis les cure des oignemens qui engenrent char.	Thus do one after another, until you have pulled out all those in the body, then heal them with ointments that generate flesh.
li cure dou trembler	the shaking treatment
Quant aucuns tremble de froidor de ners, ou de fievre quartaine ou d’autre, si covient que tu li faices IIII cauteres ou IV sus l’espinee dou dos, I cautere entre chescune espinee;	When someone trembles from coldness in their nerves, or from a fever, or something else, you should make 4 cauteries on the spine of the back, one cautery between each vertebrae:
et I cautere ou pez, et I sus l’estomac au cautere olivaire;	and one cautery on the penis, and one cautery on the stomach with an olive-oil cautery;
si laissera lou trembler, et se hastera li santez de la maladie froide.	it will stop the trembling, and hasten the healing from the cold sickness.Si aurent les ches et les costez et les cuissiez fies, si covient que li fuiles la fi
des pustules puans	of stinking pustules
Aucune fois apperent par defuers le cors bathes, ou pustules puans, que vienent de grosses matieres corrumpues.	There appear sometimes through the body sores or stinking pustules, which come from corrupt humours.
si covient au premier quant eles apperent que on faice cautere sus chescun chief de la pustule:	If they have sores and blisters on their shoulders, ribs, or thighs, then one must, when they first appear, make cauteries at the top of each blister:et li cauteres si fient ains qu’eles se brisent; et après que ele sont
un cautere subtil de fust de mirte, de coi li pointe soit emprise au feu, ou de racine de aristologe longe, ou au cautere lenticulaire.	and the cauteries should be done until they burst; and after they have been burst, a fine cautery with a sprig of myrtle, or with the long root of aristolochia, or with a lens-shaped cautery.Si aurent les ches et les costez et les cuissiez fies, si covient que li fuiles la fi
Et aucune fois les cauterize on au comencement quant il aperent, selonc ceste maniere, et il ne puent croistre des enqui en avant, mais est desrompue li superfluitez dont il vienent, et sont sanez;	And sometimes they are cauterized at the beginning when they appear, according to this manner, and they cannot grow from thereforth, but the excess from which they come is disrupted, and they are healed.
mais il covient que ceu soit fait aprés l’evacuation de sanc.	but it must be done after the evacuation of blood.
quant li artere est copee	when the artery is cut
Maintes fois avient grans decorremens de sanc de l’artere qui est copee a la plaie que vient au pardefuers, ou a l’incision de l’aposteme, ou au cautere dou membre, et as semblans choses;	Many times there are great bleeding from the artery that is cut at the wound that comes to the surface, or in the incision of an abscess, or in the cautery of a limb, and in similar things;
et est mout grief chose d’estenchier.	and it is very difficult to stop the bleeding.
Et toutevoie quant ceu avient a aucun, si te haste de mettre ton doi indice sus la plaie de la voinne, et l’estrain mout tant que li sans soit apaisiez desoz ton doi, et que goute n’en isse plus;	And yet, when this happens to someone, you must quickly place your finger over the wound of the vein and hold it very firmly until the bleeding stops underneath your finger, and no more blood comes out;
puis met au feu les cauteres olivaire plusors petis et grans tant qu’il soient tuit rouge;	then heat up several small and large olive-sized cauteries until they are all red hot;
puis empren I, ou grant ou petit selonc la plaie et lou leu en coi li artere est route, et met le cautere sus cele voine ou tu tiens ton doi, et tien le cautere tant sus que li sans soit restainchiez.	then take a large or small cautery according to the wound and the location where the artery is running, and place the cautery on that vein where you hold your finger, and hold the cautery there until the blood is staunched.
Et s’il saut fuers quant tu lieves ton doi desus la voinne, et li cauteres estint, si pren hastivement .i. autre des cauteres qui sont au feu.	And if the bleeding starts again when you lift your finger from the wound and the cautery goes out, then quickly take another of the cauteries that are in the fire.
Et ne cesser de faire ceu l’un aprés l’autre tant que li sans soit estenchiez;	And do not cease doing this one after the other until the blood is staunched;
et warde que tu n’ardes lou nerf qui est delez, et que autre malice ne viegne sus lou malaide;	and be careful not to burn the nerve that is nearby, and that no other harm comes to the patient;
et saiches que quant sans decourt de l’artere, c’on ne lou puet mie bien restenchier meismement quant li artere est grans, se ceu n’est par une des IIII manieres que nos avons dit:	and know that when blood escapes from an artery, it cannot be staunched easily itself when the artery is large, unless by one of the four methods we have described;
ou par cautere, ou par extraction quant ele n’est mie traite, ou par fort liement de fil, ou par medicines mises sus qui ont pooir de restenchier sanc;	either by cautery, or by extraction when it is not treated, or by a tight bandage, or by medicine placed on it that has the power to staunch blood;
et soit liee et estrainte avennament.	and it should be bound and restrained skillfully.
Qui i amenistrera restenchement de liier estroitement de drapelz ou de metre choses ardans sus, ou autres semblans choses, se n’i profite se poc non.	He who administers a tight bandage or places hot objects on top, or similar things, will not benefit much if at all.
Et se ce avient a aucun et il n’ait mie mire ne medicine present, si doit mettre son doi indice sus la plaie de la voinne si com nos avons dit, et bien estrendre tant qu’il soit restenchiez desus la plaie et desus la voinne;	And if this happens to anyone and there is no mirror or medicine available, one should place their index finger on the wound as we have said, and apply pressure until it feels tight on the wound and on the vein.
et ne remuer lou doit, mais lou moille d’awe froide sovent que soit mout froide tant que li sans soit congelez et engrossiez et restenchiez;	and do not move the finger but wet it with cold water often as long as it is very cold until the blood is congealed and swollen and tight.
et faice des enqui en avant ceu dont il a mestier de cauteres et de medicines.	and make inquiries beforehand about what he needs in terms of cauterizations and medications.
Ci encomence li secons livre des cures de taille	Here begins the second book of wound treatments
Nos vos avons dit ou premier chapistre toute maladie en coi il covient cautere de feu, ou de medicine ardans, et les oquisons et les causes et les estrumens et les formes des cauteres;	We have told you in the first chapter about all illnesses that require fire cauterization, or burning medications, and their actions, causes, instruments, forms of cauterizations;
et ai mis celui chapistre des lou chief jusc’a piez, et je irai en cest chapistre par celi meisme voie por ceu c’on trueve plus legierement ceu c’on voura.	and have placed this chapter from the head to the feet, and I will go through this same path in this chapter because one can more easily find what they are looking for.
Et ainsois que je encomence ceu, il covient, chier fil, que vos aprenez que en cest chapistre a plus de peril et de paor que ou premier des cauteres, et por ceu il covient plus grant cautele.	And so that I may begin this, it is necessary, dear son, for you to learn that in this chapter there is more danger and fear than in the first of the cauteries, and because of that greater caution is required.
Car en l’ovraige de cest chapistre avient maintes fois evacuation de sanc a l’ovrir la voinne, et a l’incision sus aposteme, et as cures des plaies, et a l’estraction des saiettes, et a l’incision sus la piere, et les semblans choses;	For in the work of this chapter, there is often an evacuation of blood when opening a vein, and making an incision over an abscess, and in treating wounds, and in extracting arrows, and cutting into stones, and similar things.
ou il a doutance et paor, et en vient li mors a plusors.	Where there is doubt and fear, many die.
Et je vos amoneste que vos n’entreprenez folie.	And I admonish you that you do not attempt foolishness.
Car mout de manieres de gens vienent en cures.	For in many ways people come to cures.
si vienent de telz qui s’aïrent si avec lor maladie qu’il muerent legierement por la forsenerie qu’il trueve de sa maladie, et de la grandour de son malice;	they come from such people who, because of their disease, change quickly and die because of the great severity of their illness.Quant li chiés de l’ajutoire est desaloiez par cause de moistor, et on le remet a leu, et il n’i puet demorer ains revient adés et desalue par petit movement qui avient, si com nos avons esproveit, adonques covient il que tu ramoignes la dislocation premierement.
et de ces doit on avoir paor.	and one should fear these.Dislocations est issue d’aucune jointe de son leu, por
Et de ces i a qui te done son sens, et dit:	And from these there are those who give their sense and say:"Quant li chiés de l’ajutoire est desaloiez par cause de moistor
«atendez, je sui garis»;	Wait, I am ready.
et li maladie est despitouse.	and the patient is desperate.
Il ne covient mie que vos vos consentez a ces qui vienent a vos qui ont ceste maniere, mais mettez plus grant cusanson en vostre honor qu’en vostre covoitise, et n’ovrez mie folement mais saigement de ceu dont vos estes certain, et dont vos poez avoir pris et los;	You should not consent to those who come to you with this condition, but place more importance on your honor than your desire. Do not open it recklessly, but wisely and carefully, from what you are certain of and what you can cure and gain reward from.
et usez de pronostication et de indication en cures de vos malaides a coi salus soit convertie;	Use prognosticating and indication in curing your patients so that salvation may be achieved.
et ceu vos aidera a aquester bone renommee, et gloire, et memoire de loenge.	And that will help you gain a good reputation, glory, and praise.
Tres chier fil, Nostres Sires vos doint boin entendement et droiture, et se vos vuelle espireir de la sainte inspiration de sa main, amen.	Very dear son, Our Lord gives you good understanding and uprightness, and if you wish to aspire to the holy inspiration of his hand, amen.
Or je vos ai ordeneit cest chapistre en devisant par chapistres, selonc ceu qu’il est devant ou chapistre des cauteres, que je vos ai deviseit des le chief jusc’a piez, por ceu que vos trovez plus legierement ceu dont vos avrez mestier.	Now I have assigned this chapter to you in discussing the topic of cautery, according to what has been presented before in the chapter on cautery from head to foot, so that you can find more easily whatever you need.
dou chief plein d’aigue	the head full of water
Saiches que ceste maladie vient mout de fois as enfans a l’enfanter, et quant li baille estraint trop fort le chief de l’enfant;	Know that this disease often comes to children during childbirth, and when the head of the child is squeezed too tightly.
et aucune fois vient ceu de cause reponue que on ne seit.	And sometimes it comes from an unknown cause.
Et je ne vis onques ceste maladie fuers qu’en enfans, et a toz ces que j’ai veus se hastait li mors;	I have never seen this disease in adults, and in all the cases I have observed, death has always resulted.
et por ceu me semble qu’il me vaut mues lassier l’ovraige en teilz cures.	and for this reason, it seems to me that I should leave the work in several parts.
Et je vis I enfant de coi li chiés estoit plains d’aigue, et li chief engroissoit chescun jor tant qu’il ne lou pooit sostenir;	I saw a child whose neck was filled with fluid, and his head swelled every day so much that he could not support it;
et crut tant li moistor qu’il fut mors, et ceste moistor si est assemblee desoz l’os sus lou syphac, entre lou keur et l’os;	and it filled with fluid to the point of death, and this fluid collected under the bone above the throat, between the heart and the bone;
et li ovraiges si est telz se li moistor est entre lou keur et l’os, et li apostemes est petis, que tu fendes emmi lou chief une fendure large;	and the procedure is such that if the fluid is between the heart and the bone, and the abscess is small, you should make a large incision in the neck;
et soit ausi longe com II nous, tant que li mostor corre;	and it should be as long as two fingers, so that the fluid runs out;
et vez ci la forme dou spatumile:	and here is the form of the spleen:
Se li moistor est plus creue, et li aposteme soit plus grans, si fai .ij. fendures en maniere d’une croix, selonc ceste forme:	If the hollow is deeper, and the abscess is larger, then make two slits in the shape of a cross, according to this form:
Et se li moistor est desoz l’os, et li signes que tu vois les commissures dou chief overtes de chescune partie, et li aigue saut fuer quant tu la presses de ta main au dedens, et ceu ne t’est mie reponut:	And if the fluid is under the bone, and you see the edges of the wound gaping open in every part, and the fluid spurts out when you press it with your hand from within, and it does not close up for you:
si covient que tu fendes enmi lou chief III fendures selonc ceste maniere:	then you must cut three slits on the head according to this manner:
Et aprés l’incision estrai la moistor toute fuers.	And after the incision, draw out all moisture forcefully.
Aprés estraint les fendures de drapelz et de poudres, et i met vin et oile, et laisse ensi jusc’a cinquieme jor;	After that, press the slits with pieces of cloth and powders, and apply wine and oil, and leave it thus for five days.
puis le deslie, et cure la plaie par tentes et par oignemens, et laisse estraindre le chief egaument, et done mengier au malaide viande seche de poc de moistor tant que li membre soit confortez et sanez.	Then remove it, and treat the wound with poultices and ointments, and let the head hang freely, and give the patient dry food without moisture until the member is comforted and healed.
Et une autre maniere d’incision est que tu regardes ou apert li grandor de l’aposteme, et li assemblé de l’aigue;	And another way of incision is that you observe where the abscess opens, and the gathering of pus;
car aucune fois est elle devant;	for sometimes it is in front;
aucune fois derrier;	sometimes behind;
aucune fois en destre;	sometimes on the right;
et aucune fois en senestre.	and sometimes on the left.
Taille donques lai ou li aposteme apert, et l’emplissement de l’aigue, et lou fent selonc ce que tu en as le pooir;	Therefore cut where the abscess opens and drains pus, and make an incision according to what you are able to do.
et warde que tu ne coper l’artere;	and guard against covering the artery;
et veigne flun de sanc, si que li malaides muere dou decorrement de sanc et de l’evacuation de moistor.	and blood will flow, causing the patient to die from blood loss and the evacuation of moisture.
de reume	from gout
Quant il avient a aucun une maladie qui est apelee «catarre» as eulz ou au pis, et li maladie est anciainne, et li cure de medicine ne profite mie, adonques li derraine cure si est li cauteres avec ceu c’on li copera les .ij. arteres.	When it happens to someone that they have a disease called "cataract" in the eyes or the feet, and the disease is old, and the medicine does not help, then the last resort is cautery with which one will cut the two arteries.
Il covient donques, cant tu les vues coper, que li malaides faice rere son chief;	Therefore, when you see them covered, have the patient lean back;
aprés li frotte lou leu d’un drapel aspre tant que les arteres aperent, puis estraingne li malaides son col a tout I drapel;	then rub the area with a rough cloth until the arteries appear, then squeeze the patient's neck tightly with the cloth;
puis regarde ou li voine bait, et li leus de l’une et de l’autre sont aprés les oreilles, et poc sont reponues;	then look where the vein bites, and the veins on either side are behind the ears, and they are very close together;
puis signe les leus d’enche, puis cope l’une et l’autre d’un spatumile agut de II pars, tant que li taille veigne jusc’a l’os, et ceu soit par lou large dou chief.	then sign the veins inside, then cover one and press the other with a sharp spatula for two parts, so that the neck vein comes to the bone, and it should be done from the side of the head.
Et se tu vues, boute le spatumile desoz l’artere et la cope au desus, en taillant ausi com .ij. dois au traver.	And if you see, insert the spatulum under the artery and cut it from above, cutting also .ij. fingers across.
Et quant li voinne est copee, si saut li sans en haut continuelment fuers.	And when the vein is cut, the blood will flow out continuously upward.
Et se li artere n’apert au sentir, si covient que tu mesures la quantiteit de l’espaice de III dois, puis seigne d’enche et fent jusc’a l’os;	And if the artery does not open on feeling, then you must measure the quantity of space of three beans, then sign inside and cut to the bone;
et ceu qu’il covient dou sanc mettre fuers si est VI c/, et par aventure un poc plus ou moins, selonc ce que li malaides puet soffrir, et la repletion de l’artere;	and the amount of blood to be let out should be VI ounces, and perhaps a little more or less, depending on what the patient can endure and the fullness of the artery.
puis regarde la plaie:	then examine the wound:
s’il remaint sus l’os point dou syphac, si le cope que apostemes chaus n’i veigne, puis estrain la plaie et lie, et la cure d’oignement tant qu’ele soit sanee.	if there is a lump on the bone, and pus does not come out, then open the wound and drain it, and treat it with ointment until it heals.
de emigrainne	from the emetic
Quant emigrainne anciaine vient, et catarre agut, por les moistors des larmes et les chalors en temples et sode anciene forsenee et semblans choses, et il est medicinez par manieres de cures de medicine et tout ceu ne li profite mie, si estraions les arteres des temples et lou cauterizons, si com nos avons conteit.	When old-age anemia comes, and catarrh is acute, due to moistors of the eyes and heat in the temples and ancient soddeness and similar things, and he has been treated by various methods of medicine and all of it does not help him, then we should open the arteries of the temples and cauterize them, as we have described.
Et li maniere de l’estraction d’elles si est que li malaides faice rere les poilz de ses temples, et entende a l’artere qui apert en la temple, car elle apert bien par son batement, et est poc reponue fuers que en aucuns homes qui sont trop froit;	And the method of extraction is that the patient should stand behind the hair on his temples, and feel for the artery which opens in the temple, as it can be felt clearly through its pulsation, and is not very deep beneath the skin in some people who are too thin.
et s’elle est reponue, si estraigne son col li malaides d’aucuns drapelz, puis frote le leu d’aucun aspre drap, et arose le leu d’aigue chaude tant que li artere apere manifestement;	And if it is deep, the patient should press his neck with some fabric, then rub the area with something rough, and wash the area with warm water until the artery appears clearly.
puis pren le spatumile de coi ci est li forme:	then take the spatula from which its shape comes:
puis escorche le cuir legierement tant que tu veignes a l’artere, puis la trai en haut as pinceures, et la depart bien des toiles que sont desoz li de chescune partie;	then scrape the skin lightly until you reach the artery, then pull it upward with tweezers, and carefully separate it from the tissues underneath in each part;
et se li artere est subtilz, si la torne a la pointe de l’uncine, puis la cope de celle partie selonc la quantiteit des II chiés.	and if the artery is thin, then cut off that part according to the amount of the two fingers.
Car s’elle n’est copee, si ne saut mie li sans dou tout en tout.	For if it is not cupped, the blood will not flow everywhere throughout the body.
Et trai dou sanc des VI c/, jusc’a III;	And draw out the blood from six parts, just up to three;
et se li artere est grans, si covient que tu la lies en II leus d’un fil double fort de soie, que porriture n’i veigne devant le soudement de la plaie, et veigne decorremens de sanc;	and if the artery is large, then you must tie it in two places with a strong double silk thread so that pus does not enter before the wound heals, and the blood comes out freely;
puis cope la superfluiteit qui est entre les II liiens en celle houre meisme, et puis, se tu vues, si lou cauterize dou cautere cutellaire jusc’a l’os tant que li chiés soient copez;	then cut off the excess between the two ties in that same hour, and then, if you wish, cauterize it with a hot iron all the way to the bone until the shoulder is cut through;
et c’est li muedre oevre, se li malaides n’a fievre et il est de chaude complexion.	and it is the mother's work, if the patient does not have a fever and is of a hot complexion.
Car li cauteres est aide por finir les moistors:	For the cautery is used to dry up moisture:
por ceu est il de plus grant aide as moistors.	therefore it is of greater help for moistures.
