Ou il covient por l’estraction des arteres que om emplisse lou leu de viel coton et mette on sus tentes bien faites;	Or, for the extraction of veins, one should fill the hole with old cotton and place a well-made tent on top;
et quant on les desliera, si soit curez de medicines seches que font naistre char, et de tentes, tant qu’il soit sanez;	and when they are removed, they should be treated with dry medicines that cause scabs to form, and with tents, until they are healed;
et se sans cort de l’artere tant dis com tu i oevres, si te haste dou coper par cautere, ou tu emple lou leu de vitriole et l’estrain a ta main que li sans soit estainchiez;	and if, without cutting the artery as far as you operate, you hasten to cover it with cautery, then employ the site of vitriol and squeeze it in your hand so that the blood is stanched;
et se tu n’as ceu present, si met sor le leu ton doit tant que li sans soit congelez, et arose le leu d’aigue froide tant que li sans cesse, et soit estraint si com il covient;	and if you do not have vitriol available, then place your finger on the site so that the blood congeals, and apply cold water to the site until the bleeding stops, and then squeeze it as necessary;
et ceu qui est muedre et plus legier en l’estraction de l’artere est que tu cauterizes la voinne de cest cautere trenchant de II pars, mais li trenchant soient bien espés por warder plus longement lor chalor.	and that which is more mature and easier to extract from the artery is that you cauterize the vein with this cutting cautery in two parts, but the cutting should be well-spaced so as to guard against their heat for a longer time.
Car quant li estrumens est trop tenves, si tient moins sa chalor.	Because when the instrument is too thin, it holds less heat.
Et doit avoir entre les II coutelz I doit de gros d’espaice, et puis quant tu as signiet d’enche les II leus, et tu mes lou fer ardant sus tant qu’il viegne jusc’a l’os, et cope la voinne en II leus;	And it must have between the two knives a thickness of a finger's width, and then when you have cut into both sides, you should place the hot iron on it until it reaches to the bone, and close the vein in two places.
et soient esloigniet entre les II chiés car il n’est mie soudez de cest cautere dou tout en tout;	and they must be spaced apart between the two joints because it is not fused together by this cautery in its entirety.
et c’est li forme dou cautere:	And here is the shape of the cautery:
des larmes	tears
Quant les larmes des eulz sont dessendans des voinnes que sont sus lou test dou chief de fuer, et il ne profite mie cure de medicine c’on i faice, et tu vois la faice dou malaide enrougir, et sent ou front ambulation si com de fremis;	When tears from the eyes are flowing from veins that are above the forehead, and it does not respond to any medicine that is applied, and you see the face of the ill person turning red, and feeling a pulsation as if from trembling;
et sui oil sont tenve et moiste si que li poil des papieres sont cheut, et sont eschaufees les papieres, et escorchies de l’ardor des larmes, si ait mestier de ceste cure.	and if they are dark and moist so that the hairs of the eyelids have fallen out, and the eyelids are swollen and scorched from the heat of the tears, then this treatment is necessary.
Et l’apelerent li ancien «cure contuse», et est que tu faices a rere au malaide qui a ceste maladie les poilz qu’il ait ou front, puis li fai III fendures ou front igalment selonc la longesce dou front;	And the ancients called it "cured by contusion", and it is that you do to the patient who has this disease, letting the hairs grow on his forehead, then make three incisions on his forehead evenly according to the length of his forehead;
et soit l’une des fendures ausi com II doi tout emmi lou front en avalant aval jusc’a neif, et les autres II as II costelz par desus les papieres, et te garde de l’incision des arteres que sont as II costez par desus les papieres;	and one of the incisions should be about two inches down from the forehead in the middle, and the other two at the sides above the eyelids; and beware of cutting into the arteries that are at the sides above the eyelids;
et aloigne ta main de la continuation des II mandibules, et soit chescune plaie la quantiteit de III dois au traver joins;	and keep your hand away from the continuations of the two mandibles, and let each wound be about a third of an inch deep across the joints;
et aies apparillie une piece d’esponge et mout de drapelz ses por essuer lou sanc, puis boute le spatumile agut de II pars de coi ci est li forme:	and have at hand a piece of sponge and plenty of bandages to wipe away the blood, then insert the spatulum, cut into two pieces, with which you will make the incision:
des l’incision qui est dever la temple jusc’a la seconde incision;	from the incision by the temple all the way to the second incision;
et escorche tout le keur qui est entre les II fendures a tot lou syfac qui est sus l’os, puis fai autreteil des la moiene incision jusc’a l’autre seconde, et puis estrai fuer cest spatumile.	and cut all around the skull between the two slits down to the bone, then cut from the middle slit to the other second one, and then remove this spatula.
si boute en la premiere fendure l’estrument qui est apelez «cultellaire», et est tresbien trenchans d’une part, et d’autre part est souef, ne mie trenchans, et c’est li forme:	if you put into the first cut the instrument that is called "culter", and is very sharp on one side and not sharp on the other, and this is its form:
Et met le costeit taillant vers la char aerse au keur, et lou costeit souef vers l’os, et lou boute tant qu’il veigne a la moiene fendure.	And place the knife cutting towards the chest bone in the heart, and the other knife towards the bone, and cut it so that it comes to the middle split.
Et cope toz les vasselz que dessendent dou chief as eulz tant que l’incision soit continue jusc’a ceu qui apert dou keur, et puis autreteil fai en la moiene fendure jusc’a l’autre defuer;	And cut all the vessels that descend from the head to the eyes until the incision is continuous down to that which opens up the skull, and then likewise make an incision in the middle slit up to the other one;
et puis estrai dou sanc igalment, et espresse lou leu por le sanc pris;	and then draw out the blood equally, and express the area for the blood that has been taken;
puis met en chescune fendure une tente de viel coton, et met sus drapelz moilliez en vin et en oile et en aisil, et garde que apostemes chaus n’i veigne;	then place in each slit a tent of old cotton, and place on top wet bandages soaked in wine and oil and garlic, and be sure that no abscesses form there;
et au tier jor deslie lou liien, et i amenistre grant planteit d’aigue tede, puis lou cure d’oignement basilicon avec oile roset, et d’autres cures dont on cure plaies, tant qu’il soit sanez.	and on the third day loosen the bandage, and administer a plentiful poultice of warm water, then treat with basilicon ointment and rosemary oil, and other remedies for wounds, until it is healed.
dou reume des eulz	from the eyes
Quant a aucun vienent catarre agut acostumeement, et tu vois les eulz tenves et petis, et afoiblir la veue, et les papieres brulees;	When someone experiences acute cataracts and you see their eyes become dim and small, and their vision weakens, and the eyelids burned:
et li poil chieent, et ou chief en parfont a dolor ague, et li malaides esternue;	and the hair falls out, and in the forehead there is great pain, and the patient sneezes;
adonques saiches par ces accidens que celles matieres et cil catharre ne vient fuer que de maintes voines, et li muedre cure que i est, si est ceste.	therefore you may know from these accidents that these matters and this cataract come from many veins, and the mother fluid that is in it, is thus cured.
Et est que tu comande au malaide a rere son front, puis fai une grant fendure emmi lou front, et une autre dou large I poc.	And you should command the patient to raise his forehead, then make a large cut in the middle of the forehead, and another wide one nearby.
Et comence des la fendure de la temple senestre a la temple destre, et soit li incision jusc’a l’os;	And begin from the left temple to the right temple, and make the incision up to the bone;
et esloigne ta main des ners des temples que muevent au mengier;	and keep your hand away from the nerves in the temples that move the eye;
et quant li os est descovers, si essue tout le sanc a une esponge, et puis desevre entre les II levres de la fendure et i met coton viel, et tentes de lin;	and when the bone is exposed, [the surgeon] should suck out all the blood with a sponge and then stuff between the two lips of the wound with old cotton and linen bandages.
puis lie desus drapelz moilliez en vin et en oile, et te garde d’aposteme chaut;	then [the surgeon] should lay moistened cloths in wine and oil on top, and beware of hot abscesses;
quant il est ostez, si covient que tu frottes l’os tant que chars i comence a naistre, puis le cure de choses exiccatives, que font enjanrer char.	when it is removed, you should rub the bone until pus begins to form, then clean the wound with dry substances that cause pus to form.
En teil maniere:	In this manner:
pren II parties de flor de froment, et de colofoine IIII parties, et en fai emplaustre;	take 2 parts of flower of wheat and 4 parts of colophony, and make an ointment;
et l’aministre en ces plaies por enjanrer char per tout.	and administer it in these wounds to cause pus to form throughout.
de l’estoupement des oreilles	of the cleaning of the ears
Tout ceu que chiet ens oreilles est une des IIII choses:	All that falls from the ears is one of four things:
ou grains, ou beste, ou piere de mine ou semblans chose si com fer;	or grains, or a stone from a mine, or something similar like iron;si est grain, le leve et le met en aigue vieille que n’ait poil, si covient que tu
ou semence, si com jaisses, feves, pois;	or seeds, such as beans, peas;
ou chose defluans si com aigue et aisilz et semblans choses.	or flowing substances such as water, oil, and similar things.
Quant il chiet en l’oreille piere ou autre maniere de chose que ne s’ajoste mie a l’oreille, ne ne croist en l’oreille, si met l’oreille au solel.	When it shrinks in the ear, or something else that doesn't adhere to or grow in the ear, put the ear towards the sun.
Se tu vois la piere, si distille aucun poc d’oile violet ou oile de sisament, puis i amenistre extraction;	If you see a stone, then drip some violet oil or oil of castorem, then administer an extract;
et lou fai esternuer de condisi, et li estoupe les narines quant li esternuemens vient, et met entor l’oreille pieces de drapelz ou laine;	and make him sneeze with a solution, and plug his nose when sneezing comes, and put around the ear pieces of cloth or wool;
et estent l’oreille au desus.	and prop up the ear at the top.
Mout de fois vient fuer par ceste cure;	Many times it comes out through this treatment;
et s’elle ne vient fuer, se li amenistre extraction as pinceures subtilz, de coi ci est li forme:	and if it does not come out, then administer an extract with sharp tweezers, of which this is the form:
S’elle saut fuer as pinceures, c’est boin;	If it pops out with the tweezers, that is good;
se ceu non, si amenistre extraction a l’oncine subtil de petite doubleure;	if not, then administer an extract at the thin end of a small needle;
et s’elle ne saut par ceu, si fai une caine d’arain et boute lou chief de la cainne ou pertuis de l’oreille fort, et estoupe ceu qui est entor la cainne de cire mole si que li vens n’i puisse entrer avec la cainne;	and if it does not come out with that, then make a brass rod and insert the head of the rod into the ear canal firmly, and plug around the rod with soft wax so that air cannot enter with the rod;
puis le trai fuer forment, car mout de fois vient fuer si com nos avons dit;	then treat it again later, because often it comes out again as we have said.
et s’elle ne vient fuer en teil maniere, si prent glut de coi en prent les oisiaus, et met en som aucun estrument qui soit a point por ceu faire, et met un poc de coton entor;	and if it does not come out in this way, then grab some grit with your fingers, and put some instrument that is suitable for doing this, and put a little cotton around it;
puis presse le glut sus la piere ou quel chose que ce soit, et trai fuer.	then press the grit onto the stone or whatever it is, and push it out.
Et s’elle ne saut fuer de toutes ces choses que nos avons dit, si te haste de fendre l’oreille ainsois que aposteme chalz i veigne, et spasme;	And if it does not pop out with all the things we have said, then you should quickly split the ear so that pus and blood come out, and a spasm.
et li maniere de la fendure si est que tu faices premier sainier lou malaide de la cephalique, et estrai dou sanc selonc la mesure de sa vertu, puis fai seoir lou malaide entre tes mains et li torne l’oreille au desus, et fent une petite fendure en la racine de l’oreille a la graisse ou leu dependant;	And the way to split it is that you first make the patient bleed from the head, and draw out blood according to his strength, then make the patient sit between your hands and turn his ear up, and make a small slit at the root of the ear where the grease depends;
et soit li fendure ausi com une lune, tant que tu viegnes a la piere, puis l’oste selonc ton pooir, et la suce hastanment a ta bouche;	and make the incision as deep as a moon, so that you reach the stone, then squeeze it hard with your finger and suck vigorously with your mouth;
et la cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	and treat it until it is healed.
Et se c’est grains qui est ens et il enfle, si aministre extraction;	And if there are grains within that are swollen, then administer extraction;
et si’il ne puet issir, si amenistre I spatumile tenve subtil selonc ceste forme:	and if it cannot come out, then administer the spatumile tenve subtly according to this form:
et amenistre incision de celui grain.	and bring about incision of that grain.
Mais ne faire mie ceu quant tu penses que li grains est moistes por la moistor de l’oreille, tant que tu en aies fait maintes pieces;	But do not do this if you think the grains are moist from the moisture of the ear, until you have made many pieces;
puis l’estrai as pinceures subtilz et au succier, si com nos avons dit, si que li estractions soit aligie.	then extract it with delicate tweezers and suction, as we have said, so that the extraction is gentle.
En l’aigue donques que chiet en l’oreille covient que li malaides use d’esternuement de condisi premiers, et ample l’oreille de viel coton.	Therefore in the water that runs into the ear, the patient should use scent to cause sneezing first, and fill the ear with soft cotton.Quant il distend l’oreille si que li muque se distende, met a l’entree de l’oreille, es deux costez del garnement, quelque oile violete et suc, si com nos avons dit; et s’il ne peut venir fuer par ceste manier, si covient le faire estracter as pinceures subtilz.
Et soit gisans sus celle oreille meisme ou li aigue est.	And let him lie on the affected ear itself.
s’elle saut fuer per ceu, c’est boin.	If it jumps out by itself, that is good.
se ceu non, si prent maintes pieres selonc li longesce de ton doit tenves et legieres, et les eschaufe un poc au feu;	If not, then take many stones according to the length of your fingers, thin and light, and heat them slightly in the fire;
et em mette li malaides une ou pertus de son oreille, et saille sus i. de ses piez d’autre part, et fiere d’une autre piere sus la piere qui est en l’oreille;	and cut a hole in the patient's ear, and pierce through from the other side of his foot, and pierce another stone onto the stone that is in the ear;
et ne cesse de faire ceu de piere em piere tant que li aigue isse toute fuer, et ensi saut elle toute fuer;	and do not cease to push this stone through the other until all the water comes out, and so it will flow out entirely;
et se tu vues, si prent I jonc, et boute l’un des chiés en l’oreille, et l’autre chief emprent de feu tant que li plus dou jonc soit ars;	and if you see that it is taking hold, push one end of the reed into the ear and heat the other end in fire until the most painful reed is burned;
puis refai autreteil d’autres jons tant que li aigue isse toute, si com nos avons dit en la piere.	then do this with other reeds until all the water comes out, as we have said about the stone.
En l’estraction de la beste, s’elle est de petit cors, si com puce et semblans chose, cure la si com nos avons dit en la division;	In extracting a foreign object from an animal, if it is small in size like a tick or similar, remove it as we have described in the section on division;
mais s’elle est de grant cors c’on la puisse sentir, si amenistre extraction de pinceures;	but if it is large enough to be felt, use forceps for extraction;
et c’est li chose plus legiere a oster qui soit en l’oreille.	and it is the lightest thing to remove from the ear.
En l’estraction des vers enjanrez as oreilles, quant tu lou cures si com nos avons dit en la division et ou traitier des distillations, et li cure ne profite mie, si covient que tu regardes l’oreille au soleil:	In the extraction of worms from the ears, when you treat them as we have said in the section on distillations, and the treatment is not helping, then you must examine the ear in the sunlight:
s’il i apert nulz vers, si les trai as pinceures subtilz, et s’il n’aperent, si prent la cainne de coi ci est li forme:	if you see no worms, then treat it with subtle pincers, and if they don't appear, then take the skin of a hen's egg.
Et soit estroite desoz et large desus.	And it is tight below and loose above.
Et boute lou plus subtil chief en l’oreille selonc la quantiteit de la soffrance dou malaide, puis succe forment a tot la caine;	Then insert the most slender end into the ear according to the amount of suffering of the patient, then suck gently on the egg;
fai ceu sovent tant que tuit li ver issent.	do this frequently until all the worms come out.
Et s’il n’obeissent a issir, si estoupe entor la cainne de coton si com j’ai dit en la piere;	And if they don't come out, then stop up the ear with cotton as I have said in the section on stones;
et s’il ne saillent fuer si com nos avons dit, si aministre distillations que li ancien ont esprovees en l’ocision des vers, et tu les troveras ou traitier des distillations;	and if they don't come out as we have described, then administer the distillations that the ancients have tried in the extraction of worms, and you will find them in the section on distillations;
et si distille tes oiles et tes medicines en l’oreille a tout cest estrument, de coi ci est li forme si com tu vois:	and if you distill your oils and medications into the ear with all this equipment, so that it is shaped as you see it:
Et soit d’argent ou d’arain estrois desoz a I petis pertuis, et desus overs por distiller;	And let there be tubes of silver or bronze beneath the small holes and above for distillation;
et por presser dedens la distillation a I estrument d’arain bien fait por ceu, et se tu vues pren I raseur et envoloupe entor la pointe avenanment coton;	and to push into the distillation within the instrument of bronze well made for this purpose, and if you see take a razor and wrap cotton around the point neatly;
puis i giete ton oile ou ton jus, et ceu que tu vues de tes medicines en la cainne, et li caine soit en l’oreille;	then pour your oil or juice, and whatever you want of your medications into the canal, and let the canal be in the ear;
puis boute dedens lou raseur a tout lou coton, et presse ta main tempreement tant que li oile soit distilleit ou chevement de l’oreille;	then put within the razor all the cotton, and press your hand gently until the oil is distilled into the canal of the ear;
et lou sente li malaides dedens, et soit li distillations I poc eschaufee au feu ainsois c’on la distille en l’oreille;	and let him feel the pain within, and let the distillation be heated by fire so that it is distilled into the ear;
et garde qu’elle ne soit trop froide, car li medicine ne seroit mie si bone.	and make sure it is not too cold, because the medicine would not be as good.
de l’estoupement des oreilles	of the cleaning of the ears
Aucun enfant naissent qui n’ont nul pertus ens oreilles;	No child is born without an opening in their ears;
et ceste meisme chose avient as homes par estoupement de plaie, ou de char nee dedens l’oreille, et cist estoupemens vient aucune fois em parfont en l’oreille, si c’on ne lou puet veoir;	and the same thing happens in houses through a blockage of the ear, or from pus born within the ear, and this blockage sometimes bursts open in the ear, if one cannot see it;
et aucune fois avient I poc defuer lou pertus, et lou voit om bien.	and sometimes there is a slight discharge from the opening, which one can see quite clearly.
Celle donques que vient em parfont, si c’on ne la puet veoir, est de grief sanation em plusors dispositions, et en cele c’on voit covient que tu mettes l’oreille dou malaide au soleil;	When it bursts open without being seen, it is a sign of a serious condition in many cases, and when one can see it, you should put the patient's ear to the sun;
et regarde dedens:	and look inside:si li pertus de l’oreille est em par
se tu vois l’opilation apparent, si la oevre a tot cest spatumile de coi ci est li forme:	if you see the lining exposed, and the hole in the eardrum is visible, then this is how it should be treated:et s’il n’est pas em parfont, tu mets l’oreille au soleil, et la oevre a tot cest
Et soit agus et trenchans devant et derrier tout plain, si qu’il ne blece l’oreille;	And let it be sharp and pointed at both ends, so that it does not pierce the ear.
se li opilation est de char nee ou cors de l’oreille, si la tien as pinceures subtilz, et la cope legierement, tant que celle chars soit toute ostee.	if the operation is on the cartilage of the ear, hold it with small forceps and cut gently until all the cartilage is removed.
Et se li opilations est em parfont en l’oreille, si pren I raseur subtil legier et l’eschaufe un petit au feu, puis li met ou cors de l’oreille.	And if the growths are deep in the ear, take a thin, small razor and heat it slightly in the fire, then place it on the body of the ear.
Se tu sens l’opilation dont li malaides sent grieteit a l’oïr, perce legierement, et garde que tu ne grever les ners de l’oreille;	If you feel the operation where the patient feels great pain in his ear, pierce gently and be careful not to cut the nerves of the ear;
puis met en l’oreille une tente selonc la largesce dou pertus, et la moille en l’oignement egyptien.	then insert a tent into the ear according to the size of the hole, and moisten it with Egyptian ointment.
Fai ceu aucun jor tant que li plaie soit soudee, ou tu pren une tente et la moille en aigue rose, et poudre sus vitriole broiet;	Do this for several days until the wound is closed, or take a tent and moisten it with rose water, and powder over with ground vitriol;
et se tu vois enflee l’oreille, si couvient que tu traies la tente et remue une autre tente moillie en cerote qui soit fait d’oile roset et de cire, tant que li enfleure soit ostee;	and if you see the ear is swollen, it is necessary to pull out the tent and insert another tent moistened with cerotum made of rose oil and wax, until the swelling is removed;
puis le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	then treat it until it heals.
Et se decorremens de sanc vient, si plonge une esponge et drapelz en aigue froide, et le met sus l’oreille, et use d’autres cures qui oste lou decorrement de sanc qui sont ou traitier des destillations.	And if there is bleeding, take a sponge and dip it in cold water, and apply it to the ear, and use other remedies which stop the bleeding that come from distilling treatments.
de la char des papieres	from the ash of papers
Cist althelul que vienent em papieres des eulz quant ils sont moiste et sont sec, si covient que tu les estendes de tenailles et de pinceures, et le cope d’un spatumile de ses racines;	This is a description of a treatment for hair that is damp and tangled. The instructions are to use tweezers and pinches to straighten it out from the roots, and then cut off the ends with a spatulum.
puis met sor le leu vitriole broiet.	then apply powdered vitriol to the area.
Et se sans en decort, si le cauterize dou cautere lenticulaire subtil, et li cauterizeir aprés l’incision vaut mues;	If there is no scabs, then cauterize it with a thin lens-shaped cautery iron, and after the incision, apply honey.
et maintes fois repairent, cant aucune chose demoure de lor racines;	Many times they grow back, as nothing remains of their roots;
et quant elles sont cauterizees par feu, si sont arses celles racines et ne revienent mie.	and when they are cauterized by fire, the roots are burned and they do not return.
de la gresle	of hail
Maintes fois vienent em papieres des eulz unes choses que semblent gresle en sa forme et en sa duresce, et por ceu est ceste maladie apelee «grandine», et est une assemblee de moistor grosse en la papiere desus et desoz;	Many times, a substance that looks like gravel forms on the hair, and this is what the disease is called "hail," as it is a collection of thick moisture above and below the hair.
li ovraiges est telz:	the works are such:
pren warde se li grandine se muet d’une part et d’autre, et c’est legiere chose a savoir;	take care that hail does not strike from both sides simultaneously, and this is an easy thing to understand.
fent la donques dou large, puis l’escorche de chescune partie legierement, puis la prent as pinceures, et la cope.	then make a large cut, then very gently peel the skin from each side, and then grasp it with forceps and stitch it up.
se tu ne la pues coper sens percier un poc la papiere, si ne grieve rien au malaide;	if you cannot sew it closed without piercing the paper a little, do not worry, as this will not harm the patient;
et se li fendure est grans, si l’assemble a une costure, et la cure tant qu’ele soit sanee;	and if the wound is large, stitch it closed and treat it until it is healed;
et s’elle est petite, si n’i faire point de force, car li oignemens la restoure tantost et enjanre char.	and if it is small, do not force it shut, as the natural healing process will restore and close it quickly.
Et se li grandine est dessendans au dedens de l’oreille vers la partie desus, si enverse la papiere, et estent la grandine a unes pinceures, et la cope et presse d’une part et d’autre;	And if the hematoma is descending into the ear towards the upper part, turn the paper inside out and grasp it with forceps and stitch it up, pressing from both sides;
et se li papiere est esloignie par l’incision, ce ne grieve rien;	and if the paper is removed by incision, this does not matter;
et quant li grandine est copee, si leive l’oil d’aigue salee, et cure le leu de ceu qui enjanre char tant que li malaides soit sanez.	and when the blisters are cut, wash with salty water and treat the area with a poultice until the patient is healed.
de la graisse des eulz	of the fat of the eyes
Exinach est une graisse qui est enjanree en toiles des papieres desus, et ce avient plus as enfans c’a nules gens, et grieve mout a lor eulz, et li vienent li catharre as matinees, et ne pueent regardeir la lumiere dou soleil por ceu que les larmes se hastent a lor eulz;	Eczema is a fat that is woven into the paper-thin skin of children and the elderly, and it is very painful. They get pus in the mornings and cannot look at sunlight because their tears flow freely.
et por ceu se couchent il sor lor faices adés, et dorment sus, et sont lor papieres desoz lor sorcilz moistes que li enfleure et li apparance ont covert de l’exinach qui apert en l’oil.	This is why they sleep with their mouths open and snore, because the skin around their eyes is wet and swollen, covering the eczema that appears in the corners of their eyes.
Et quant tu presses lou leu a tes dois et sent l’exirnach entr’ous.	And when you press the place between your fingers and feel the exinach between them.
Et li maniere de l’ovraige si est que li malaides mette son chief en ton sain;	And the way to treat this is for the patient to put his head on the lap of the healthy person;
et puis pren I drapeil de lin, et appareille une tente em maniere d’un cercle selonc la quantiteit que conteigne exirnach de chescune partie, puis le met sus li;	And then take a linen cloth, and prepare a tent in the manner of a circle according to the quantity that contains exirnach from each part, then place it on him;
et presse a tes dois d’une part et d’autre, si que li exirnach soit assemblez emmi le cercle;	And press with your fingers on both sides so that the exirnach is gathered within the circle;
puis fent em mileu de la moistor au spatumile trenchant une fendure dou large, et ne soit mie plus grans que li plaie c’on fait a la sainie de voinne;	Then make in the center of the moisture with a sharp spatula a slit that is not wider than the wound one makes to let blood out of a vein;
et fent le cuir em parfont tant que tu veignes a l’exirnach;	And cut through the skin down to the bone until you reach the exirnach;
et em plusors dispositions vient exirnach de la fendure, selonc la forme d’une piece de graisse blainche.	And in many cases, exirnach comes out of the slit, according to the shape of a piece of white grease.
Estrai la donques a tout une piece de drap charpit entre tes dois au defuer, et torne ta main a destre et a senestre tant qu’il soit espars;	Therefore, take it all out with a piece of cloth squeezed between your fingers, turning your hand to the right and left until it is spread out;
et garde que tu n’ajoster en la fendure, que tu ne viegnes a tout le spatumile jusc’a l’oil, que tu ne le bleces.	and be careful not to cut into the fissure, or you will reach all the way to the eye and injure it.
Et se li exirnach n’apert en l’encomencement de la fendure, si acroi un poc la fendure legierement tant qu’il apere;	And if the pus does not open at the beginning of the fissure, then gently widen the fissure slightly until it opens;
puis l’estrai si com nos avons dit, puis moille drapelz en aisil et en aigue, et met sus le leu, et estrain de bendelz.	then extract it as we have said, then moisten the area with water-soaked cloth and apply pressure to stop the bleeding, and finally bind it up tightly.
Et si a de tels homes qui broient seil et mettent sus por corrompre cele moistor qui est demoree.	And if there are men who grind salt and place it on to corrupt that moisture which remains.
Puis le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then heal it until it is cured.
Et s’il vient au leu aposteme chaut, si lou cure d’emplaustres assouajant tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if a hot abscess comes to the place, then treat it with cooling poultices until it is healed.
des poilz des papieres	of hair from papers
Quant em papieres naissent poilz ajostez autre que li naturez, et sont enveillit, si nuisent as eulz, et font venir manieres de maladies si com larmes acostumees et mollifications des papieres et albugine, tant que c’est cause de la destruction des eulz;	When hairs grow from paper, other than the natural color, and they turn grey, then they harm the eyes, and cause various diseases such as inflammation of the eyelids, softness of the paper, and white film, until it leads to the destruction of the eyes;
et est li cure selonc IIII manieres:	and there are three ways to treat this:
ou par cautere ensamble feu, ou par medicine ague selonc ceu qu’il est devant ou chapistre de cautere, et est fais ou par incision et costure ou par caines, selonc ceu que je dirai.	either by cauterization with fire, or with medicine according to what is written in the chapter on cauterization, and it can be done by incision and stitching, or with tweezers, according to what I will describe.
Il covient que tu mettes lou chief dou malaide en ton sain, puis torne la papiere de l’oil a ta main senestre;	You must place the patient's head in your lap, then return the paper to your left hand.
s’elle est convertie, c’est boin;	If it is converted, that is good.
se ceu non, si i boute une aguille a tout I fil desus;	If not, put an awl through the thread.
et soit ce delez la marge de la papiere ou li poil naissent delez ces poilz, et trai I fil au desus a tout la papiere, et la torne au raseur;	and it is to be at the edge of the paper where the hairs grow along these hairs, and draw the thread across to the other side of the paper, and return it to the razor.
puis fent en la partie desoz la papiere, desoz les poilz ajostez, a tout le spatumile copant, des le grant larmier jusc’au petit;	Then they make an incision under the paper, under the hairs, all the way to the great artery, just to the small one.
puis estrai I fil, et met desoz la papiere une petite tente de couton et de drapeil, puis seigne sus la papiere une figure d’enche, si com la fuelle de mirte, et toutevoie il covient que li figure soit selonc la quantiteit que tu vues eslever la papiere qui est devisez a toz.	Then pull out the thread, and place under the paper a small tent of cotton and linen, then mark on the paper a figure in the shape of an inchworm, as the fuel of myrtle, and still according to the quantity you see rising up through the divided paper.
Et si a teil qui a mestier c’on cope grant quantiteit de la papiere selonc ceu que li papiere est mollifie;	And if to one who needs it, he applies a large amount of the paper according to how soft the paper is;
puis fent a tout le spatumile sus les II lignes que tu as signiet, et comence des lou grant larmier jusc’a petit;	then make the spatumile over the 2 lines you have signed, and start from the large armpit up to the small one;
et soit li une des fendures pres des poilz naturez en la groissece d’un raiz, puis boute l’oncine en l’un des II angles dou keur, puis l’escorche toute;	and let one of the slits be near the natural hair in the thickness of a hair root, then pierce the skin in one of the 2 angles of the heart, then peel it all off;
puis assemble les II levres a une costure d’une aguille a tout I fil de laine subtil, et essue le sanc, et fai aerdre la superfluiteit des filz sus les II sorcilz a tout aucunes choses gluans, se tu vues faire ce;	then join the 2 lips with a single thread of fine wool through an eye needle, and stop the bleeding, and dry up the excess threads over the 2 eyelids with any sticky substance if you see fit to do so;
et se ce non, si n’en aies cure, puis laisse la costure et les filz jusc’a III jors ou IIII;	and if not, then don't worry about it, and leave the stitches and threads for 3 or 4 days;
puis cure la plaie sens costure de choses sechans et constrignans, car li papiere se relive au soudement de la plaie et l’assemblement de li, mais li costure est muedre (si com dirent li ancien), et c’est ovraiges sens paor;	then dress the wound without suturing with dry and constricting things, for paper lifts up suddenly from the wound and its closing, but sutures are painful (as the ancients say), and this is a work without fear;
et si a une autre maniere:	and if in another way:
et est que tu seignes la papiere d’une figure qui soit ausi com li fuelle de mirte, si com nos avons conteit, a III oncines desevrez selonc la forme qui est ci:	and you should mark the paper with a shape that is also like the leaf of myrtle, as we have described, at three inches removed according to the form which is here:
puis cope ceu qui sormonte as petites forces igalment selonc la forme qui est ci:	then cut what is on top into small pieces evenly according to the shape that is there:
Et se tu n’as pooir de tenir les tenailles, et li chose n’est mie igalz, si prent une aguille ou il ait I fil, et la boute emmi la figure;	And if you cannot hold the tweezers and the object is not straight, then take a needle with a thread and weave it through the shape;
et boute I autre fil delez lou grant larmier, et lou secont fil delez lou petit, et assemble entre tes dois les filz igalment;	and weave another thread through the larger pore, and the second thread through the smaller, and bring the threads together evenly between your fingers;
puis lieve ta main igalment, et lieve tout le cuir sus coi tu as signiet, si com nos avons conteit, puis assemble les II levres de la plaie par costure, et le cure tant qu’il soit sanez;	then lift your hand evenly, and lift all the skin that you have marked, as we have described, then bring together the two lips of the wound by suturing, and dress it until it is healed;
et se aposteme vient a ton incision, si l’apaise de cerote et de semblans oignement assouajans;	and if an abscess comes to your incision, then soothe it with cerotem and similar soothing ointments.
et aucune fois avient que li poil de la papiere sont convertit:	and sometimes the hairs of the paper are converted:
si covient que tu uses ceu que nos avons dit de l’incision;	if you should use what we have said about the incision;
mais li costure en l’une et en l’autre est plus artificialz.	but the stitching in one and the other is more artificial.
Li cure des caines si est selonc ceste forme:	The treatment of bones is as follows:
et est que tu convertisses la papiere et la fent dedens selonc ceu que j’ai dit, et puis fai II caines par art, et II liiens subtilz ausi lonc com li papiere et li largesce dou spatumile est;	and is to convert the paper and insert it inside according to what I have said, then make two bones by art, and two subtle strings as long as the paper and the spatulum is wide;
et cope as II chiés de II pars ou tu tiens les filz;	and cut as two heads on either side where you hold the strings;
puis assemble l’un et l’autre subtilment sus ceu que sormonte de la papiere de l’oil, et estrain les II cainnes des II parties forment;	then assemble one and the other subtly above what is on top of the paper of the eye, and straining the two bones from the two formed parts;
et le laisse ensi aucuns jors, et li cuir qui iert estrainte morra et nercira et porrira, tant qu’il cherra par lui.	and let it remain thus for a few days, and the skin that is stretched will die and shrivel and fall off as it dries.
S’il tarde, si le cope a unes forces, puis le cure tant qu’il soit sanez;	If it takes time, if the wound has some strength, then treat the scar until it heals;
et quant li plaie iert soudee, et si ert levee li papiere, et ne poindront plus li poil;	and when the wound is sewn up and the paper is lifted, the hairs will no longer be pricked;
et c’est li forme des II cainnes que tu feras selonc ceste figure, et selonc ceste quantiteit de lonc et de large:	And this is the form of the II chains that you will make according to this figure, and according to this quantity of long and wide:
li ovraiges est telz que tu preignes une aguille subtil, et i boute I fil de soie souef et subtil;	The work is such that you thread a fine needle, and put in it a fine silk thread;et li bout esguisies, et li passe au traittement des ovraiges sus la piere ou sur les saiges, et ad leu les guarisit.
puis assemble les chiés et noe l’un et l’autre subtilment, et soit li longesce des filz une palme de lonc;	Then assemble the heads and tie them together deftly, and let the length of the threads be a palm long;et si adonques covient que tu le remees en la dislocation du chie, car il ne peuit demorer ains doit ad les remuement de l’ovraige qu’il revint.
puis ordene en la chasse I autre fil subtil de soie briément, et noe les chief dou fil;	then place in the wound another fine silk thread, and tie the ends of the thread together.
puis mette li malaides son chief en ton sain;	then put the patient's head into your lap;
et soit delez lou soleil si que li ovraiges soit declairiez, car c’est uns ovraiges subtilz et menus, puis boute l’aguille a tout la chasse en la racine dou poil ajosteit, et la fai percier en la papiere hastanment tant que tu la traies desus lou poil natureil;	and be in the shade so that the work is clearly seen, for this is a fine and delicate work. Then insert the needle into the skin at the root of the hair, and pierce through the paper slowly while pulling the thread through above the natural hair;
puis estrai le poil jusque sus la chasse, et boute en la chasse celui poil, s’il en i a I ou II ou III ou plusors;	then pull out the hair to the surface of the skin, and put in that hair into the wound, whether there is one, two, three, or more hairs;
puis estrai ta main tant que li poilz veigne fuers a tout la chasse en la papiere avec lou poil natureil.	then pull your hand back so that the hair comes out through the skin and paper with the natural hair.
Et se li chasse est traite et li poilz ne vient fuer avec li, si trairas la chasse au desoz a tout le fil que tu i as ordeneit, tant que li chasse veigne fuer dou pertus desus et que tu la voies par la vision de l’oil;	And if the wound is treated and the hair does not come out with it, then pull at the thread that you have placed in the wound from underneath, until the wound comes out through the opening above and you can see it with your eye.
adonques si trairas la chasse et le fil, et clo l’oil et lou laisse clo II jors ou III, tant que li poil s’aerde en son leu et naisse li char sus;	then you will pull out the hair and thread, and close the eye and leave it closed for two or three days, until the hair grows back in its place and the skin grows over it.
et se li poilz est petis, si acompaigne I poil lonc des chevoulz naturez, et soit alevez avec celui ou tu le laisse, tant qu’il soit eslongiez et puis le lieve.	And if the hairs are short, accompany them with a long hair from the eyebrows, and let it grow with that one, until it is grown out and then you can pluck it out.
de la porriture de l’oil	of the eye pustule
Quant ceste maladie qui est apelee «aleacrati» ou li porriture vient en l’oil, si en i a de II manieres:	When this disease called 'aleacrati' or warts comes in the eye, there are two ways in which it can manifest.
l’une natureil, et l’autre innatureil.	One is natural, and one is supernatural.La natureile est qu’alques fois li ommes ayent en lor oeuil un porriture
Et avient par soudement de plaie, ou de tailleure ou de cautere, et par semblans choses.	And it happens suddenly from a wound, or cutting, or cauterization, and similar things.
Et li maniere de l’ovraige en li est que tu fendes celle soudure, et dessevre les levres de li, et met dedens tentes de lin, et la lie tant qu’elle soit sanee;	The natural way is that sometimes people have a wart in their eye. And the treatment for this is to split the wart, open up its edges, place linen tenters inside it, and keep it clean until it heals.et li natureil est que alques fois li ommes ayent en lor oeuil un porriture qui soit natureile, c’est asses que la soudure se fende et la peau s’eslieve et ne soit point brusee, si
et ne covient mie que tu uses en la cure de li de choses que sechent et restraignent.	and you must not use in the treatment of it things that dry and constrict.
Car se tu fais ceu, si revient li maladie pire que li premiere;	For if you do this, the disease will return worse than before;
mais i oevre de choses amollissans, si com fenugreic;	but work with softening things, such as fenugreek;
et l’arose d’aigue ou altee et semence de lin soient cuites, et oignemens dyaquilon fondut en aucun des oiles, et i envoloupe une tente, et le cure de ceu.	and rosewater or elderflower and flaxseed are cooked, and onions fried in some oil, and wrap it in a tent, and treat it this way.
Et li tresors de ta cure si est que tu te dones en garde qu’ele ne soude mie selonc la forme qu’elle fut devant;	And the essence of your treatment is to ensure that it does not harden according to its previous shape;
et cist ovraiges que nos avons dit nen est fuers que adresemens de ceste maladie, qu’elle ne reviegne selonc la forme qu’elle fut devant.	and these procedures that we have described are not remedies for this disease, so that it does not return according to its previous shape.
de la char qui vient en l’oil	from the pus that comes in the eye
Ceste maladie que est desoz qui vraiement est apelee «axacrati», et est naturelz et accidens.	This disease which is below and which is truly called "axacrati", and is natural and accidental.
Li accidens vient de plaie et de fendure et de cautere et de choses semblans;	Accidents come from wounds and cuts and cauterization and similar things;
et li voie de l’ovraige en li si est que tu preignes un aguille, en coi il ait I fil double, et la fiche en la char, et li fai percier des le senestre larmier tant c’a destre, si que li filz veigne en II chiés de la char;	and the way to do this is to take a needle and thread it with a double thread, and insert it into the flesh, and make it pierce from one earlobe to the other, so that the thread comes out in both ears;
puis estent la char au desus a tout l’aguille, et la cope a I spatumile large.	then the hair is pulled up to the top of the needle, and the cap is placed over the broad spatula.
Et se li figure de la papiere revient selonc ceu qu’il covient, c’est boin;	And if the shape of the paper returns as it should, that is good;
se ceu non, si pren I raseur et le met en la fendure, et torne la papiere, et fent II fendures ou costeit dedens la papiere;	if not, then take a razor and place it in the slit, and turn the paper over, and make two slits along the inside of the paper;
et soient li chiés des II fendures des II angles de l’incision que tu as copeit, et soit fais uns angles si que quant elles sont assemblees, que li figure soit ausi com li figure d’une lettre qui a non «I griesche»;	and let the edges of the two slits be the two angles of the incision that you have cut, and make angles so that when they are assembled, the shape is like the shape of a letter which has the form «I griesche»;
puis oste celle char, selonc la quantiteit que ses costez est agus desoz, de ceu qui enseut la papiere, puis ajoste les II parties desevrees, et les cout d’un fil de lainne;	then remove this hair, according to the amount that its sides are cut under, from that which follows the paper, then join the two separated parts and sew them with a thread of wool;
puis lou cure de ceu que nos avons dit des medicines mollifians, et de tentes, tant qu’il soit sanez.	then treat it with what we have said about the softening remedies, and with poultices, until it is healed.
Et se li maladie vient de fendure ou de costure ou de cautere, si covient que tu fendes une fendure plainne desoz les poilz des papieres, et selonc ceu qui est ci devant;	And if the disease comes from a split or stitch or cautery, then you must make a clean split under the hair of the eyelids, and according to what is written above.
puis desevre entre les II leivres d’une tente, si com j’ai dit;	then split between the two lips of the tent, as I have said.
et doit on faire l’ovraige selonc la forme de la maladie, car elle est mout diverse en forme, et li saiges maistres appareille engien de tout som pooir coment il faice revenir la figure a sa forme natureil;	And one must do the work according to the form of the disease, because it is very diverse in form, and the wise master prepares tools with all his might so that he may bring the form back to its natural shape.
et li malaides meisme, selonc ceu qu’il i covient d’ovraige et d’estrumens em plusors dispositions.	And the disease itself, according to what it needs in terms of work and instruments, in many different arrangements.
dou soudement de la papiere	Sudden movement of the skin
Quant ceste soudure avient a mains homes en teil maniere que li papiere desus est sodee avec le blanc de l’oil, et ne puet movoir ne faire ses ovraiges naturez, si covient donques que tu i boutes la pointe d’un raseur desoz la papiere, et la lieve en haut;	When this soudure happens to men in such a way that the papery part above is separated from the white of the eye, and cannot move or perform its natural functions, then you must insert the tip of a razor under the papery part and lift it upward;
et l’estent as pinceures, tant que tu copes ceu qui est aert au spatumile subtil, qui ne soit mie trop agus ne trop trenchans, si que li malaides ne puisse soffrir que li spatumile trop agus ne blecent l’oil;	and stretch them as pins until you reach the тонкие, not too pointed or too sharp, so that the patient does not feel pain and the тонкие do not hurt the eye;
et soit ton incision, dont tu escorche celle assemblee, legierement, si que li papiere reviegne selonc sa forme natureil;	and make your incision lightly, so that the paper returns to its natural shape;
et est sanee toute celle assemblee, et font aucune fois en l’oil aigue salee, et le leve d’aigue douce, et de coliere;	and all of this assembly is healed, and sometimes in the eye there is a salty water, and they lift it with fresh water, and bandages;
puis met entre la papiere et l’oil une tente de lin, et met sus l’oil laine moillie en abun d’uef;	then place between the paper and the eye a tent of linen, and place on the eye wool dampened with egg;
et aprés le tier jor use dou coliere et des choses soudans tant qu’il soit sanez.	and after the third day, use a bandage and soothing things until it is healed.
de l’ungle de l’oil	of the nail of the eye
Saiches que li ungle est selonc II manieres:	You know that the nail is in two ways:
elle est nervouse et semblans a I dur syfac, et une autre qui n’est mie nervouse, mais est semblans a blainche moistor congelee, que quant on la touche de fer et on la cuide panre as pinceures, si ne puet om;	it is nervous and resembles a hard cyst, and another that is not nervous, but resembles frozen white moisture, which, when touched with iron and pinched, cannot be pierced by anyone;
et l’une et l’autre semblance encomence devers le grant larmier, et croist poc et poc tant qu’ele cuevre toute la veue et toute la lumiere et le movement de l’oil.	and both appear from the great tear duct, and grow little by little until they cover the entire eye and all sight and movement.
Et li maniere de l’incision si est que li malaides mette son chief en ton sain, puis li oevre les eulz;	And the way of the incision is that the patient puts his head to you, then you work on them.
et lieve la papiere a ta main, puis coil l’ungle as pinceures de petite doubleure, et l’estent au desus;	and lightly hold the eyelid in your hand, then use your fingernails like tiny pincers, and stretch it upwards;
puis pren une aguille, et i met I poil de cheval, ou de vaiche, ou de buef, et I fil fort;	then take a needle, and thread it with horsehair, or cow hair, or ox hair, and strong thread;
et double la pointe de l’aguille un poc et la fiche emmi l’ungle, et la perce a tout l’aguille, et lie l’ungle d’un fil et l’estent au desus, et escorche a tout lou poil le costeit de l’ungle qui enseut la prunele et la soie au poil jusc’au chief, puis cope lou remanant en la racine dou larmier a tout lou spatumile subtil et as petites forces, et laisse la char natureil ou larmier, si que par l’incision ne veigne li cors des larmes acostumeement;	and double the needle's point slightly and insert it into the eyelid, and pierce all the way through the needle, and tie the eyelid with a thread and stretch it upwards, and scrape along the edge of the eyelid that follows the tear duct to the eye socket gently and with small forces, and leave the natural channel for tears, so that by the incision the body's tears do not leak;
et aucune fois s’estent li ungle a l’oncine soulement, et au fil, si com nos avons dit;	and sometimes only the nail at the finger or toe is affected, and on the thread, as we have said;
puis l’escorche on a tout le spatumile souef de coi ci est li forme:	then there is scaling all over the scrotum, from which comes the form of this disease.
Et garde que li spatumile ne touche la toile charnue et la rompe, et que li prunele ne soit percie;	And be careful that the scrotum does not touch and break the flesh-colored membrane, and that the foreskin is not pierced;
et aprés l’incision giete en l’oil un poc de seil broiet, et dou coliere fait de litargire, et le laisse jusc’a l’autre jor;	and after the incision, put a little crushed vitriol in the eye, and the collar made of litharge, and leave it until the next day;
puis le cure de ceu qu’il i covient tant qu’il soit sanez.	then treat it as needed until it is healed.Et se li gautes de l’oil sont troves ou l’incision a este feite, si li traie le sang par la fente, et li
Et se li ungle n’est mie nervouse, et tu ne pues bouter l’aguille, et li uncines n’i puet entrer, maintes fois est curee ceste semblance d’ungle de medicines;	And if the eyelids are swollen where the incision was made, and the thread draws blood from the wound, and the
et naissent sicom j’ai conteit en la division, et se tu la vues coper, si oevre l’oil dou malaide, et pren le spatumile legier poc agut selonc ceste forme:	and they grow as I have described in the division, and if you see it covered, then operate on the eye of the patient, and take the spatulum lightly, poking gently according to this form:
Et reis l’ungle desus subtilment, et se tu vois qu’elle amenuise point et li rasion i apresse, si distille de ta bouche en l’oil coliere fait de litargire et dou coliere rouge et seil broiet, et estoupe l’oil jusc’a l’autre jor;	And gently press the nail on top, and if you see that it does not lessen and the inflammation gets worse, then drop from your mouth into the eye a collar made of litarge and red copper ore, ground up, and stop up the eye until the next day;
puis rencomence l’autre ovraige selonc ceste meisme oevre, tant qu’elle soit toute ostee.	then restart the other work according to this same method, until it is completely removed.
Se aucune chose ne t’est contraire en l’oil, si com aposteme chaus, adonques la lait, et cure premier l’aposteme chaut tant qu’il soit sanez, puis rencomence l’ovraige si com devant, tant qu’il soit sanez.	If nothing is contrary to you in the eye, such as a hot abscess, then milk it, and first cure the hot abscess until it is healed, then begin again the work as before, until it is healed.Et se il y aveit aposteme froid, adonques cure l’aposteme par le chaus; et si tu vois qu’elle ne voulent point arder, si distille en l’oil du vin de groseille, et du coliere dou ver, et du litargire, et du sal amoniac; et si la chose n’est pas trop chaude, si peit de ta bouche.
Et se li apparance de la chair dou larmier nuit en l’oil par grant nuisement, si la sospent a l’oncine, et en cope une partie et non mie tot, que cors de larmes n’i viegne;	And if the appearance of the flesh around the eyelid is harmful to the eye through great damage, then suspend it on the lid, and cut off a part and not all of it, so that no tear fluid enters;
puis distille en l’oil coliere rouge qui est fais de litargire.	then drop into the eye red collar made of litarge.
de la char qui naist sus la prunelle	of the flesh that grows over the pupil
Es eulz d’aucuns homes naist aucune fois char rouge, et cuevre la prunele et restraint sus les papieres et les torne au defuer, et semble une rose de balauste;	In some men, a red lump sometimes grows from their testicles, covering the scrotum and constricting it on top of the papers, and it looks like a rose from a balcony.
et li ovraiges si est que li malaides mette son chief en ton sain, puis li oevre les eulz, et coil toute celle char as uncines convenaubles a ceu, et la sostien a la force;	and the treatment is for the patient to put his head on something firm, then he works on the lump, and then he twists it into knots appropriate for that purpose, and holds it firmly in place.
puis cope la premiere char, et vai tout copant au raseur jusc’a la fin, et te garde que tu ne bleces l’oil a l’ovraige;	Then he shaves the first lump, going all around at the base, and you must be careful not to cut the eye during this treatment.
et soit li incision dou spatumile que nos avons dit en l’incision de l’ungle et as petites forces de coi on oste lou sebel, si com li forme aprés cest chapistre lou demostre;	and make an incision at the bottom of the testicle, as we have described in the section on incisions for nails, and with small tools you remove the pus, as the diagram in this chapter shows.
et quant li incision est acomplie et ostee toute li char, si emple l’oil de seil broiet ou tu i distille coliere rouge et semblans medicines corrosives, et met sus l’oil defuer coton avec abin d’uef, si qu’il soit asseurez d’aposteme chaut;	And when the incision is complete and all the pus has been removed, apply a mixture of egg white and red vitriol to the eye, and then cover it with cotton soaked in egg white so that the abscess remains warm.
et s’il i demore rien, et li sans chaus te sormonte, et tu doutes aposteme chaut, si laisse l’oil et cure l’aposteme de choses apaisant aposteme chaut;	and if it persists, and the hot pus overcomes the blood, and you doubt that it is a hot abscess, then leave the eye and treat the abscess with things that soothe the hot abscess;
puis revien a ton ovraige tant qu’il soit sanez, et ensi fai cant chars est ajostee en l’oil par ceste semblance.	then return to your work until it is healed, and thus you will treat any eye that is affected in this way.
Mais toutevoie il covient que tu aliges la cure de chescun oil foible de la voie natureil;	However, you should still lighten the treatment for each weak eye in the natural way;
et de la voie accident, en ovraige de fer;	and in accidental work, with iron;
et ne bouter mie ta main en aucun de ces ovraiges tant que tu voies que cist membres soit soffrans celui ovraige.	and do not put your hand into any of these works until you see that this member is suffering from that work.
des voines des eulz	of the veins of the eyes
Sebel sont voinnes rouges que sont covertes sus l’oil, et tolent a la veue son ovraige et afoiblissent l’oil toz jors.	So are red veins that are covered over the eye, and tolerate the sight of its work and weaken the eye all day.
Mestier est donques au premier que tu regardes se li oil, en coi sebel est, est fors, et n’i a autre maladie fuers que lou sebel;	So therefore, first you must look at the eye, and see if it is soft, swollen, and free of any other disease except for the ulcer;
adonques le coil en teil maniere:	then treat it in this way:
comande au malaide qu’il mette son chief en ton sain, puis sospent celles voines a tout l’oncine selonc sa sapience, et soit li oncines subtilz double selonc ceste forme:	instruct the patient to put his head in yours, then open the veins all around gently according to your wisdom, and make the openings subtle twice according to this form:
Et soient dui oncine par degrez en .i. cors selonc ceste forme:	And two edges in .I. body according to this form:
puis c’on coil as forces celles voinnes subtilment, et essue lou sanc houre aprés autre, tant que tu voies removoir celles voines fuers de l’oil;	then we press these veins gently, and let the blood flow out an hour after another, until you see the veins recede from the eye;
et garde que tu ne blecier l’oil as pointes des spatumiles, et fai cest ovraige a houre de midi devant lou soleil, et soies mout fervans en ton ovraige si que tu ne copes fuer que celles voinnes;	and be careful not to cut the eye on the points of the spatulas, and do this work at noon before the sun, and be very diligent in your work so that you don't go beyond these veins;
et quant tu avras ce fait, si distille en l’oil coliere vert et rouge por corrumpre ceu qui est demorez dou sebel.	And when you have done this, distill into the eye a green and red collyrium to corrupt what remains of the disease.
Et se tu n’as pooir de coillir tout ceu en celle houre, si fai emplastre sus l’oil de choses apaisans la dolor des eulz, et le laisse aucuns jors tant que li dolors soit apaisie et soit asseurez d’aposteme chaut, puis rencomence selonc ceste maniere qui est devant tant qu’il soit sanez;	And if you do not have the power to collect it all in that hour, then make an ointment for the eye of soothing things for eye pain, and let it be for several days until the pain is eased and there is a hot abscess formed, then start again according to what is before until it is healed.
et c’est li forme des forces:	and this is the form of strength:
de la fistule de l’oil	of the eye fistula
Li mire si nomment «arissati» fistule:	He calls these "arissati" fistulas:
quant tu la cures per cautere et par medicine ague ardant selonc ceu que j’ai devant dit, et elle n’est mie sanee, si est engien en li que tu fendes sus l’aposteme, lai ou il doit meurer, et trai toute la moistor que i est, tant que li os soit descovers.	when you treat it with cautery and medicine with fire according to what I have already said, and it is not healed, then there is a lump in it that you must cut open over the abscess, where it should be, and draw out all the moisture until the bone is exposed.
Et quant li os iert descovers, et tu verras la corruption et la noiror, si la reis a tout l’estrument de coi ci est li forme;	And when the bone is exposed, and you see the decay and blackness, then return to the instrument from which this form comes;
et est apelez «aspre chief», et soit fait de feir inde a I chief reont, et soit pointoiez si com une lime si com il est en la presente forme:	and it is called "aspre chief", and it should be made of iron into a sharp chisel, and pointed like a file as it is in the current form.
Et met sus lou leu de l’os corrumput, puis le torne entre tes dois, et presse ta main un poc tant que tu saiches que celle corruption est rese;	And place it on the decayed bone, then turn it between your fingers and press your hand a little so that you know the decay has been removed;
et fai ceu aucune fois, puis restoure lou leu de medicines exiccatives.	and do this sometimes, then restore the place with drying medicines.
se li leus est soudez, et char i naist, et li cors de la bowe est soudez, et remaint ensi XL jors, et il ne renovele et n’est mie apostemez, et accidens mavais n’i vient, saiches qu’il est sanez;	if the sores are healed, and hair grows from it, and the body of the boil is healed, and remains so for 40 days, and it does not open up again and no bad thing happens, you may know that he is healed;
se ceu non, si n’i a autre engien que de ramener la fistule au pertus dou neif selonc ceste forme:	if not, there is only one other thing to do, which is to open the fistula at its narrow opening according to this form:
et est que tu descuevre de l’os la seconde fois par fer, et par medicines agues, et quant il iert descovers si prent I foret selonc ceste forme, et soit li chiés de fer a III angles, et li fust soit atenuis jusc’a chief si com tu vois ci:	and you must uncover the bone a second time with iron and hot medicines; and when it is uncovered, take an iron tool according to this form, and let the head of the tool have three edges, and let the shaft be tapered to a point as you see here:
puis le met sus l’os delez lou larmier, et esloigne ta main de l’oil I poc, puis torne a tot le foret tant qu’il perce l’os et le sent li malaides par ceu que li vens en ist s’il tient sa main sus son neif;	then place the tool on the bone next to the fistula, and move your hand away from the eye, then return the tool repeatedly until it pierces the bone, and the patient will feel it through his nail if he holds his hand over his nail;
et pues restoure lou leu de medicines seches, si com je t’ai ensigniet, et quant li char naist et endurcist li leus, si vait li matiere au neif;	and then restore the place with dry medicine as I have shown you, and when the flesh has grown and hardened, look at the matter with your fingernail;
si est plus legiere chose au malaide.	if it is a minor issue for the patient.
de l’issue de l’oil	of the exit of the eye:
Quant li eulz apert fuer dou tout en tout, et il ne vient point de destorbier au nef, ne amenuisement, si covient que tu lies lou malaide;	When the eye is fully opened, and there is no disturbance or lessening, then you should bind the patient's eye;
puis le saine, puis li met ventouses ou haterel sens ferir por succier, puis met sus l’oil I liien fait d’acaice et de aloe et d’encens et de sarcocolle, et puis estrain l’oil, et l’emplaustre sus de bendes et de drapelz;	then cleanse the eye, then apply leeches or a hot iron without burning to suck it out, then apply to the eye an ointment made of honey and aloes and incense and myrrh, and then bind it up, and put on bandages and linen;
et li maniere des drapelz si est que tu preignes drapelz assez molz, et double chescun en IIII, et puis met l’un sus l’autre selonc la quantiteit que li eulz en ait mestier;	and the manner of the bandages is such that you fold soft linen several times, and then put one on top of another according to the amount that the eye needs;
puis l’estrain par desus d’un bendeil dur forment, et rencomence les ventouses por succier sens ferir;	then we stretch it with a hard bandage tightly, and reapply the cupping glasses to draw out without hurting.
puis oste les ventouses et laisse l’oil estraint jor et nuit, et se li liiens amolist, si covient que tu l’estraignes mout;	then remove the cupping glasses and leave the area stretched day and night, and if the ligature softens, then you must stretch it tightly.
puis oste lou liien aprés le jor et la nut, et se tu vois l’oil repairier, c’est boin;	then remove the bandage after a day and a night, and if you see the eye iyile, that is good;
se ce non;	if not,
si rencomence l’emplaustre et les drapelz et lou liien et les ventouses tant qu’il soit sanez.	reapply the ointment and the bandages, and the ligature, and the cupping glasses until it is healed.
dou derrompement de toile uvee	from the rupture of a woven cloth
Quant disruptions vient en la toile uvee, puis apert, et vient fuer des papieres si com I grain de resins, et est espoantauble a veoir;	When disruption occurs in the woven web, then it opens, and there comes out of the paper like grains of resin, and is terrible to see;
adonques se tu la vues coper, li ovraiges est telz que tu boutes une aguille en la racine des la partie desoz jusc’a celi desus, puis boute une autre aguille ou il ait I fil double des la partie dou larmier;	then if you see it covering, the work is such that you push a needle into the root of the part below up to the ceiling of the part above; then push another needle where there is a double thread from the eye socket;
et la fai percier, et laisse la premiere aguille selonc la disposition;	and have them pierce, and leave the first needle according to the arrangement;
puis cope lou leu dou fil double et lie une partie de l’uve entor, et l’estraint bien, puis estrai l’aguille et met sus l’oil lainne moillie en abun d’uef;	then thread the double thread through the hole and tie one end around the tissue, and tighten it well; then withdraw the needle and place the other eye of the needle in the moistened wound;
et le laisse tant que li filz chiece avec l’uve, puis cure l’oil de choses confortans tant que li plaie soit sanee;	and let it be until the thread cuts into the tissue, then treat the wound with comforting things until it is healed;
et aucune fois li plaie est restrainte par l’uve chescune part d’un cercle de drap, tant qu’elle soit sanee.	and sometimes the wound is constrained by the cloth on each side in a circle, so that it may be healed.
Et se li eulz done grant apparance, si le perce au spatumile subtil qui viegne em parfont de l’oil, et corre la moistor albuginé et dessende li eulz, et entre ens tantost;	And if the eyes are pushing out, then pierce them with a sharp spatula which comes from the corner of the eye, and correct the white bulging and push in the eyes, and enter immediately;
puis l’estrai tant qu’il soit sanez.	then withdraw it as soon as it is healed.
de la bowe de l’oil	from the socket of the eye
Ceste maladie qui est apelee «alcunnati» nen est fuers que bowe qui est assemblee en l’oil, semblant a aigue dessendant, et ce n’est mie aigue;	This disease which is called "alcunnati" is nothing other than an inflammation which has gathered in the eye, resembling descending water, but it is not water;It may be white or yellow, and it is hot,
et li maniere de l’apparance de l’ovraige si est que tu faices seoir lou malaide sus I siege appareilliet et droit, puis prent le chief entre tes mains de II pars, et lou muef tant que tu voies la bowe venir au desus a tes eulz;	and the manner of the appearance of the work is such that you cause the patient to sit on a prepared and straight seat, then take the head between your hands from both sides, and move it until you see the bow come above your eyes;
puis soit ens fichie, et ne dessende et soit descombree li lumiere, et voie li malaides les choses si com il soloit;	then it is fixed, and the light is dimmed, and the patient sees things as he used to;
et s’elle ne dessent desoz, saiches que c’est aigue, et se li dessendemens de la bowe n’est appareilliez si com nos avons dit.	and if it does not go down, know that it is acute, and if the movement of the bow is not prepared as we have said.
si fai seoir lou malaide entre tes mains, puis prent le spatumile subtil et fent sus la toile cornee I poc par la continuation de la conjunctive avec la toile cornee et la corone, tant que li bowe isse;	have the patient sit between your hands, then take the spatula and gently press on the white of the eye, along the extension of the conjunctiva with the white of the eye and the cornea, until the bow comes out;
et quant elle ert issue, si distille en l’oil aigue chaude mellee a miel, ou aigue ou fenugreic est boillis et miel, puis soit curee d’autre cure tant qu’elle soit sanee.	and when it is out, drop into the eye warm water mixed with honey, or hot water or fenugreek boiled and strained through honey, then cure it with other cures until it is healed.
des aigues de l’oil	of eye waters
Nos avons jai les semblances des aigues en la division, et ceu qu’il covient por percier;	We have learned the appearances of diseases in their varieties, and what is needed to pierce them.
si en oevre selonc la santeit.	act according to health.
Il covient que tu faices seoir lou malaide entre tes mains croisiet, fuers de la lumiere por le soleil, et li lie l’oil sain et estreint mout fort;	You should make the patient sit between your crossed hands, away from the light to avoid the sun, and press his healthy eye tightly while keeping it still.
puis met la papiere de l’oil a ta main senestre se li eulz est senestres, ou a ta main destre se li eulz est destres;	Then, hold the paper over the eye with your left hand if the eye is on the left, and with your right hand if it is on the right.
puis prent en ta main destre, se li eulz est senestres, l’estrument qui est apelez «almagda», ou a ta main senestre, se li eulz est destre;	Take in your right hand, if the eye is on the left, the instrument called "almagda", or in your left hand, if the eye is on the right.
puis met la pointe de l’estrument delez la corone par la groissece d’un rait en celle blenchor de l’oil a la partie dou menor larmier, puis boute l’estrument qui est apelez «almagda» vertuousement, et trestorne ta main tant qu’il perce en la blenchor de l’oil, et sente que almagda viegne a la chose vuide;	Then, place the tip of the instrument, which is called "almagda", alongside the edge of the eyeball at the white part of the eye near where the tear duct is located. Push the instrument gently and firmly until it penetrates the eyeball, feeling for when the almagda reaches the hollow space inside;
et covient que li mesure de la voie almagda soit au parfont de la mesure des l’espaice qui est des la prunele jusc’a la fin de la noirour;	and it is necessary that the measure of the alchemy way be at the bottom of the space measure which is from the prunelle until the end of the nourishment.
et c’est li corone de l’oil;	and that is the crown of the eye;
si verras l’os en celle papiere por la clarteit de la toile cornee, et pues met l’estrument jusc’a leu ou li aigue est, puis l’espresse desoz une voie aprés autre.	if you see the bone in that paper due to the clarity of the horny tissue, then place the instrument where the water is and then press it down a little at a time.
se li aigue dessent maintenant, si voit li malaides devant lui et l’estrument en son oil.	If the water is coming out now, then the patient can see his own instrument and himself in front of him.
Aprés repose I petit, et se li aigue remonte la seconde voie, met la fuer avec l’estrument, et quant elle est ens fichie et ele ne monte, si estrai almagda legierement en tornoiant ta main poc et poc;	After you wait a little, and if the water rises up the second way, push it down with the instrument, and when it is stuck in and does not rise, gently pull out the alchemy while turning your hand a little bit at a time.
et puis remette en aigue un poc de seil gemme, et leive de ceu l’oil dedens.	Then put in some water with a little sealing wax, and leave the eye inside.
Puis met par defuer l’oil estoupes ou lainne moillie en oile roset et en abun d’uef, et lie avec l’oil sain.	Then insert an eyeball soaked in rose oil and abundance of egg white, and bind it with clean eye-oil.
Nos, et cil qui sont de nostre tens, mettons sus comin broiet avec abun d’uef.	We, and those who are from our time, put on comfrey crushed with an abundance of egg white.Et si li aigue ne descend pas la seconde voie, puis remette l’oil de l’autre costé, et met par defuer sus leu de l’eyelet une piece de lainne moillie en oile roset; et lie almain avec l’oil sain.
Et se almagda n’i puet entrer en l’oil par sa duresce, car il i a de teilz homes qui ont trop durs les eulz, si covient que tu preignes l’estrument qui est apelez «alberit», de coi ci est li forme:	And if the almagda cannot enter the eye due to its hardness, for there are some people whose eyes are too hard, then you should take the instrument called "alberit", of which this is the shape:
Et perce donques la conjunctive soulement, et n’aler mie trop em parfont, mais fai I leu subtil, puis i boute almagda, si com nos avons dit;	And so just pierce the conjunctiva, and do not go in too deep, but make the hole subtle, then insert alchemy as we have said.
et au complissement de l’uevre appareille au malaide I dorteur avenant, en coi il dorme sus son dos en I leu tenebrous;	and when the work is complete, prepare for the patient to lie on his back in a dark place;
et soit deveez de toz movemens, et preigne legieres viandes, et ne mueve son chief ne a destre ne a senestre, et soit liiez selonc sa disposition jusc’a tier jor;	and he must be restrained from all movement, and eat light foods, and not move his head or to the right or left, and be tied according to his condition for three days;
puis le deslie en cele maison meisme tenebrouse, et esprueve sa veue, et lou fai veoir aucunes choses, et puis li remet lou lien jusc’a septime jor;	then untie him in the same dark house, and test his vision, and show him some things, and then put the bandage back on until the seventh day;
et ne covient mie que tu faices ceu en l’oure de la cure ou aprés l’incision maintenant, mais il covient que tu aliges ceu, por ceu que li aigue monte hastanment.	and you must not do this during the hour of the procedure or after the incision now, but you must reduce it, so that the water rises rapidly.
se apostemes chaus vient, que tu desliies l’oil devant le septime jor, et l’adrece de ceu qui assouaige aposteme;	if a warm abscess comes, remove the bandage before the seventh day and use that which soothes the abscess;
et quant il est apaisiez, si deslie la veue et met sus sa faice I orilliet por covrir aucun jor, et soit adés en celle maison tenebrouse.	and when it is quiet, he uncovers his face and puts on an eye-patch to protect his eyes from the light, and then he can go into that dark house.
Et puis isse de la maison poc et poc, et se convertisse en ses cas;	And then he leaves the house little by little, and returns to his normal state;
et saiches que nulz deciples ne se doit entremettre en cest cas.	and know that no student should interfere in this case.
Et uns vint a nos qui estoit de la Yrach, qui nos dist que en som pais faisoit om almagda perciet, a coi on succe l’aigue, mais toutevoie je n’en vis onques nul en nostre terre, ne je ne lou lis onques en livres des anciens;	And one came to us from Spain who said that in his country they made almucadars, which they used to draw out water, but I have never seen any in our land, nor have I ever read about them in ancient books;
et par aventure c’est une novele chose.	and perhaps it is a new thing.Et si le poignent est de la guirbe ou de la teste, il conv
Et ce sont les semblances des formes de almagda, por ceu que cil qui ne les conoit les voie;	And these are the similarities of the forms of almucadars, so that those who do not know them may see them;
et soient d’arain proprement:	and they should be made of proper bronze:
Et soient li chief d’aus de ceste meisme subtiliteit, et li derriene en .iij. angles ague.	And let the ends of these be of the same subtlety, and the hindmost have four points.
de la char sor le neis	of the heart above the diaphragm
Aucune fois naissent ou neis chars ajostees diverses, de coi il i a aucunes qui semblent scorpions a mout de piez;	There are times when various types of warts grow on the body, some resembling scorpions with many feet.
et si i a de telz ou il ait char enchancree de fuxe color, et si a char souef de bone color.	Some have warts that are raised and a dark color, while others have warts that are flat and the color of skin.
En celle donques de ces chars qui est souef, et ne mie enchancree, covient que tu faices seoir lou malaide entre tes mains encontre lou soleil;	For those warts which are flat and not raised, you should have the patient sit in your hands facing the sun;
et oevre ses narines, et giete l’oncine a celles chars, et les trai fuers;	and open his nostrils, and breathe onto the warts, and drive them out.
pues cope ceu que tu em pues sostenir au spatumile subtil agut d’une part, tant que tu saiches que celle char est toute ostee.	Then, hold the spatulum firmly with one hand as you know that the wart has been completely removed.
Et s’il en remaint aucune chose c’on ne puisse coper, si l’ovrez a tout I des estrumens subtil legierement, si qu’il n’i demoure rien;	And if anything remains which you cannot scrape away, open it with the sharp end of a straw, so that nothing is left;
et se sans te sormonte, ou aposteme chaus, si lou secort si com il covient;	and if there is an abscess, pierce it as it should be;
et se c’est apostemes malignes, si te haste et lou cauterize tant que li sans soit estainchiez et soient ostees toutes les chars, puis giete ou neis aisil et aigue ou vin.	and if it is a malignant abscess, then hasten and cauterize it until the pus is dried out and all the corrupt matter has been removed; then pour in vinegar or wine and water.
Se li neis oevre, et moistors en vient jusc’a palais, saiches qu’il est sanez;	If the nose works, and moisture comes up to the palate, you will know that it is healthy;
et se moistors ne perce si com il covient, saiches qu’il i a char nee en l’os desus, a coi li estrumens ne vient mie por taillier:	and if moisture does not pass through as it should, you will know that there is corrupt matter in the bone above, and so the instruments will not come to cut it out;
