et sont ausi com les aguilles dont on cout les sorceles, et sont d’arain citrin, ou de fer, ou d’argent, et mues valent cil qui sont jaune, et sont plus esprovez de plonc noir por encerchier les corbeures de fistule;	and they are also like the needles that pierce sorceries, and they are made of brass, iron, or silver, and those with yellow tips are more effective in black pus for surrounding the curves of fistulas;
et sont de III manieres:	and are of three kinds:
grans, moiens, et petis, selonc la quantiteit de la largesce des pertus.	large or small, depending on the size of the hole.
Les formes des oncines sont de mout de semblances, si com tu vois ci:	The shapes of the scissors are very similar, as you can see here:
grans, moiens, et petis;	large, medium and small;
et si a oncines qui ont II corbeures de III manieres ausi;	and there are scissors with two curves of three kinds;
et si a oncines qui ont III corbeures, et sont ausi de III manieres;	and there are scissors with three curves, and they are also of three kinds;
et si a oncines qui ont II corbeures, et oncines d’une corbeure soulement, et sont de III manieres;	and there are scissors with two curves and scissors with only one curve, and they are of three kinds;
et tuit cist sont necessaire en lor leu.	and all these are necessary in their place.
Li chief de ces a coi on fent sont trenchant, et de telz i a qui ne taillent mie fuer que d’une part, dont on escorche les nous, por ceu c’on ne cope la voine ne le nerf;	The heads of these tools are sharp, and some only cut one side, so that they do not cut the vein or nerve;
et de ces intromissoires sont les alemeles reponues en mainches, si que li malaide ne s’en persoivent a l’overture des apostemes;	and these tweezers are placed in handles so that the patient does not hurt themselves when opening abscesses;
et sont de III manieres:	and they are of three kinds:
grant, petit, et moien, si com tu vois;	great, small, and medium, as you can see;
et n’en use on mie fuer que en leu charnut, si com jambes, et bras, et mameles, et as angres, et en semblans leus;	and we do not use them except in fleshy places, such as legs, and arms, and breasts, and in similar places;
et aucune fois fait on I autre estrument petit, semblant a escorces de fistices, selonc ceste forme, a coi on estainche sanc:	and sometimes another small instrument is made, similar to slices of garlic, according to this shape, with which blood is stopped:
et le met on aucune fois au leu qui saine a copement des voines, et as arteres, et aucune fois reont selonc ceste grant forme:	and it is sometimes placed in the area that heals by stopping the flow of blood from the veins and arteries, and sometimes they are cut according to this large form:
Aucune fois enflent les mameles d’aucuns homes quant cil encomencent estre corrumput, tant qu’eles semblent mameles de feme;	Sometimes the breasts of some men swell when they become corrupt, so that they look like women's breasts;
et demorent laides et enflees, et qui les vuet curer, si le covient soier selonc ceste forme des ceste ligne .b. jusques a .g.:	and they remain ugly and swollen, and if anyone wants to cure them, they must cut according to this shape from line b. to line g.:
puis escorche la graisse, et emple la plaie de medicine enjanrant char, puis assemble les II levres de la plaie a costure, et la cure tant qu’ele soit sanee;	then cut into the fat, and fill the wound with healing medicine, then bring together the two lips of the wound with stitches, and heal it until it is cured;
et se li mamele cline aval, et est amolie por sa grandor si com il avient as femmes, si la fent en II costelz desus, par II semblans fendures;	and if the breast sags down, and is softened due to its size as it does in women, then they make two cuts above, through two similar slits;
de coi l’une soit tenans a l’autre a la fin de l’une et de l’autre, si que li plus grans ligne conteigne la menor selonc ceste forme, des ceste ligne .b. jusc’a la ligne .g.;	one of which is attached to the other at their end, so that the larger line contains the smaller according to this form, from line b to line g;
puis escorche le cuir qui est entre les II levres, et oste la graisse, et i amenistre ceu que nos avons dit de costure et de poudres, et ceu qui est necessaire en la cure, tant qu’il soit sanez;	then scrape the skin between the two lips, and remove the fat, and apply what we have said about stitches and powders, and what is necessary for the treatment, until it is healed;
et s’il n’est sanez, ou li incision n’est mie toute faite, por ceu que li malaides ne vuet reposer, ou por le decorrement de sanc, si covient que tu emplisses la plaie de coton moilliet en oignement corrosif;	and if it is not healed, or the incision is not fully made, because the patient will not rest, or due to bleeding, then you must fill the wound with wet cotton soaked in corrosive ointment;
et le laisse tant qu’il menjuce le remenant et la graisse, puis le cure tant qu’il soit saneis.	and let it sit until it absorbs the remainder and the fat, then treat it until it is healed.
des apostemes des asselles	of abscesses of the armpit
Cist apostemes que vienent desoz les asseles sont manieres de scrophules dures ou il ait cotes, et s’en i a que contienent moistor.	This abscess that comes under the armpit is like a hard scrofula, and some contain moisture.
Cil donques qui contienent moistor covient qu’il soient copez selonc ceste forme, des la ligne .b. jusc’a la ligne .g.:	Those who contain moisture should be cut according to this form, from line .b. up to line .g.
Et quant toute li bowe qui est en l’aposteme est vuidie, si emple la plaie de viel coton, et la laisse jusc’a l’autre jor, puis oste tout le coton, et cure d’oignement avenant a ceu tant qu’il soit sanez.	And when all the pus inside the abscess has been drained, employ the wound with old cotton, and leave it until the next day, then remove all the cotton and treat it with appropriate ointment until it is healed.
Et se li apostemes est de semblances de scrophules, si le fent si com nos avons dit en fendures des scrophules, et se li plaie rent bowe, si amenistre cautere si com nos avons dit devant.	And if the abscess is like scrofula, they should proceed as we have said in the treatment of scrofula, and if the wound becomes pus-filled, they should apply cauterization as we have described earlier.
de la routure de l’artere	of the rupture of an artery
Quant li artere est route, et li cuir est soudez qui est sus, si en vient maintes fois apostemes, et tout aussi avient il a la voine enflee et aposteme;	When the artery is open and the skin above it is sewn up, then abscesses often result, and this also happens in the swollen vein and abscess.
et si le conoist on ensi quant c’est por l’artere, si est li apostemes lons em parfont;	and if one knows it thus when it is from the artery, then the abscesses are long and deep.
et quant tu le sens a tes dois, si sens I estraignement;	and when you feel it with your fingers, you feel the estrangement;
et quant c’est por la voine, si est reons defuer aparans;	and when it is from the vein, then there are visible pus and blood;
et c’est folie de coper cest aposteme, et meismement quant il est desoz les asseles et as angres et ou col et em mout d’autres leus, et est mout grans.	and it is foolishness to cover this abscess, especially when it is under the armpits and in the groin, neck, and many other places, and it is large.
Il covient donques eschuir la cure de fer, et celui qui est a chief covient eschuir ausi, et en celui qui est d’enfleure d’artere fent par desus le cuir dou lonc;	Therefore, one must avoid using an iron needle, and that which is on top should also be avoided, and with that which is swollen from the artery, they should pierce through the skin above.
puis oevre la taille as oncines, et depart bellement l’artere des toiles, tant qu’ele soit descoverte;	then cut the arterioles, and carefully separate the artery from the veins, until it is exposed.
puis boute desoz li une aguille, et la fai percier jusc’a l’autre costeit, et estraint l’artere d’un fil double en II leus, selonc ceu que je t’ai ensigniet en l’estraction des II arteres qui sont en temples;	then insert a needle underneath and pierce it all the way to the other side, and compress the artery with a double thread in two places, according to what I taught you in the extraction of the two arteries in the temples.
puis point le leu qui est entre les II liens d’un intromissoire tant que li sans en isse qui i est, et soit deliiez li aposteme;	then puncture the area between the two ties with an introducer, so that the blood flows out and the abscess is drained.
puis amenistre la cure que enjanre bowe, tant que li liien chient;	then administer the cure that turns yellow, until the tie falls off.
puis cure ceu d’oignement avenant a ceu, tant qu’il soit sanez;	then treat it with an appropriate ointment until it is healed.
et se li apostemes est por la taille de la voinne, si covient que tu teignes a ta main ceu que tu pues de l’aposteme a tout le cuir, puis boute l’aguille desoz le leu que tu tiens a ta main, et la fai percier, et i ait I fil double, si que tu le trais de l’autre costeit;	and if the abscess is due to a vein opening, then you should dye your hand with something from the abscess all over the skin, then insert the needle underneath the area you are holding in your hand, and pierce it, and use a double thread so that you can pull it from the other side;
puis lie l’aposteme, si com je t’ai dit, ou liien de l’une de II pars as II chiés dou fil;	then tie the abscess, as I told you, or one of its two parts to the shoulder with a thread.
et se tu doutes que li filz n’isse fuer, si i reboute une autre aguille a tout I fil desoz tout l’aposteme a l’incision de la premiere aguille, et estraint les filz en IIII leus;	and if you fear that the thread might slip out, then insert another needle through both threads under the abscess at the incision of the first needle, and tie the threads in four places.
puis cope l’aposteme tant que li superfluitez en isse, puis cope la superfluiteit dou keur et laisse ceu qui est liiez;	then scrape off the excess pus, then scrape off the excess from the skin and leave what is tied [to the thread].
puis met sus I drapeil moilliet en vin et en oile, puis li amenistre cures de tentes et d’oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez.	then place a moistened cloth in wine and oil on top, then administer treatments of bandages and ointments until it is healed.
des apostemes des ners	of abscesses of the nerves
Ausi com aposteme vienent en l’artere et en la voine, vienent aposteme as ners quant il sont ferut, ou par trop grant travail, et semblans choses.	Also, as abscesses come in the artery and vein, they come to the nerves when they are hurt, or from too much work, and similar things.
Et ceu avient plus sovent as adjutoires et as dois et en toz leus ou il ait jointures, et c’est I grief apostemes, et sa color semble la color dou cors, et est em plusors dispositions sens dolor;	And this happens more often in shoulders and elbows, and all joints where there are abscesses, and the color resembles that of the body, and it has various conditions without pain.
et quant on l’estraint forment, si sent li malaides dolor, et n’est mie em parfont dou cors, mais desoz lou keur;	and when it is tightly restrained, the patient feels pain, and it is not completely in the body, but under the skin.
et muet bien de toutes pars, et ne va ne avant ne arrier, ne desoz ne desus, et celui qui est en jointures ne covient mie coper par fer:	and must be quiet everywhere, and neither go forward nor backward, nor downward nor upward, and that which is in joints should not be covered by iron:
par aventure i vanroit contraction;	by chance there might be contraction;
et cil qui est ou chief ou ou front, fent le cuir au spatumile.	and those who are on the head or forehead, use the spatulum.
Se li apostemes est petis, si le tien a unes tenailles, et le cope en sa racine;	If the abscess is small, hold it with tweezers and cut it at its root;
et s’il est grans, si le sospent a l’oncine, et l’escorche, puis l’oste et assemble la plaie a la costure, et lou cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	and if it is large, they suspend it on the hook, and slit it open, then cut out the stone and close the wound with stitches, and heal it up.
des grosses boces pendans	large bumps hanging
Aucune fois avient en ventres et ne mie autre part thelul, et est une maladie qui est apelee «funge» par la semblance d’aus, et est li racine subtilz, et li chiez gros;	Sometimes this happens in bellies and nowhere else, and it is a disease called 'fungus' because of its resemblance to an ear, and its root is fine but the head is large;
et en i a de petis et de mout grans;	and there are both small and very large ones;
et je vis I home qui en avoit II ou ventre qui estoient plus semblans a funges que ai autre chose, et n’i avoit point de difference, et estoient blanc, et avoient menue racine, et estoient jai fendut, et en corroit adés moistor.	I also saw one man who had two in his belly that looked more like mushrooms than anything else; there was no difference between them, they were white and had thin roots, and they were split open and moist fluid ran from them.
Je les copai et trovai en l’un XVIII onces pesant, et en l’autre VI З., et li ovraiges en l’incision si est que tu regardes se li malaides est moistes, et li color de l’artelul est blainche et moiste et de subtil racine;	I cut them open and found that one weighed 18 ounces and the other 6 ounces; the procedure for incising them is to look at whether the illness is moist, and the color of the articulations is white and moist with fine roots:
si le cope au spatumile large, et soient en ta presence li cautere au feu.	if the spatumil is large enough, and have the fire cautery ready in front of you.
Car au taillier vient maintes fois trop grans decorremens de sanc, et se li sans te vaint, si te haste donques dou cauterizer;	For many times there are great bleeding wounds when cutting, and if the blood does not stop, then hurry to use the cautery:
et se tu vois le malaide espoanteit et paourous de l’incision dou fer, si prent I fil de plonc bien fait, et en lie l’artelul si com nos avons dit, et le laisse II jors;	and if you see the patient frightened and fearful of the iron incision, then take a well-prepared piece of lead wire, bind the articulation as we have said, and leave it for two days;
et puis le restraint, et ne cesser d’estraindre lou fil de plonc tant qu’il cope l’artelul, et chiece par lui sens travail;	and then restrain it, and do not cease to squeeze the hair of the finger until it pops out the joint, and piece by piece without effort;
et se les racines sont grosses, si a paour au coper meismement por le ventre, mais tu em pues bien coper la moitiet, puis le cauterize qu’il ne reviegne;	and if the roots are thick, then have fear of covering it all at once in the same way for the belly, but you can indeed cover half of it, then cauterize it so that it does not return;
puis cure la plaie, et garde que tu ne coper le thelul qui est de fuxe color et de povre sens et de lait regart.	then cure the wound, and be careful not to cover the tubercle which is of a purple color and poor in sensation and of milky aspect.
Car c’est uns apostemes enchancrez, et je venrai a la cure de chancre ci aprés.	For this is a deep abscess, and I will come to the treatment of sores next.
quant li boude ist fuer	when the boil bursts
Se li apparance de la boude vient par cautere de plaie ou de fendure de syfac, et est sus le ventre et en ist aucuns des bouez, si com il avient en autres routures, ou de sanc qui cort de voines ou d’arteres selonc ceu qui est devant, ou de ventositeit;	If the appearance of the boil comes from cauterization of a wound or split ulcer, and it is on the belly and in some of the bowels, as happens in other routings, or of blood coming from veins or arteries according to what is before, or from windiness;
et se c’est par la routure dou syfac et par l’issue dou bouel, si est li color de l’aposteme semblans a la color dou cors, et est legiere chose sens dolor, et apert de diverse issue.	and if it is from the routing of the ulcer and from the exit of the bowels, then the color of the abscess is similar to the color of the body, and it is a slight thing without pain, and it opens with diverse exits.
Et se c’est por l’issue de l’intestine, adonques est il plus divers, et quant on le presse a ses dois si se repont, et puis revient, et par aventure si est sarrez, et agrandist mout a l’entree dou bain et por fort travail.	And if it is through the outlet of the intestine, then it is more diverse, and when one presses it with their fingers, it recoils, and then returns, and sometimes it becomes serrated, and grows larger at the entrance of the bath and from great exertion.
Et se c’est por moistor, c’est legiere chose, et apert bien quant tu le presses a ta main, ne ne constraint mie;	If it is due to moisture, it is a minor matter, and it becomes apparent when you press it with your hand, and it does not restrict movement.
et se c’est por sanc, si apert par ces signes li apostemes gros et dur, et est fichiez selonc une quantiteit;	and if it is due to blood, it is indicated by large, hard abscesses, and it is fixed according to a certain quantity;
et se c’est por ventositeit, si est souef au tochier, et li ovraiges si est que tu regarde se li apparance est por le sanc de l’artere, ou de la voine, ou ventositeit.	and if it is due to wind, there will be swelling upon touch, and the actions will indicate whether it is due to arterial or venous blood, or wind.
Si covient que tu laisses la cure.	Let the wound heal.
Car il en a doutance et paor, si com je t’ai dit ou chapistre des apostemes, por l’artere et por la voine.	For there is doubt and fear, as I told you in the chapter on abscesses, because of the artery and vein.
Et se li apparance est por l’intestine ou lou boueil, si covient que tu comandes au malaide qu’il teigne son alaine, et soit estendus tout drois, puis seigne d’enche tout entor la boude;	And if the appearance is due to the intestines or bowels, then you must instruct the patient to tighten his abdomen and extend it straight, then sign all around the navel;
puis le comande a gesir sovin entre tes mains, puis va entor le leu que tu as signiet a tout le spatumile, puis estent la moitiet de l’aposteme au desus a tout le grant uncine;	then command him to lie down quickly between your hands, then go around the area you have signed all around the navel, then bring half of the abscess up to the top, all along the great toenail;
puis le lie entor d’un fil fort, ou d’une corde de fort soie fermement, et soit li nous dou liien assolz;	then tightly wind it with a strong thread or a firm silk cord, and let us tie it firmly.
puis oevre la moitiet de l’aposteme estendut sus le liien, et i boute ton doit indice, et quier l’intestine;	then cut the abscess open halfway along its length over the ligature, and push your finger inside, and seek out the intestine;
se tu le trueves pris dou liien, si le deslie, et boute l’intestine au defuer dou ventre;	if you find it caught on the ligature, then release it and pull the intestine outside the abdomen;
et se tu trueves le boueil, si le prent a l’oncine, et en cope la superfluiteit;	and if you find a lump, then cut it off at its base and remove the excess;
et se li artere te fait contraire, ou li voine, si vai belement entor, puis revien a ton ovraige et pren II aguilles, et i boute II fors filz, et boute les II aguilles entor ceu que tu as fait en crois que tu feis percier;	and if the artery or vein opposes you, go around it smoothly, then return to your task and take two needles, thread them with strong thread, and pierce through what you have done in a cross shape;
puis estrain l’aposteme en IIII leus sus les aguilles, et se tu vues, oste les aguilles, et laisse lou leu tant qu’il porrisse, et chiece li char morte par soi;	then draw the abscess out in three places over the needles, and if you see, remove the needles, and leave it open so that it may drain on its own;
ou tu la cope quant elle iert subtiliie et porrie, puis le cure de ceu qu’il covient, et cheve l’aposteme si com nos avons dit;	or you cup it when it is subtle and porous, then the cure of what is appropriate, and drain the abscess as we have said;
et estrai le sanc ou la moistor que tu trueves, puis cure le leu de ceu qu’il couvient, et soude le leu.	and extract the blood or moisture that you find, then cure the area as is appropriate, and close up the wound.
dou chancre	from cancer
Nos avons dit en la division les semblances de chancre, et coment on i doit ovrer par medicines, et coment on doit eschuer la cure de fer;	We have already discussed the types of sores and how to treat them with medicine, as well as how to avoid using iron in the treatment.
et disons le chancre enjanreit en la marris, et grant cautele a en la cure, et dirent li ancien que quant chancres est en leu ou on le puet raier si com chancre qui est em mameles, et en la cuixe, et en semblans leus, et le doit tout oster quant il est en l’encomencement;	and we shall speak of the sore in ulcers, and the great care that must be taken in treating them, and the ancient writers say that when a sore is in a place where it can be scratched, like a sore on breasts, or thighs, or similar places, and it must all be removed when it is in its early stages;
et quant il est grans et anciens, si ne covient mie que tu l’aproches, car je n’en poi onques nul saner;	and when they are large and old, you must not touch them, for I cannot heal any of them.
ne nulz n’en sana onques devant moi.	I have never seen anyone heal from this.
Et li ovraiges, quant il est en leu ou on le puet oster, si com nos avons dit, est que tu purge aucune fois le malaide de cole noire;	And the treatment, when it is in a place where it can be removed, as we have said, is that you sometimes purge the patient of black bile;
puis le fai sainier s’il ait manifeste repletion, puis afaite le malaide I boin leu por faire l’ovraige;	then let him bleed if he has a manifest fullness, then bind up the wound in a good place to perform the operation;
puis giete tes oncines ou chancre, et le cheve de toutes pars, et l’oste de toutes pars sens rien laissier;	then cut your onions or garlic, and shave the head all over, and remove the bones without leaving anything behind;
et laisse corre le sanc tout fuer, et espreint bien le leu a ta main ou a aucune chose, et se li decorremens de sanc te fait contraire de l’incision de l’artere ou de la voine, si le cauterize tant que li sans soit estainchiez;	and let the blood flow out freely, and squeeze the wound with your hand or something else, and if the blood flow is contrary to the incision of the artery or vein, then cauterize it until the bleeding stops;
puis le cure d’autre cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	then heal the wound with another healing until it is healed.
de ydropisie	of dropsy
Nos avons jai dit en la division les semblances d’idropisie, et en queil maniere li assemblee de l’aigue est faite, et les signes de chescune semblance, et la cure qui est faite par medicines, et cele qui est curee par fer:	We have already said in the section on dropsy the similarities and how the accumulation of fluid is made, and the signs of each similarity, and the treatment which is made with medicine, and that which is treated with iron:
si est eclites soulement;	if they are only dislocated;
et ne doit on touchier de fer en ces II semblances:	and one must not touch with iron in these two cases:
c’est a savoir, tympanites et yposarche, car c’est mortelz chose;	that is to say, tympany and iposarchy, for it is a deadly thing;
donques quant tu medicines ceste semblance de ydropisie qui est apelee «eclites» de medicines, et li cure ne profite, si regarde se li malaides est foibles, ou s’il ait autre maladie que ydropisie, si com toust et solution de ventre et semblans choses;	therefore when you treat this condition of dropsy which is called "dislocation" in medicine, and the treatment does not help, then consider whether the patient is weak, or has another illness than dropsy, such as a fever and similar things;
si n’i touchier de fer, car il i a doutance;	do not touch with iron, for there is doubt in it;
et se tu vois le malaide de fort vertut, et il n’a autre maladie que ydropisie soulement, et il n’est mie trop jones ne trop vielz, si dois ensi ovrer:	and if you see the patient is very strong, and has no other illness but dropsy alone, and is not too young or too old, then you must work thus:
lieve le malaide droit sus tes mains, et li ministres presse le ventre em boutant l’aigue a la plus basse partie dou pis, puis pren le spatumile espinous selonc ceste forme:	let the patient lie on his back in your arms, and press his belly down by pushing out the water to the lowest part of the penis, then take the spatula according to this form:
Et soit trenchans de II pars.	And make an incision of 2 parts.
a pointe, et toutevoie ne soit mie si entrans qu’il puist venir jusc’a l’intestine quant on le fiche ens, et ne le puist blecier;	to a point, and yet not so sharp that it can penetrate to the intestines when pushed in, nor can it pierce the skin.
puis regarde se li ydropisie est enjanree devers les intestines:	then look to see if the dropsy is pressing on the intestines:
si covient que tu fendes ensus de la boude III dois droit desoz sus lou poignil;	you should split open under the armpit;
et se li ydropisie est por la maladie dou foie, si soit ta fendure au senestre de la boude III dois;	and if the dropsy is due to a liver ailment, then your split should be on the left side of the armpit;
et se c’est por la miuce, si soit a destre, et ne covient mie que li malaides gise sus la fendure que les superfluitez ne corrent a celui foible leu;	and if it's due to a kidney ailment, then it should be on the right, and the patient should not lie on the split so that the excess fluids do not flow to that weak spot;
puis perce tout le cuir a l’estrument, et le boute, et lieve ta main a tout le spatumile entre le cuir et le syfac ausi com en escorchant a la quantiteit d’une ungle ou enqui entor;	then pierce the skin with your instrument, and stab it, and lift your hand to the entire area between the skin and the syringe as if you were skinning in the amount of a fingernail or more;
puis perce lou syfac tant que li spatumile viegne au leu vuit, et c’est li leus de l’aigue, puis le trai fuer, et i boute cest estrument de coi ci est li forme:	then pierce the syphilis until the pus comes to the surface, and that is the place of the water, then pull it out, and insert this instrument from which there is the form:
Et est semblans a une caine d’argent subtil, et est d’arain ou d’archaut legier, et a en la partie desoz I petit pertus;	And it is similar to a thin silver needle, and it is made of lightweight copper or brass, and has at the bottom a small hole:
et ou costeit d’une part, III pertus;	and on one side there are three holes;
et II d’autre part, et I d’autre;	and two on the other, and one elsewhere;
et est li chiés tailliez si com une penne, et c’est li forme de l’incision dont li escrivains taille la penne:	and the head is shaped like a feather, and that is the shape of the incision that scribes make in feathers:
au chief desus est li alemele, si que quant li estrumens vient a l’aigue, si dessent maintenant sus l’estrument;	at the top there is an eyelet, so that when the instrument reaches the water, it is pulled up through the eyelet;
vuide la donques la moitiet ou la tierce part, car se tu en vuides plus qu’il ne covient en celle houre, par aventure si muert li malaides por la resolution de son esperit de l’arme, ou il chiet paumez, ou il aproche a la mort;	therefore empty half or a third of it, because if you empty more than is appropriate in that hour, the patient might die from the loss of vital fluids, or he will faint, or he will approach death.
mais en vuide selonc la quantiteit de sa vertut, et selonc ceu que les dispositions de la vertut dou malaide signifient, et ses poulz;	but empty according to the quantity of its virtue, and according to what the dispositions of the virtue of the disease signify, and his pulses;
puis trai l’estrument et retien l’aigue, et elle est retenue maintenant por le keur qui estoupe le pertus qui est sus le syfac, de coi j’ai parleit, que tu perces selonc ceste maniere;	then treat the instrument and retain the water, which is now retained by the membrane that blocks the aperture above the sciatic nerve, about which I have spoken, piercing it according to this method:
puis rencomence l’estrument l’autre jor, se tu vois le malaide soffrant ceu, et trai de l’aigue une petite quantiteit;	then resume the instrument the next day if you see that the patient is suffering from it, and treat a small amount of water;
fai ce aucun jor, et te garde de foloier tant qu’il ni demore mais c’un poc d’aigue.	do this for a few days, and be careful not to follow until there is no more water left but a little bit.
Et se tu doutes sus le malaide, et tu i lais mout d’aigue, si le cure de la sepulture ou sablon chaut, et par mout sueir ou bain et au soleil, et se teigne de boivre;	And if you doubt the disease, and leave a lot of water, then treat with hot sand or ash, and much sweating in a bath, and tanning, and drinking;
et le cure de medicines desiccatives tant qu’il soit sanez, et cauterize sus l’estomac et sus lou foie et sus l’esplen aprés l’estraction de l’aigue, si com j’ai dit devant.	and treat with drying medicines until he is healed, and cauterize the stomach and liver and spleen after extracting the pus, as I said before.
de l’estopement de la verge	of the penis
Aucune fois naissent enfant qui n’ont point de pertus en la verge, ou li pertus est petis, ou il n’est mie en son leu.	Sometimes children are born without a foreskin, or with a small foreskin, or it is not in its place.
Si le covient tantost qu’il n’aist percier a tout I spatumile molt subtil selonc ceste forme:	If necessary, cut it with a very sharp knife according to this form:
puis met ou pertus I clo subtil de plonc, et le lie et le tien ensi III jors ou IIII et quant il vuet faire urine, si soit ostez li clos, et faice urine, et puis li remet;	Then put a subtle plug into the penis, and tie it and keep it like that for 3 or 4 days. And when he wants to urinate, remove the plug and urinate, then put it back in again.
et par aventure nen i couvient point, car li urine qui vient fuer ne lou laisse close.	And by chance, this may not be necessary, because the urine that comes out doesn't let it stay closed.
Cil de cui li pertus est petis, si est medicinez dou clo de plonc, si com nos avons dit, si s’eslargera.	Those with small wounds, if treated with a plaster of honey, as we have said, will broaden.
Cil qui n’ont mie le pertus en lor leu sont bleciet, car aucun naissent qui ont le pertus au chief de la verge, por coi il ne puient pissier avant s’il ne lievent lor verge en haut;	Those who don't have the opening in their place are blue, because some are born with the opening at the tip of the penis, which prevents them from urinating until they lift their penis upwards.
et ne pueent enjanrer por ceu que li matiere ne puet venir jusc’a la marris, et c’est une male maladie.	And they can't ejaculate because the fluid can't reach the glans, and this is a serious illness.
Et li maniere de l’ovraige si est que li malaides gise sovin sus son dos, puies estent le chief de la verge et le cope ausi com la taille d’une penne, si ke li pertus chiece em mileu, si com il covient;	And the way to do this is for the patient to lie on his back, then the tip of the penis and glans are cut to the size of a feather, so that the slit goes through the middle, as it should be.
et te garde de decorrement de sanc qui i vient maintes fois, et s’il avient, si l’estainche de ceu qui estainche sanc, et cure la plaie tant qu’il soit sanez.	and beware of bleeding which often occurs, and if it does, then stanch the bleeding with something that stanches blood, and treat the wound until it is healed.
des pustules de la verge	of the penis
Maintes fois vienent cist albathe en la verge, et est une apparance de char laide;	Many times this hernia occurs in the penis, and it has an ugly appearance;
et en i a malignes et non malignes;	and there are both malignant and non-malignant types;
si covient que tu les preignes a I oncine subtil, et les cope et munde toutes, puis met sus coton moilliet en oignement egiptien;	so you should grasp them with tweezers very gently, pull them out and clean the area thoroughly, then place wet cotton wool soaked in Egyptian ointment over it.
puis le cure d’oignement diafinicon tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then treat it with diafinicon ointment until it is healed.
Et se li albathe est maligne, de pute color et depuant, si covient que tu i amenistres cautere.	And if the ulcer is malignant, discolored and putrid, then you must apply cautery.
Quant tu l’as copeit, et se li albathe est en som la verge, et en ait partie dedens la peil et partie defuer, si covient que tu oste l’albathe qui est dedens premier;	When you have cut it, and if the wound is on the shaft, and part of it is inside the skin and part outside, then you must first remove the foreign object that is inside.
et quant il est soudez, si le cure defuer.	And when it is sewn up, the patient can be discharged.
Car quant tu le cures ensamble, si n’est mie asseurez li chiez de la verge qu’il ne soit perciez, et vient noiror et corruption en son la verge et ou coion;	For when you treat it together, there is the risk that the head of the shaft is not healed and it becomes perforated, causing blackness and corruption in the shaft and in the scrotum.
si covient chever tout ceu qui est noir et corrumput, puis lie sus l’emplaustre de miel et de farine qui soit fait d’escorce de poumes grenates et de veces, puis le cure d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez.	So you must cut away all that is black and corrupted, then apply an ointment made of honey and flour from pomegranate rind and poppies, and then treat it with other remedies until it is healed.
Et se decorremens de sanc vient, si amenistre le cautere lunaire selonc ceste forme:	And if there is a bleeding, apply the lunar cautery according to this form:
Li cauteres si aide as II dispositions ensamble:	There are two ways to perform cautery:the first is when the wound is old and the skin around it is hard, which
c’est asavoir, au decorrement de sanc, et a la corruption;	that is, in the case of bleeding and corruption.And the second is when the wound is new and the skin around it is soft, which is as follows:
et se li chiés de la verge est corrumpus et retrais, si covient que tu boutes ou conduit de la verge une cainne de plonc, et pisse li malaides parmi;	and if the head of the penis is corrupted and withdrawn, then you should pierce or insert a cane of reed into the penis, and the patient should urinate through it.
et quant li pelz iert aerse au chief de la verge qui avient a ces qui n’ont mie esteit circoncis, ou il avient por plaie ou por aposteme, si covient donques que tu l’escorches a I estrument cheveit, tant que li liiens soit desliiez, et soit delivrez li chiez de la verge de toutes pars;	and when the foreskin is swollen at the head of the penis, which happens to those who have not been circumcised, whether due to a wound or an abscess, then you should cut it with a sharp instrument until the swelling is reduced and the head of the penis is relieved of pressure all around.
et se c’est grief chose de deviser ceu, si covient que tu l’escorches a I spatumile aucun poc dou chief de la verge et de la peil;	and if it is a serious matter to discuss this, then you should cut it with a spatulum on the head of the penis and the foreskin.
puis dessevre belement entre II, et i met I subtil drapeil de lin moilliet an aigue froide, qu’il n’aerse derechief.	Then clean gently between them, and place a thin, damp linen cloth in cold water on it so that it does not swell again.
de la circoncision	on circumcision
Circoncision n’est mie desliemens de continuation si com les autres plaies;	Circumcision is not a matter of dislocation like the other wounds;
toutevoie quant nos faison ceste oevre de nostre volenteit, et proprement as enfans, si est mestier que nos faisiens la millor oevre, et la plus legiere a salut.	Yet when we do this work of our own will, and properly with children, it is necessary that we make the best work, and the lightest for their salvation.
Je dis que li ancien ne dirent mie la circoncision de lor enfans, car il n’en usent mie en lor loi, et n’en avons mais que ceu que nos avons aquis par experiment.	I say that the ancients did not mention the circumcision of their children, because they did not use it in their law, and we have only what we have acquired through experimentation.
Car j’ai veut la plus grant partie des maistres et des sainors qui faisoient circumcision entor I dal, et as forces, et a tout une novacule;	For I have seen most of the masters and surgeons who made circumcision around the foreskin, and with force, and on every new born baby.
si fuioit li keurs car il i a II toiles, et par aventure si cope on celi desus et demore celle desoz.	If it is a hernia because there are two membranes, and by chance one is above and the other below remains.
Or la recovient coper, et est li dolor double, et a la mundification qui est dou dal n’est mie asseuree li pointe dou membre;	Now they cover it again, and the pain is doubled, and in the purification which is from the foreskin is not secure the tip of the member.
et a la mundification de l’ungle par aventure eschaipe li fer, et corront l’uevre, et maintes fois naissent ensi qu’il n’ont mestier de mundification et je l’ai veut.	And in the purification of the nail by chance escapes the iron, and they ruin the work, and many times are born so that they do not need purification, and I have seen it.
De la mondification qui est faite as forces a tout le liien de fil ai je troveit la bonteit de l’experiment, car les forces taillent justement ausi bien desus com desoz.	From the cleaning that is done on the scrotum, I have found the goodness of the experiment, for the testicles are cut justly above and below.
Car quant tu presses ta main, si tailles igalment en I tout soul tens;	For when you press your hand, you cut equally in a circle all around.
mais que li filz soit bien estrois entor lou cuir;	but that the son be well tied around the skin;
et soit li maniere dou premier ovraige si est que tu faices penser l’enfant, s’il entent, que tu ne li fais fuer que liier le fil entor la verge tant soulement, et pues le fai esjoir en toutes les manieres que tu pues;	and the method of the first work is that you make the child think, if he understands, that you only tie the thread around the penis, and then pull it in all the ways you can;
puis le fai ester entre tes mains tout droit, et repont les forces entre tes mains ou desoz tes piez que li enfes ne les voie, ne aucun des estrumens;	then hold him upright between your hands, and press down on his genitals with your hands or under your feet so that the child cannot see them, or any of the instruments;
puis boute ta main a la verge et souffle ou keur, et la trai en haut tant que li chiés de la verge soit ens;	then put your hand over the penis and blow or breathe on it, and pull it upwards so that the head of the penis goes in;
puis la mundifie bien de l’ordure qui i est assemblee, puis lie le leu signiet d’un fil double, puis la lie desoz I poc a I autre liien;	then cleanse it well from the dirt that has accumulated there, then tie the place with a double thread, then tie it under the testicles with another thread;
et la tien as II dois par la seconde lieeure au pouchet et au doit indice, et cope entre les II liiens, puis lieve le keur desus hastanment et trai le chief de la verge;	and hold it by the two fingers of the second hand at the scrotum and index finger, and squeeze between the two threads, then lift the head of the penis rapidly and pull the chief of the penis;
puis laisse corre le sanc poc et poc, car c’est li muedres;	then let the blood flow little by little, for it is the wound.
et met poudre sus et sus la poudre I drapeil glueit d’un moieuf d’uef cuit destempreit d’aigue rose, confit avec oile roset boin et fres, et lou laisse sus jusc’a l’autre jor, et le cure d’autre cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	and put powder on top of the powder and then cover with a bandage glued with an egg yolk cooked in rose water, infused with rosemary oil, and left until the next day, then treat it with another treatment until it is healed.
Li forme des forces a la mundification si est ceste:	The shape of the forces for purification is as follows:
li dui chiés soient tenves et soient trenchans, et soient li chiés ausi grant com li mainche igalment:	the two shoulders should be thin and sharp, and the hands should also be as large as the wrists evenly:
li error de la mundification si est quant li keurs dedens fuit a l’incision;	the mistake of purification is when the heart inside bleeds with the incision;
donques il covient que tu l’estendes a ton ungle, ainsois que li leus faice aposteme;	therefore, you must stretch it with your fingernail so that the flesh makes an abscess;
et le cope igalment, et se tu ne lou pues tenir a ton ungle, si le tien as tenailles, et puis le cope.	and cut it evenly, and if you cannot hold it with your fingernail, hold it with tweezers and then cut it.
Et s’il trespassent III jors, et ceu qui est desoz la verge est enflez, si le laisse tant que li apostemes chaus soit apaisiez, et l’escorche legierement;	And if they persist for three days, and what is underneath the skin is swollen, let it be until the abscess is drained and the skin slightly scarred.
si le cope si com tu pues mues, et te garde de la partie de la verge, ce ne li nuira niant.	then press on it as much as you can, but avoid the area of the penis, which will not be harmed by this.
Cure donques le leu de choses soudans plaie de poudre, que nos avons dit ou traitier des poudres, et s’on cope dou keur outre mesure, et il va au desus, si ne nuira point;	Then treat the area of the wound with a poultice, as we described in the treatise on powders. If they press on it too hard, and the swelling goes above, this will not cause any harm.
cure le donques, si com nos avons dit, tant qu’il soit sanez.	Treat it then as we have said until it is healed.
dou retenement de l’urine	from the retention of urine
Li retenue de l’urine si est d’opilation de piere, ou de sanc congeleit, ou de bowe, ou de char nee, ou de semblans choses, que nos avons dit en la division;	The obstruction of urine may be due to a stone, or frozen blood, or bowels, or dead flesh, or similar conditions which we have described in the division.
et se li urine n’est desliie , et tu vois estre la retenue por la piere qui est jai ou col de la vessie, si covient que li malaides soit corbés sus ses genoulz;	And if the urine is not flowing freely and you see that it is retained by a stone which is lodged in the throat of the bladder, then the patient should be made to bend his knees;
et li soient mis li piez sor le dos, et estende son ventre de la partie desus lou dos, et restraigne li malaides s’alainne tant com il puet;	and let his feet be placed on his back, and extend his belly from the upper part of his back, and restrain the patient's pain as much as he can.
et adonques est constrains li colz de la vessie a l’expression de la piere au desus, por coi li urine est desliie e;	and then the bladder is compressed for the extraction of stones from above, which causes the urine to flow out.
et s’elle ne vient, si com nos avons dit, et li malaides sent grant dolor, si covient que tu i aministres extraction a tout l’estrument qui est apelez «siringue», de coi ci est li forme:	And if it does not come out as we have said, and the patient feels great pain, then you must perform an extraction using a instrument called a "syringe," which has this form:
et soit d’argent subtilz legiere chevee, si com li penne d’un oiseil;	And it should be made of thin silver wire, like the feather of a bird;
et soit li caine d’une palme de lonc et demie, et soit subtilz au chief.	The cane should be about a palm and a half long, and thin at the end.
Et li maniere de l’issue de l’urine si est que tu pren I fil double, et lie au chief I poc de laine ou de couton, et boute le chief dou fil dedens la siringue;	And the way to extract the urine is as follows: take a doubled wire and attach a ball of wool or cotton at its end, then insert the end of the wire into the syringe.
et cope la superfluiteit de la lainne et le boute jusc’au chief de la siringue, puis oint la siringue d’oile ou de burre et d’aubin d’uef, et fai seoir le malaide sus I siege, et li arose la vessie et la verge d’oile moiste et d’oile d’olive et d’aigue tede;	and cut away the excess of the wool and plug it up to the tip of the syringe, then anoint the syringe with oil or lard and yolk of egg, and have the patient sit on a chair, and raise his bladder and penis with moist oil and olive oil and warm water;
puis met legierement la siringue en la verge, tant qu’elle viegne a la racine de la verge, puis double la verge desus devers la boude;	then gently insert the syringe into the penis, until it reaches the root of the penis, then fold the foreskin back over the glans;
puis boute la siringue avant jusc’a la vessie, et la sente li malaides venir jusc’a la chose vuide, et ceu n’est mie fait selonc cest ordre fuer que por ceu que li conduis ou elle vait est tors;	then fill the syringe up to the bladder, and feel the patient urinate until the bladder is empty, and this is not done according to this order unless the conductor where it goes is crooked;
puis estent le fil a tout la laine poc et poc, et li urine en suit la laine, puis l’estrai fuer, et fai corre l’urine;	then wind the thread around all the wool little by little, and the urine will follow the wool, then pull it out, and let the urine flow;
et rencomence la siringue tant que li vessie soit vuidie, et soit aligiez li malaides.	and restart the syringe until the bladder is emptied and the patient is relieved.
des maladies de la vessie	of diseases of the bladder
Quant escorcheures ou sanc vient en la vessie, ou porriture i est assemblee, et tu i vues distiller aigues et medicines, si fai a tout l’estrument qui est apellé «clepsedre», et c’est li forme:	When scabs or blood comes into the bladder, or pus is accumulated there, and you see it oozing out with water and medicine, then do everything using the instrument called "clepsydra", and that is its form:
Elle est close, et si a III pertus:	It is closed and has three openings:
II d’une part, et I d’autre, si com tu vois;	II on one side and I on the other, as you can see;
et li leus chevez par coi li medicine cort soit telz qu’il estoupe bien la verge sens adition, si c’on em puisse traire la moistor, et bouter quant mestier est;	and the small hole through which the medicine is applied should be such that it blocks the penis without addition, and one should be able to draw out moisture and insert when necessary;
et quant tu vues giter tes medicines en la vessie, met le chief dou keusteur en la moistor, et trai au traiant qui est ens;	and when you see your medicines entering the bladder, place the tip of the syringe in the moisture and draw it out through the opening;
si trairas la moistor au kesteur, et puis reboute fort le traiant ens;	you will draw out the moisture with the syringe, then quickly plug the hole;et si le chief dou keusteur est en la moistor, tu le tiens, et trais au traiant qui est ens.
si entrera li moistors ens, et venra a la vessie maintenant, si que li malaides la sentira;	if the tip of the syringe is in the moisture, hold it there and draw out through the opening. If the moisture enters now, the patient will feel it;
et c’est li forme dou clistere subtil dont on clisterize la vessie:	and this is the shape of the subtle catheter used to catheterize the bladder:
si est ci:	if it is here:
Et est d’argent ou d’archaut, et est li chiés plus haut;	And it is made of silver or bronze, and its head is higher;
et desoz a I sein ou li liiens chiet;	and below to the armpit where the lymph nodes are located;
puis pren une vessie de mouton et i met la moistor dont tu vues clisterizer la vessie, puis la lie entre les II seins forment d’un boin fil double, et chaufe I poc celle moistor sus le feu;	then take a sheep's bladder and put in it the moisture you see fitting for the blistering of the bladder, then tie it between the two breasts in the form of a loop made from a double thread, and heat that moisture over the fire;
puis boute le chief dou clistere en la verge, puis estrain ta main sus la vessie a tout la moistor avenanment, tant que li malaides sente que celle moistor est jai venue a la vessie;	then insert the tip of the blister into the penis, then squeeze your hand over the bladder gently, until the patient feels that the moisture has reached the bladder;
et se tu n’as la vessie, si pren une piece de parchemin, et en fai I cercle, et le perce rondement entor;	and if you don't have a bladder, take a piece of parchment and make it into a round, holey circle;
puis boute I fil fort en ces pertus, puis assemble le cercle si com on assemble I dal, et met dedens ceu que tu vues d’oile et de moistor et d’aigue, et le lie en l’estrument;	then thread a strong cord through these holes and assemble the circle like one assembles a wheel, and put inside what you want of oil, moisture, and water, and tie it in the instrument;
et fai si com tu as fait de la vessie, de presser a ta main tant que li moistor veigne a la vessie.	and do as you did with the bladder, squeezing it with your hand until the moisture comes out into the bladder.
de la piere	of stone
Nos avons jai dit en la division les manieres de piere, et l’estraction ensamble medicines;	We have already discussed in the division the methods of stone extraction, along with medicine;
et ai dit la difference entre la piere enjanree as rains, et toz les signes, et en queil piere on doit ovrer de taille;	and I have described the difference between a stone in the bladder and all the signs, and which type of stone one should operate on;
et en la vessie, et en la verge;	and in the bladder and penis;
et je le vos dirai apertement et briément.	and I will tell you plainly and briefly.
Je dis que li piere qui est enjanree en la vessie si avient plus sovent as enfans, et c’est signe que li aigue saut de la vessie semblans a aigue en sa subtiliteit;	I say that the stone which is lodged in the bladder happens more often to children, and it is a sign that the water flows from the bladder like water in its subtlety;
et i apert harene, et graite li malaides sa verge, et li pent maintes fois, et puis enroidist;	and he clearly sees, and feels pain in his penis, and he can urinate many times, and then it blocks up;
et a mout de ces saut li fondemens;	and has much of these discharges the fundament;
et est legiere li sanation des enfans jusqu’il ont IIII ans, et est mout grief en viellars, et est as jones moiene, a ces qui sont entre jonesce et viellece;	and healing is swift in children until they are four years old, and it is very slow in the elderly, and it is moderate in those between youth and old age;
et est li cure plus legiere de ces qui ont la piere grans, que de ces qui l’ont petite.	and the cure is easier for those who have large stones than for those who have small ones.
Et quant nos venons a la cure, si couvient premier mundifier le malaide per clistere, por traire tout le fiens qui est as intestines.	And when we come to the treatment, it is necessary first to cleanse the patient through an enema, to draw out all the feces that are in the intestines.
Car il encombre aucune fois a querir la piere.	For it sometimes blocks the search for stones.
Puis prenez le malaide par les piez, et lou deboutez et movez au desoz, si que li piere dessende au parfont de la vessie, et saille aucune fois dou leu haut;	Then take the patient by the feet and lift and move him so that the stone sinks to the bottom of the bladder, sometimes emerging from above.
puis le fai seoir entre tes mains appareilliet, et ses mains soient desoz ses cuisses, si que li vessie soit toute declinans aval;	Then have him sit in your lap, his hands under his thighs so that his bladder is completely tilted downward;
puis la quier et la touche dedens;	then probe and touch it inside;
se tu sens la piere en l’espaice, si te haste maintenant de taillier sus la piere.	If you feel the stone in the channel, then hurry to cut on the stone.Et s’il ne le sent pas dedens, si doit il demorer assiez ains qu’il ait grant desir; et tu te leves dedens li quier
Et s’elle ne chiet au touchier dou tout, si moille ton doi indice d’oile de la main senestre, se li malaides est enfes, ou ton doi moien, se li malaides est jovencelz acomplis;	And if it does not drop when touched, then the patient should remain sitting until he feels a great desire; and you lift up inside him the urethraIf it does not drop from the touch of the whole, then wet your index finger with oil from your left hand, if the patient is adult, or your middle finger, if the patient is a young man.
et le boute en son fondement, et quier la piere, et quant tu la sens a ton doi, si l’amoine au col de la vessie;	and press it into its socket, and seek out the stone, and when you feel it with your finger, then draw it towards the neck of the bladder;
puis presse sus a ton doi, et la boute au defuer lai ou tu vues taillier.	then press down on your finger, and put the stone back into its socket where you see the incision.
Et comande au ministre qu’il presse la vessie a sa main, et li comande qu’il estende a sa main destre les coions en haut, et a sa main senestre oste le cuir qui est desoz les coions en la partie ou on fait la taille;	And instruct the assistant to press the bladder with his hand, and tell the patient to extend his testicles upwards in his right hand, and with his left hand pull back the skin underneath the testicles in the area where the incision is made;
puis i boute le spatumile copant, de coi ce est li forme:	then put the spatulum in its proper place, for that is how it is formed:
Et fent entre ceu qui est entre les coions et le fondement, ne mie em mileu mais au costeit de la naige senestre;	And cut between what is between the testicles and the anus, not in the middle but on the left side of the navel;
et soit drois sus la piere, et tes dois soit adés ou fondement, et soit li taille dou traver si qu’ele soit large par defuer, et dedens estroite, selonc la quantiteit de la piere, ne mie trop grans;	and cut straight down to the stone, and your fingers should be pressed against the anus, and the incision should be made across so that it is wide at the top, and narrow inside, according to the size of the stone, not too large;
par aventure la presse si li dois qui est ou fondement, qu’elle saut fuer sens travail;	perchance the press so the testicles which are at the foundation, that they leap out without work;
et saiches qu’il i a teil piere ou il a angles, et marges:	and know that there is a certain stone in it with angles and margins:
si est griés a issir;	if it is grazed to come out;
et si a teil qui est souez, semblans a une glant, et reonde, dont li issue est legiere.	and if there is one underneath that resembles a grape, and round, whose exit is easy.
A celi donques ou il a angles et marge, fai la taille plus grant;	For those therefore with whom it has angles and margins, make the incision larger;
et s’elle ne saut, si covient que tu estraignes sus as tenailles qui sont ausi com une lime au chief, por mues estraindre la piere si qu’elle n’eschaipe;	and if it does not jump out, then you must hold the testicles steady with tweezers that are just like a file at their tip in order to squeeze out the stone so that it doesn't escape;
ou tu boute desoz li I estrument subtil corbé au chief;	or you insert under the instrument an extremely thin, curved hook;
et se tu ne la pues engignier ensi, si eslarge I poc lou pertus, et se li sans decort, si l’estrainche de vitriole;	and if you cannot grab it like this, then enlarge the opening and if the blood is exposed, then squeeze it with vitriol;
et s’il i a plus d’une piere, si boute premier la plus grant au col de la vessie, puis cope sus, puis le trai fuer, et les petites aprés s’il en i a plusors.	and if there is more than one stone, then plug the largest first at the neck of the bladder, then pour water on top, then pull it out, and the smaller ones afterwards if there are several.
Et s’elle est mout grans, si la covient soier, et faire plus grant plaie.	And if it is very large, then it needs to be sutured, and a larger wound made.
Car II choses avienent au malaide:	For two things happen to the patient:
ou il muert, ou li urine vient adés par lai que li leus ne puet souder;	either he dies, or the urine comes again through the opening where the urethra cannot heal;
mais toutevoie t’efforce dou traire, ou dou debrisier as tenailles, tant que tu la traies par pieces;	but nevertheless try to draw it out, or tear it with tweezers, until you have drawn it out in pieces;
et quant tu as acomplit ton oevre, si emple la plaie d’encens et d’aloe et de sanc de dragon, et l’estraint, et met par sus I drapeil moilliet en oile et en vin, ou en oile et en aigue rose et aigue froide, por apaisier l’aposteme chaut;	and when you have finished your work, apply the wound with incense and aloe and dragon's blood, and press it, and put over it a damp cloth soaked in oil and wine, or oil and rose water and cold water, to soothe the hot abscess;
puis resovine le malaide sus son col, et ne desliier lou lien jusc’au tier jor.	then re-catheterize the patient on his neck, and do not loosen the ligature until the third day.
Et quant tu le desliies, si arose mout bien lou leu d’oile et d’aigue, puis le cure d’oignement dyafinicon et d’oignement basilicon, tant qu’il soit sanez.	And when you loosen it, wash the site well with oil and water, then treat the wound with thin ointment and thick ointment until it is healed.
Et se apostemes chaus vient en la plaie et corrosions, et congelemens de sanc en la vessie, et soit par ceu retenue li urine, qui est conue en teil maniere que sans saut avec l’urine:	And if hot abscesses come upon the wound and scorchings, and blood clots in the bladder, and the urine is retained by this, which occurs in such a way that without salt with the urine:
boutes donques ton doi en la plaie, et estrai celui sanc, car s’il i remaint, si corront la vessie, et la porrit;	therefore you should place your finger into the wound, and draw out that blood, for if it remains, it will corrupt the bladder, and burst it;
puis leve la plaie d’aigue et d’aisil et de seil, et li aide en toutes les manieres que tu seis, tant qu’il soit sanez;	then open the wound with water and vinegar and salt, and help him in every way you know until he is healed;
et covient que toutes les oures que tu le cures, que tu li lie les II cuisses, et assemble les medicines sus le leu.	and you should bind his two thighs together with medicine on the wound every hour that you treat him.
Et se li piere est petite, et ele est ou conduit de la verge, et fichie ens, et li urine ne puet issir;	And if the stone is small, and it is in the ureter, and lodged there, and the urine cannot pass through;
si le cure de ceu que je dis ainsois, que tu lou tailles maintes fois, est on escusez de la taille per ceste cure.	if this treatment that I say is done several times, it is an excuse for the cutting, because of this treatment.Et si li piere sont grans et ne puent issir, mais sont en leu ou li urine se retint;
Je ai ja ce proveit ensi.	I have tried this myself.
Pren .i. foret de fer selonc ceste forme et soit a .iij. angles fichiees en .i. tison:	Take a piece of iron according to this shape and let it be spiked at three angles on a poker:
puis pren I fil et lou lie entor la verge desoz la piere, si qu’ele ne puist venir arrier en la vessie;	then take thread and tie it around the end of the penis, so that it cannot go back into the bladder.
puis boute le foret en la verge legierement, tant qu’il viegne a la piere;	then pierce the foreskin lightly with an awl, until it reaches the glans;
et torne le foret a ta main en la piere poc et poc, tant que tu puisses percier la piere d’autre part;	and turn the awl in your hand in the penis little by little, until you can pierce the glans from another side;
si venra tantost li urine, puis presse ta main sus ceu qui est demorez de la piere qui est dedens la verge.	then the urine will flow, and then press your hand on what is left of the stone which is inside the penis.
Si est tantost brisie, et saut fuer avec l’urine, et est garis li malaides;	It will be broken at once, and will come out with the urine, and the patient is cured;
et se tu ne pues ce faire por aucune chose qui le deffent, si lie I fil desoz la piere et I autre desus, puis fent la verge endroit la piere entre les II liiens, puis l’estrai fuer, et deslie lou liien, et mundifie lou sanc congeleit qui est en la plaie;	and if you cannot do this for any reason that impedes it, then tie a thread under the glans and another one above, then make an incision in the penis between the two threads, then pull it out, and untie the thread, and cleanse the congealed blood that is in the wound;
et le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	and let them grow until they are healthy.
de la piere des femmes	of women's stones
Poc avient que piere soit enjanree en femmes, et s’il avient aucune fois, si est li cure grief, et est deffendut por III choses:	It sometimes happens that stones are lodged in women's wombs, and if it does, the cure is difficult and prohibited for three reasons:
l’une est que per aventure li femme est vierge;	one is that the woman may be a virgin;
et li seconde est c’on ne puet trover femme bien saichant qui se descuevre as mires, meismement quant elle est caste.	and the second is that one cannot find a woman who is skilled enough to examine her, especially if she is chaste.
Et li tierce maniere si est que par aventure on ne puet trover femme bien saichant en cest art de mains;	And the third reason is that perhaps one cannot find a skilled woman skilled in this manual art;
et li quarte maniere si est que li piere de la femme si est plus em parfont que li piere de l’ome, por coi il i couvient faire plus parfonde taille, et grant paour i a. Et se necessitez semont a ceu, si covient que tu preignes une mieresse bien sachant, et a poines la trueve on, et se tu n’en trueves, point si quier I caste mire subtil;	and the fourth reason is that the woman's stone is often deeper than a man's, so it requires a deeper incision, and there is great fear involved. If necessity demands it, then you should press a skilled midwife, and with difficulty you will find one, and if you do not find one, then seek out a subtle, clever castor.
et li presente une baile bien saige en la vie des femmes, ou une femme qui saiche une partie de l’art, et li comande qu’ele faice ceu que tu li comandes de l’inquisicion de la piere;	and present to her a very wise dance in the life of women, or a woman who knows part of the art, and command her to do what you command of the inquiry into the stone;
et regarde mout bien se li femme est vierge:	and look very carefully if the woman is a virgin:
adonques li covient bouter son doit ou fondement et querir la piere;	then she must push her finger into her vagina and search for the stone;
et s’ele la trueve, si la constraigne desoz son doit, et li recomande qu’elle boute son doit ou con la malaide, et quiere et presse sa main senestre sus la vessie forment.	and if she finds it, she should press it under her finger, and he should command her to push her finger into the wound and squeeze and press her left hand firmly on the bladder.
S’elle la trueve, si covient qu’elle la mueve de greit en greit des l’entree de la vessie jusque desoz, tant qu’elle viegne a la racine de la cuisse;	If she finds it, then she should move it gradually from the entrance of the bladder until it comes to the root of the thigh;
puis cope sus la piere en la racine de la cuisse encontre le mileu dou con, lai ou il est mues apparilliet, et sent la piere en celle partie;	then she should press on the stone in the root of the thigh against the middle of the urethra, the place where it is located; then she will feel the stone in that part;
et ne mueve son doi desus la piere ou desoz, et soit li taille au premier petite;	and do not move his bowels above or below, and let the incision be small at first;
puis boute lou rait en la taille, se tu sens la piere si acroi la plaie tant que li piere puisse issir fuer, et saiches que maintes manieres de pieres sont:	then pour in wine into the incision if you feel that the stone is as sharp as the wound so that the stone can come out, and know that there are many kinds of stones;
c’est a savoir, petites et grans et aspres et souez, longes et reondes, et qui ont rains.	that is to say, small and large, rough and smooth, long and round, and which have many variations.
si saiches les semblances por savoir l’issue.	And if you know their appearances to identify the exit.
Et se li sans te vaint, si met au leu vitriole broiet, et li tien une houre tant que li sans soit estainchiez;	And if the blood flows, put crushed vitriol in its place, and hold it there for an hour until the bleeding stops;
puis revien a ton ovraige, tant que li piere soit fuer, et aies des estrumens que je t’ai dit en l’estraction de la piere as homes por toi aidier en ton oevre;	then return to your work until the stone is out, and have the instruments that I told you about for extracting stones in men to assist you in your task;
et se li sans te vaint, et c’est de l’artere qui est copee, si met la poudre sus le leu et l’estrain de tentes et de bendelz, et ne rencomencier plus ceu, et laisse la piere et ne la traire mie, que par aventure morroit li malaide;	and if the blood flows and it is from the artery that has been cut, put the powder on the spot and hold it in place with bandages and splints, and do not touch it again, and leave the stone and do not pull at it, or the patient might die;
puis cure la plaie.	then treat the wound.
Et quant li chalor dou sanc est apaisie, et li leus porrist, si revien a ton ovraige, tant que li piere soit fuer.	And when the heat of the blood has subsided and the swelling has gone down, return to your work until the stone is out.
de hernie carnouse	of flesh hernia
Ramice aquouse n’est autre chose que assemblee de moistor ou blanc syfac, qui est desoz lou keur des coions, que contient l’uef;	Ramice aquose is nothing other than an assembly of moisture or white pus, which is under the skin of the testicles that contains the egg;
et est apelez «syfac», et aucune fois est proprement en la toile de l’uef, si c’on cuide que ce soit I autre oef;	and is called "syfac", and sometimes it is properly in the membrane of the egg if one believes that it is another egg;
et c’est li cuir dou coion entre lou blanc syfac que nos avons dit;	and it is the skin of the testicle between the white pus which we have mentioned;
et ceu n’avient se poc non.	and that does not happen by itself.
Et li generation de cest ramice si est de foibleteit que vient as coions, et est espandue celle matiere.	And the generation of this disease is due to weakness that comes from the testicles, and this matter is spread out.
Et aucune fois si vient de percussion sus les coions, et ceste moistor si a maintes colors:	And sometimes it comes from a blow to the testicles, and this moisture has many colours:
ou c’est color declinans a jaunice, ou c’est sans rouge, ou noir, ou aquous blans, et ce avient plus;	or it is yellow-tinged, or white, or black, or water-white, and there are more variations;et ceste moistor, s’el est de color declinant a jaunice, si vient de malancolie, ou de sang mist en la veine, et ceste moistor ne doit estre curée:
et ce sont li signe de conoistre ceste assemblee, car s’elle est ou blanc syfac que nos avons dit, si est li apostemes reons, I poc lonc si com li figure d’un oef, et n’apert mie li coions, car il a moistor tout entor.	and the signs to recognize this assembly are that if it is in the white pus which we have mentioned, then it is an abscess, a little longer than an egg, and does not open the testicle, because there is moisture all around it.
Et s’il a moistor en la propre toile, si est li apostemes reons avec une partie de l’uef, et por ceu pense on que c’est uns autres oef;	And if there is moisture in its own webbing, then abscesses are formed with an egg-sized portion, and because of this, one thinks it is another egg.
et se li moistor est entre le cuir des coions et le blanc syfac, si le sent om bien;	and if the moisture is between the skin of the testicles and the white scrotum, then he feels good;
donques quant tu vues savoir la color de la moistor, si esprueve a tout l’intromissoire quarreit, de coi li forme est ci devant.	therefore, when you want to know the color of the moisture, test throughout the entire scrotum, from which the form is as follows.
Selonc ceu donques qui vient aprés l’intromissoire, juge de ceu qui est dedens.	According to this, then, which comes after the instrument, judge what is inside.
Et quant nos la curons par fer, si covient que li malaides soit sainiez selonc som pooir et la repletion de son cors;	And when we treat it with iron, then the patient should be healed according to his strength and the fullness of his body;
puis le sovine sus son dos, sus une chose un poc haute, et met desoz lui mout de drapelz;	then lie on his back, on something slightly elevated, and put under him a lot of blankets;
puis sié sus sa senestre, et comande au ministre qu’il sié a destre, et estende la verge a l’un des II costelz dou keur des coions;	then sit on his left, and instruct the assistant to sit on the right, and extend the scrotum towards one of the two ribs near the heart of the testicles;
puis pren le spatumile leit, et cope le cuir des coions parmi leu dou lonc jusque delez lou poignil, et soit ta fendure toute droite en devisant le cuir des coions jusc’a syfac blanc, et l’escorche subtilment selonc tom pooir;	then take the spatule of lead, and cut into the skin of the testicles from their end to the root, and make your incision straight while separating the skin of the testicles up to the white scrotum, and carefully peel it according to your ability.
puis perce lou syfac plain d’aigue a I large pertus, et estrai toute l’aigue, et puis met tes oncines, et estent lou syfac amont;	then pierce the scrotum with a large hole, and draw out all the water, and then insert your fingers, and lift up the scrotum.
et ne touchier le keur des coions, mais que le syfac soulement;	and do not touch the heart of the testicles but only the scrotum;
cope tout ou par pieces meismement le costeit de lui subtil, que se tu ne le copes bien saigement, si revenra li aigue;	cut into it all around carefully and in sections, especially the edges of it subtly, for if you do not cut well enough to draw blood, then the water will return.
et se l’uef saut fuer a ton oevre, si le ramoinne en son leu quant tu avras acomplit l’uevre dou syfac;	and if the testicle jumped out of place during your work, then put it back into its place when you have finished working on the scrotum.
puis assemble les II leivres dou keur des coions a une costure, puis le cure si com les autres plaies, tant qu’il soit sanez.	then sew up the two lips of the cut with one stitch, then treat it as you would any other wound until it is healed.
Et se tu trueves l’uef corromput d’autre maladie, si covient que tu lies les vasselz que sont suspensoire, en doutant le decorrement de sanc;	And if you find the egg corrupted by another disease, then you must tie off the suspended vessels to prevent the flow of blood.
puis cope le coion a tout le suspensoire, et estrai l’uef, et le cure si com nos avons dit.	Then cut the scrotum all the way around the suspendory ligament, extract the testicle, and treat it as we have described.
Et se aigue est assemblee en II parties ensamble, saiches que ce sont II ramices;	If the wound is divided into two parts, know that these are two testicles;
si cope l’autre partie si com tu as fait la premiere igalment, puis essue lou sanc, et met en la plaie lainne moillie en oile roset;	cut the other part in the same way, then wipe away the blood and put soft lamb's wool soaked in rose oil into the wound;
et met defuer autre laine moillie en vin et en oile, et met sus les II coions, et met desus drapelz doublés, et le lie sus a tout le liien qui est selonc ceste forme:	and put on another layer of lamb's wool soaked in wine and oil, and place it over the testicles, and put on doubled linen, and tie it all around according to this form:
Puis pren II drapelz, et les emple de laine charpie selonc ceste semblance et soient assemblez par cousture en la gorle des braies, et li uns des chiés preigne sus le fondement jusc’au dos, et li autres a la partie dou poignil;	Take two pieces of cloth and fill them with wool wadding according to this appearance and sew them together at the crotch of the breeches, and let one piece hang over the buttocks to the back, and the other to the part of the groin.
et li autre dui chief sus les II angres, et soit toute assemblee li restreinture en la boucle dou braier;	and let the other two ends hang over the two hips, and let the whole girdle be tied in a knot at the loop of the breeches;
et aucune fois est medicinee ceste ramice de cautere en leu de taille de fer, et est que tu preignes I cautere cultellaire subtil, et cope le cuir des coions, et soit eschaufez si com nos avons dit, si que li syfac blanc que contient l’aigue est descovers;	and sometimes this ramice is used as a cautery instead of an iron knife, and you must grasp the thin cautery with tongs, and cut through the skin of the testicles, and it will be heated as we have said, so that the white pus contained in the fluid is exposed;
si pren lou cautere selonc ceste forme, et perce celui syfac as oncines, et l’escorche a cest subtil cautere chaut:	take the cautery according to this shape, and pierce that testicle gently, and scorch it with this thin hot cautery:
Et lou cope en toutes les manieres que tu pues, tant que tu esraiches tout;	And cut in every way you can, until you have cut out everything.
et garde que li feus ne touche l’uef;	and be careful that the fire does not touch the egg;
et saiches que ceste oevre est plus salve;	and know that this work is safer;
et mues gardans de decorrement de sanc, et muedres que li ovraiges de taille;	and avoid bloodletting and cutting wounds;
et se nulle chose te fait contraire, ou aposteme chaus ou decorremens de sanc ou autre chose, si cure ce qui te fait contraire, selonc ceu qui est devant dit.	And if anything goes against you, such as an abscess, bleeding, or anything else, then treat what goes against you according to what is said above.
Et se li malaides est paourous, et ne vuet atendre cest ovraige por son horribleteit, si amenistre perforation, si com je te di, et est que quant tu es bien certains par les significations que nos avons dit que ramice aquouse est lai, si fai seoir le malaide sus I siege leveit;	And if the patient is fearful and does not want to undergo this procedure due to its horrible appearance, then perform a puncture, as I have told you, and when you are certain through the signs we have discussed that the watery fluid is gone, then have the patient sit on a raised seat;
pues perce l’aposteme an la partie desoz a tout le spatumile large, et met la perforation dou lonc dou cors;	then pierce the abscess at its lowest point all the way to the bottom of the body;
et soit larges li pertus, si que toute li aigue corre fuer;	and let the holes be wide so that all the water flows out
puis met coton sus le leu, et le lie, et laisse por corre le remenant de l’aigue, puis le cure tant que li plaie soit sanee;	then put cotton on the spot, and tie it, and leave it so that the rest of the water flows out, then treat the wound until it is healed.
et se li blainche toile ne laisse issir l’aigue en la bouche de la plaie, si covient que tu i boutes une penne ou l’estrument dont on trait l’aigue des ydropiques, de coi li forme est ci devant;	and if the white membrane does not let the water out through the mouth of the wound, then you must pierce it with a needle or instrument used to treat water in hydrophobia, as described earlier.
et eslarge I poc la plaie, et saiches que li aigue revient, et est assemblee aprés VI mois ou enqui entor, et quant elle est assemblee si com devant, et ensi passera li malaides ses jors.	and widen the wound, and know that the water will come out, and will gather again after six months or so, and when it is gathered as before, then the illness will pass its course.
de l’aposteme des coions	of the testicle abscess
Saiches que en la section de ceste ramice a paor em plusors dispositions, por coi il me semble que mues vaut c’on la laisse;	Know that in the cutting of this nerve there is fear in many ways, because of which I think it is better to leave it alone.
et je vos dirai l’ovraige et les semblances de l’aposteme.	And I will tell you the treatment and the appearance of the abscess.
Je dis donques que maint aposteme vienent ou cors, et meismement as coions;	I therefore say that many abscesses come about the body, and especially in the groin.
et c’est par mout de cas.	and this happens in many cases.
C’est a savoir par superfluiteit aigre et ague, qui est espandue as coions, ou de percussion;	This is to be understood as resulting from an excess of bitterness and ague, which is spread to the groin, or from a blow;
et est li color de l’aposteme selonc la color dou cors;	and the color of the abscess follows the color of the body;
et ne trueve point de dolor, et est aposteme grief;	and it causes no pain, and is a serious abscess;
et par aventure est uns apostemes griés paourous et pierous, et de fuxe color, et aucune fois vient de nout d’artere, ou d’enfleure de voine.	and sometimes there are dark, pus-filled abscesses, and others that are blood-red in color, and at times they originate from an artery, or from a vein swelling.
Quant c’est par nout d’artere, si est conus par la disposition d’aposteme chaut, quant tu la presses a tes dois;	When it is from an artery, it can be detected by the hot disposition of the abscess when you press on it with your fingers;
et ne covient mie que tu i touches.	and you must not touch it.
Cil qui est fais d’enfleure de voine est conus par sa disposition a l’expression dou touchement des dois, et puet om bien faire la taille sus ceste semblance, et sus les autres chars;	He who is made from the swelling of a vein is known by his reaction to the touch of your fingers, and anyone can properly make an incision on this sort of abscess, and on others like it;
et est que tu cope lou keur des coions, puis estent l’uef en haut, et le trai fuer dou blanc syfac, et delivre lou suspensoire de toutes pars de l’uef.	and you should cut the skin of the testicles, then the sac will be above, and the thread will come out from under the white membrane, and free the suspensory ligament from all parts of the sac.
