Se li uef est ja sodez avec ces chars nees, si covient donques que tu traies l’uef, et lou cope;	If the testicle is already swollen with these new growths, then you should cut the sac and tie it off;
et s’il est aers au syfac, ou en ceu qui est dedens les vasselz, si covient que tu delivre toute celle tenve, et la cope reondement.	and if it is herniated in the membrane, or in what is inside the vessels, then you should free that tendon and tie it off roundly.
Et se li naissance de la char est ou leu derrier, si covient que tu la copes toute, et estrai l’uef, si com nous avons dit.	And if the tumor is in the back, then you must cut it out entirely and extract the egg, as we have said.
Et quant tes ovraiges est acomplis, si emple la plaie de laine moillie en oile roset et en vin, puis le cure d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez.	And when your work is finished, then dress the wound with wool moistened in rose oil and wine, then apply other remedies until it is healed.Et quant tu as curé la plaie, si covient que li patient soit a l’ombrage et au repos, et qu’il s’alimente de boire et manger legier, et qu’il ait peu de dormance, si com il oult.
de l’aposteme des coions	of the testicle abscess
Cis est uns apostemes envoloupez d’un envoloupement semblant a I borjon, avec le mollifiement des coions, et se muet li malaides griement quant il vait;	This is a hernia wrapped in a wrapper similar to a cherry, with the softening of the testicles, and the patient suffers greatly when he walks;
et li cure de ceste maladie si est bien pres ausi paourouse com ceste ci devant, et toutevoie nos vos dirons l’ovraige de li, selonc ceu que li ancien firent.	and the treatment of this disease is just as fearful as the one above, and yet we will tell you about it according to what the ancients did.
Il covient que tu faices seoir lou malaide sus I siege aleveit, puis li boute le suspensoire des coions aval a tes dois, a tout le vasseil qui sont prochien a la verge, et les teigne li maistres, et les estende forment;	It is necessary that you make the patient sit on an elevated seat, then tie the suspenders of the testicles low to your fingers, to all the vessels that are near the penis, and press them firmly, and extend them strongly.
puis cope au spatumile trenchant large dou traver endroit les vasselz, tant qu’il soient descovert, et puis escorche de chescune part, si com nos avons dit en l’estraction des arteres qui sont en temples;	Then cut through the skin with a sharp, wide blade across the vessels, so that they are exposed, and then scrape on each side, as we have said in the extraction of the arteries which are in the temples;
puis i fiche une aguille ou il ait I fil double, et le lie au premier leu ou li vis est venue, et le lie derechief a l’autre chief;	Then he inserts a needle where the thread is doubled, and ties it at the first place where the vein appeared, and ties it directly to the other end.
puis les cope em mileu droitement, selonc la longesce dou cors, et en trai les moistors corrumpues;	Then he cuts them in the middle correctly, following the length of the body, and draws out the corrupted moisture;
puis cure la plaie si com les autres ou on enjanre bowe, si que aucun vassel chiecent que norrissent l’un des coions;	Then he treats the wound as in the others, that is, one testicle may hang down;
car par ceu n’i vient point de mal, et se a toz les vasselz vient vis, si covient traire les coions a tout les vasselz;	for there is no harm from this, and if it becomes visible in all the vessels, then one must milk the testicles through all the vessels;
si que li oes ne perde son norrissement por l’incision des vasselz, et sechent et ne se puient aidier.	so that the veins do not lose their color due to the incision of the vessels, and dry up and cannot help themselves.
de la routure dou syfac	from the root of the eye socket
Li avenemens de ceste ramice si est par la section que vient ou syfac, ou l’estension sus le ventre en la partie des angres, por coi li intestine dessendent de celle routure a l’un des coions;	The cause of this disorder is due to the incision that occurs in the sigmoid colon, or the extension over the abdomen in the area of the veins, causing the intestines to descend from that rupture to one of the testicles;
et ceste routure est ou dou syfac, ou de l’estension de li, et vienent ces II manieres de mout de causes:	and this rupture is in the sigmoid colon, or due to the extension of it, and these two types come from many causes:
ou de percussion, ou de saut, ou de braire, ou de levement de grief faix, et par semblans choses;	or from percussion, or jumping, or coughing, or lifting a heavy load, and from similar activities;and this happens through the sigmoid colon, or its extension, and these two types come from many causes:
et li signes quant c’est de l’estension dou syfac, si est qu’il avient poc et poc, en lonc tens, et ne vient mie soudainnement;	and the signs that it is due to the extension of the sigmoid colon are that it occurs little by little over a long time, and does not happen suddenly;and this happens through the sigmoid colon, or its extension, and these two types come from many causes:
et est li apostemes igalz jusque vers le parfont, por ceu que li syfac apresse l’intestine.	and the abscess is even all the way to the bottom, because the ulcer pushes on the intestine.
Et li signes est quant c’est de la section dou syfac, qu’elle fait venir a l’encomencement dolor soudaine, et est li apostemes divers apparans, desoz le cuir pres, et c’est por l’issue de l’intestine et le cors au defuer dou syfac.	And the signs are when it is a dissection of the shoulder, that it brings sudden pain at the beginning, and the abscesses are diverse appearances under the skin near the surface, and this is due to the output of the intestine and the body being pushed by the shoulder.
Et aucune fois dessent li cirbes avec l’intestine, et est retenus enqui, et fait grant dolor soffrir au malaide, meismement quant il est pressez.	And sometimes the nerves go with the intestine, and are retained inside, and cause great pain for the patient, especially when they are pressed.
Et en ces cures de fer a paor, por coi il s’en covient eschuir.	And in these cures of iron, one must fear, for which one must avoid it.
Et li maniere de l’ovraige si est que tu comande ou malaide qu’il ramoine l’intestine a sa main au dedens en la plaie, s’il i puet rentreir;	And the method of treatment is to have the patient push his intestine back into his abdomen with his hand through the wound, if he can reach it.
puis soit sovinez sus son col. entre tes mains, et lieve les cuixes;	then you should hold him by the neck between your hands and lift his hips;
puis estent le keur au desus, et cope tout le cuir des coions dou lonc;	then they are pressed down from above, and all the skin of the scrotum is cut away from the testicles;
puis boute dedens les leivres de la taille uncines selonc ceu que tu en as mestier por ovrir la plaie, et soit telz que li oes em puist issir;	then insert hooks into the wounds of the abdomen according to what is needed to open the wound, so that the intestines can come out;
puis escorche lou syfac que est desoz lou cuir des coions, tant que li blans syfac dur soit descovers de toutes pars;	then scrape away the ulcer under the skin of the scrotum until all of the hard, white ulcer is exposed on all sides;
puis boute ton doi indice en ceu qui enseut lou coion, en ceu qui est entre lou blanc syfac qui est desoz lou cuir de l’uef, et entre lou secont syfac, et depart ceu qui est derrier l’uef, et entre lou secont syfac;	then insert your index finger into what follows the testicle, in between the white ulcer under the skin of the scrotum and the second ulcer, and separate what is behind the testicle from the second ulcer;
et pues muef a la main destre dedens lou keur des coions, et estent lou blanc syfac en haut a ta main senestre, et lieve l’uef a tout lou syfac devers la taille;	and then move your right hand inside the heart of the testicles, and have the white soffac on top in your left hand, and lift the egg to the entire soffac towards the waist;
et comande au ministre qu’il estende l’uef en haut, et deslie ceu qui est aers derrier le liement;	and instruct the assistant to stretch the egg upwards and loosen what is air behind the string;
et quier a tes dois s’il a point de l’intestine envoloupeit ou blanc syfac dur, et se tu en trueves aucune chose, si le boute au ventre desoz;	and feel with your fingers if there is any intestine wrapped or hard white soffac, and if you find anything, push it into the belly below;
puis pren une aguille ou il ait I gros fil fait de X filz, et la boute en la derriere partie dou syfac, qui est aprés lou cuir des coions;	then take a needle with a thick thread made of six threads, and insert it into the back part of the soffac, which is after the skin of the testicles;et puis tire fortement l’aguille et le fil dedens, si que li intestin soit tirée derrier le syfac, et est le membre en sa place.
aprés la taille, puis cope les chiés qui apperent des filz, tant qu’il i ait IIII filz;	and then pull the needle and thread inside strongly so that the intestine is pulled behind the soffac, and the limb will be in its place.Afterwards, cut the shoulders which appear from the threads, so that there are four threads left;et puis quier si li chiés ne se remue pas
puis les assemble l’un sus l’autre en maniere de croix, et en lie lou syfac, dont nos avons dit qui est desoz lou cuir des coions, d’un fort liien de II pars;	then he ties them one on top of the other in the shape of a cross, and binds it with a strong thread made of two parts.
puis envoloupe les chiés des filz, et les lie forment de II pars, si que nuls des vasselz que les norrissent ne puissent entrer en ous, que aposteme chaus n’i viegne;	then he wraps the roots of the threads and binds them tightly from two parts, so that none of the vessels that nourish them can enter, so that no abscess forms;
et met derechief le liien selonc le premier liien lonc II dois de celui, et aprés ces II liiens laisse dou syfac qui est desoz lou keur des coions le grant d’un doi;	and ties the thread according to the first long thread in two parts, and after these two threads leaves the syringe which is under the skin of the scrotum with a large amount of one egg;
et aprés tout l’autre selonc la rondesce que li euf porte;	and then the other according to the roundness that the egg carries;
puis cope en la partie qui est desoz le cuir des coions, tant qui li sans corre, et li bowe, si com nos avons dit ci devant;	then cut into the part which is under the skin of the scrotum, so that the blood flows, and the bowels, as we have said before;
puis amenistre laine moillie en oile, et met em plaies, et i amenistre le liien que nos avons dit.	then apply wool moistened in oil, and place it on the wounds, and then the thread that we have mentioned.
Et aucune fois est cauterizez li blans syfac que nos avons dit, aprés l’incision, par doutance de decorrement de sanc.	And sometimes the white syphilis that we have mentioned is cauterized after the incision out of fear of bloodletting.
Car ce avient maintes fois, et laisse le liien tant qu’il chiece per lui;	For this happens many times, leaving the ligament intact as it tears through.
et s’il tarde au cheoir, si soit arosez d’aigue chaude, et met sus ceu que nos avons dit, tant qu’il chiece;	And if it doesn't drop quickly, use a hot water compress and apply what we have described until it does.
puis cure la plaie d’autre cure, tant qu’il soit sanez parfaitement.	Then treat the wound with another treatment until it is perfectly healed.
de hernie carnouse	of flesh hernia
En ceste ramice ne vis je onques nul qui osast faire la cure par fer.	In this section, I have never seen anyone dare to perform the cure with iron.
Et li ancien dirent qu’ele est faite si com li ramice qui est ensamble la vis, en teil maniere que tu lie les vasselz, aprés la taille sus ous legierement au desoz;	And the ancients say that it is made like the thread that binds the vessel, after cutting it slightly from above to below;
puis cope em mi, et cure l’aposteme de ceu qui oevre, tant que li vasselz chient;	then cut it in half, and treat the abscess with this, until the vessels are closed;
et le cure si com nos avons dit, tant qu’il soit sanez.	and treat it as we have said, until it is healed.
Aucune fois vient routure ens angres, si com nos avons dit, et apert li leus;	Sometimes, a rot comes in the gums, as we have said, and the place opens;
et ne dessent nulz des intestines as coions, et s’il en i dessent, c’est poc, et repaire toutes houres;	and none of the intestines come out as testicles, and if any do, it is rare, and they heal quickly;
et toutevoie s’il demoure trop en cest point, si croit li plaie ou syphac, tant que li intestine dessent;	and yet if it remains too long in this state, the wound or ulcer will increase in size as the intestines descend;
et ceu avient par l’estension dou syfac qui est as angres, si com nos avons dit, car il est estendus, puis est mollifiez et enflez li leus et apert;	and this happens because of the extension of the ulcer which is in the intestines, as we have said, for it is extended, then made soft and swollen, and open;
et li cure si est par cautere, si com nos avons devant dit;	and the treatment is by cautery, as we have previously said;
et aucune fois est curee par fer en ceste maniere:	and sometimes it is treated with iron in this way:
et est que li malaides gise sovin sus son dos entre tes mains, puis cope le leu de la routure enfleit dou large selonc la quantiteit de III dois;	and the patient should lie on his back between your hands, then apply a poultice of the powdered herb according to the size of a bean three times;
et puis estrai le syfac qui est desoz le cuir que l’ensuet, puis pren lou rait et lou met sor le leu apparant dou syfac;	then draw out the ulcer which is under the skin and take some of the juice and place it on the visible ulcer;
et lou presse au parfont dou ventre, puis cout les II leus apparans dou syfac sus lou chief dou rait, et cout l’un et l’autre;	and press it into the depth of the abdomen, then cut the two visible ulcers on the head of the juice, and cut both;
puis estrai le chief dou rait, et ne coper point dou syfac ne n’estendre l’uef n’autre chose, si com je t’ai fait savoir en la cure de la ramice des intestines;	then pull out the head of the bowel, and do not cover it with a bandage or extend it with anything else, as I have made you aware in the treatment of the rupture of the intestines;
puis le cure par la cure des plaies.	then treat it through the treatment of wounds.
Et quant tu copes les filz, si le mundefie et cure la plaie, tant qu’elle soit sanee.	And when you cut the threads, clean and treat the wound until it is healed.
Li syfac est constrains, et n’a point d’apparance en la routure, et li cauteres est muedres en cest leu, et plus prochiens a salut.	The ulcer is constrained and has no appearance in the roux, and cautery is more beneficial in this case and closer to healing.
de l’amollissement dou cuir des coions	softening of the skin of the testicles
Maintes fois est amollis li cuirs des coions en aucuns homes, por ceu que les chars que sont dedens sont mollifiees, et est lait a veoir;	Many times the skin of the testicles becomes soft in some men, because the parts inside become soft and can be seen through the skin;
et est mestier, quant on le vuet curer, c’on faice gesir lou malaide sus son dos, et li cope le cuir qui est mollifiez sus le cuir natureil;	and it is necessary, when one wants to treat it, that the patient lies on his back, and the physician presses the soft skin over the natural skin;
puis assemble les II levres a une costure, et se tu vues, cout premier la superfluiteit dou cuir mollifiiez a III costures ou IIII fermement;	then bring together the two lips of the wound with one stitch, and if you see it, sew the excess of the soft skin firmly with three or four stitches;
puis cope entre les costures, et lou cure si com les autres plaies, tant qu’il soit sanez, et chient li fil.	then bandage between the stitches, and treat it like other wounds until it is healed, then remove the thread.
dou chastrement	of chastisement
Saiches que chastremens est escomeniez en nostre loi, et por ceu il me plairoit que je n’en parlasse mie en cest livre;	Know that castration is considered a sin in our law, and for this reason I would prefer not to speak of it in this book;
et n’est necessaires fuer que por II manieres:	and it is only necessary for two reasons:
dont l’une est que li mires en saiche respondre quant on li demandera, et en saiche la cure;	the first is that physicians know how to answer when asked about it, and know how to treat it;
et li autre, por ceu que nos avons sovent mestier de chastrement d’aucunes bestes por nos aidier, si com de bouc et de mouton et de chait et d’autres bestes.	and the other is that we often need castration of certain animals to help us, such as goats and sheep and donkeys and other beasts.
Je dis donques que chastremens est fais selonc II manieres:	I say then that castration is done in two ways:
ou par atraction, ou par fendure.	either by attraction or by cutting.
En celle que nos faisons par attraction, faisons nos seoir la beste en aigue chaude, tant que li coion soient mollifiez et pendant;	In the one that we do by attraction, we have the animal sit in warm water until the testicles become soft and hanging;
puis les preing a ta main, tant qu’il soient remis et que tu ne les sentes plus.	then grab them with your hand, until they are dislocated and you no longer feel them.Et si li testiculoz ne sont pas pendans, mets ta main souz le menton et tire vers le haut tant qu’il soit dem
Du chastrement de taille:	On the castration of the testicles:
covient que tu teignes la beste, et li presse le cuir des coions a ta main senestre, puis lie le suspensoire, et cope sus chescun oef a I cop, quant tu les avras bien escorchiez;	you should hold the animal down and squeeze its scrotum with your left hand, then tie off the scrotal suspension strap, and cut into each testicle at the bottom, when you have thoroughly dried them.
et i laisse aucun poc dou syfac et lou subtil syfac qui est sor les vasselz;	and leave a little pouch of fat on top of the delicate vessels;
et ceste maniere de chastrement est muedre que cele qui est faite par attraction, por ceu que a l’atraction demoure par aventure aucune chose des coions, par coi li beste desire luxure;	and this method of castration is better than the one done by pulling them off, because in that method some testicle might be left behind and cause the animal to desire sex.
puis cure la plaie tant qu’ele soit sanee.	then treat the wound until it heals.
des hermofrodites	Of Hermaphrodites
Hermofrodie est selonc II manieres as homes:	There are two types of hermaphrodites in men:
l’une si est que entre les II coions apert ausi com li figure de la nature d’une femme, ou il ait poil, et aucunes fois en cort li urine.	one type is where between the testicles there appears a woman's sexual organs, with hair and sometimes the ability to urinate.
Et li autre maniere si est en femmes, et ait sus lou poignil ausi com une verge et II coions.	And the other method is for women; it has a handle like a rod and two testicles.
Et li cure de l’ome et de la fame si est que tu copes les chars ajostees toutes, et les cure si com autres plaies;	And the treatment for both men and women is that you cut off all the extra growths and treat them like any other wound.
en la seconde maniere, des homes dont li urine saut par lou cuir des coions, si n’a point de cure.	in the second way, men whose urine leaks through the skin of their scrotum, there is no cure.
de la tentigene	of the testicles
Tentigene est une chars ajostee sus la partie natureil, tant qu’elle est trop laide a veoir;	A tentige is a wound that is healed over the natural part, so that it is too ugly to look at;
et aucunes femmes l’ont ausi grant com une main, et c’est li cure.	and some women have them as large as a hand, and that is the cure.
Il covient que tu teignes la superfluiteit de la tentigene a ta main ou as oncines, et la cope legierement;	You should dye the excess of the tentige with your hand or with a knife, and then scrape it gently;
et n’aler mie trop em parfont, que decorremens de sanc n’i viegne, puis le cure d’autre cure tant qu’il soit sanez;	and do not go too deep, so that bleeding does not occur, then the cure of one cure with another until it is healed;
et a une autre char que naist a la bouche de la marris, et l’emple, et par aventure saut fuer, et est selonc la semblance d’une kowe, et por ceu l’apelerent li ancien «maladie kowee».	and at another wound that occurs at the mouth of the ulcer, and treat it, and perhaps it will heal, and is according to the appearance of a boil, and therefore they called it the 'cow disease'.
Si covient que tu la copes, si com nos avons dit la tentigene, et la cure tant qu’elle soit sanee.	If you must treat it, as we have said regarding the tenting, and heal it until it is cured.
de erratique	of the erratics
Erratique si est quant li nature de la femme n’est mie percie, ou li pertus est petis;	Erratic is when the nature of the woman is not understood, or the passage is small.
et est naturez par naissance, ou accidens par maladie que venue i est;	It is natural at birth, or accidental due to illness that comes upon it;
ou c’est par char ajostee, ou dou syfac subtil ou espés, et est fais em parfont en la marris, ou en costez, ou desoz, ou que soit;	or it is caused by a foreign object, or by a suppurating ulcer or wart, and it is formed as a deep wound in the mouth, or on the sides, or underneath, wherever it may be;
et deffent le concevoir, et l’enfantement, et par aventure les flors a avoir;	and they affect conception and childbirth, and sometimes flowers as well;
et li connoissance de ceu si est par le regart de la baile.	and the understanding of this is through observing the urine.
Se li estoupemens est prochiens apparans, si quier a tes dois ou au rait.	If the stumps are visibly close by, then cut them with your fingers or with a knife.Si li estoupemens est prochiens apparans, si quier a tes dois ou au rait.
S’il est dou syfac subtil, et il est prochiens as II leivres, si te haste, et la ront ensi:	If it is due to a wart and it is close to the urethra, then hasten and treat it thus:
met tes II dois indices ensamble, et li femme soit sus son dos, espandues ses jambes;	Place your two index fingers together, and have the woman lie on her back with her legs spread;
puis estent les II leivres forment, tant que li subtilz syfac soit rons, et soit overs li estoupemens;	then squeeze the urethra firmly until the wart is dislodged and expelled;
puis pren laine, et la moille en oile, et la met sus le leu, et gise li femme a home chescun jor, si qu’il ne puist souder.	take wool, moistened in oil, and apply it to the area, and let the woman lie still for seven days, so that it may not heal.
Et se li syfac est dur et espés, si covient que tu lou copes au spatumile semblant a foille de mirte.	And if the syphilitic sore is hard and thick, then you should cut it with a spatula similar to a myrtle leaf.
Se li estoupemens est de char nee, si la sospent a l’oncine et la cope;	if the wound is new, suspend them from the ceiling and the beam;
et aies les medicines estainchans sanc, si com acaice, sanc de dragon, encens, ensamble abun d’uef;	and have the blood-stanching remedies, such as oak gall, dragon's blood, incense, and an abundance of egg yolk;
puis amenistre une caine de plonc large, si que li plaie ne puisse souder;	then apply a plaster made from crushed lead, so that the wound may not heal;
et ensi soit longement, et li amenistre une tente de lin sec;	and for a long time, and let him use a tent of dry flax;
puis soit curez d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez.	then other treatments until he is healed.
Et quant en la marris vient char nee, si la covient coper selonc ceste maniere, se ce n’est apostemes enchancrez.	And when there is fresh flesh in the ulcer, it should be cut in this way, unless it is a deep abscess.
Car a l’aposteme enchancreit qui est en la marris, ne doit on touchier de feir.	For one must not touch an abscess that is deep in the ulcer.Et se li syfac est dur et espés, si covient que tu lou copes au spatumile semblant a foille de mirte.
des emorroides	of hemorrhoids
Emorroydes sont overtures de voines dont sans cort acostumeement, et quant les emorroydes sont vielles si devienent thelul;	Hemorrhoids are openings of veins from which blood flows without cessation, and when they are old, they become thrombosed;
et nos avons jai dit en la division les semblances d’aus, et les signes, et je dirai ci celles qui resoivent curation.	And we have already spoken about their likenesses in the section on signs, and I will now speak of those that can be cured.First, take a cautery made of fire, and apply it to the hemorrhoid so that it leaves the hair; let the hair grow long and even; and if they prick
Je di que les emorroides et li thelul, quant il sont em parfont en la marris, et il n’aperent au sentir, si n’est mie li cure par fer.	I say that hemorrhoids and throbbin, when they are deeply embedded in the rectum, and do not appear to the touch, are not cured by a cautery with iron.
Cil qui sont a la bouche de la marris, c’on puet sentir, sont cil c’on puet curer.	Those that are at the mouth of the rectum, which one can feel, are those that can be cured.Si on appert li thelul et les emorroides par grant dolur, si convient que l’on le cuie par fer; car la piere n’est mie trove a la guaine, ains est trove en la chair, ou il avient grant dolor, et s’eleve li sang.
Il covient donques que tu mettes la femme en une maison froide, puis estent l’altelul as tenailles, et le cope en ses racines, puis poudre sus medicines restraignans sanc, si com acaice et sanc de dragon et encens, et semblans choses;	You should therefore place the woman in a cool house, then heat the tweezers and the comb at their roots, then powder them with blood-stopping medicines such as aconite and dragon's blood and incense, and similar things.
puis boute ses piez a la paroit une houre, puis la met en aigue froide;	Then tie her feet to the wall for an hour, then put her in cold water;
et se decorremens de sanc i vient, si la fai seoir en une decoction de sumac et d’escorce de pomes grenates et de gales et de semblans choses, et puis pren farine d’orge, et la confis avec miel et aisil, et en fai I emplaustre sus son dos.	And if bleeding occurs, then she should sit in a decoction of sumac and pomegranate bark and gall and similar things, and then take barley flour and boil it with honey and garlic, and make a poultice out of it for her back.
Et se il estainche, c’est boin.	And if it stops, that is good.
Se ceu non, se li fai aerdre ventouses au dos et as mameles sens ferir;	If not, she should breathe in steam on her back and breasts without hurting herself;
puis pren lainne, et la moille en jus de plantain ou en jus d’aglentier avec vin viel, et fai aerdre au leu.	Then take wool, and moisten it in plantain juice or dogwood juice with old wine, and breathe in the steam on her back.
Et quant li aposteme repose, si cure lou leu d’oignement tant qu’il soit sanez;	And when the abscess has drained, then apply ointment to the wound until it heals.
et celle qui est apelee «albathir» est rouge, et est semblans a I chief aspre, si le covient coper si com j’ai dit le thelul;	and that which is called "albathir" is red, and resembles rough wool, so it should be covered as I have said before.
et puis lou cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	And then cure the wound until it heals.
des apostemes de la marris	of abscesses in the rectum
Maintes manieres d’aposteme vienent en la marris, si com chancre et aposteme pierous et herpes et estiomenes et fistules et emorroides et aposteme chaut, et plusors autres maladies que j’ai dit en la division.	Many types of abscesses come about in the body, such as ulcers and pus-filled sores, and herpes, and boils, and fistulas, and hemorrhoids, and hot abscesses, and various other ailments which I have detailed in the classification.
Il covient donques que je die en cest traitier l’aposteme chaut qui vient en la marris, qui n’est mie des apostemes que coillent bowe;	Therefore, I shall discuss in this treatise about hot abscesses that occur in the intestines, which are not among those that occur in the bowels:
et se tu vues savoir l’ovraige de fer, si regarde se li apostemes est agus en l’encomencement de sa venue, et plain de chalor et de fievre, et s’il devient rouge se tu le pues veoir.	and if you wish to know the treatment for iron, then observe whether the abscess is painful at the beginning of its appearance, and full of heat and fever, and whether it becomes red when you can see it.
Adonques ne te haster mie de percier, mais lou fais meurer tant que li dolor soit apaisie;	Therefore, do not be hasty in piercing it, but let it drain as long as the pain is relieved;
et puis fai seoir lou malaide sus I siege, et ait II petis sieges ou il se cline, et apoie sus son dos et assemble ses piez as parties defuer la jambe;	and then let the patient sit on a chair, and have two small chairs on which he can lean, and support his back and gather his feet towards his leg;
et soient ses cuixes espandues, et mette ses braz desoz ses genous, et les lie bien d’un boin liien;	and let his buttocks be spread out, and let him put his arms under his knees, and tie them well with a good rope;
puis succe li baille devers lou destre costeit, et i amenistre l’estrument dont on oevre la bouche de la marris, de coi ci aprés vient li forme;	then suck the wound towards the right side, and administer the instrument with which one opens the mouth of the wound, from which the shape [of the cautery] comes;
et covient que quant tu i vues amenistrer cest estrument, que tu fiches le rait premier ens por savoir la parfondeté de la marris, si que ceu qui entre ens de l’estrument n’i viegne plus em parfont qu’il ne doit, et qu’il ne blece la malaide;	and it is necessary that when you see the instrument being administered, you should insert the rod first to know the depth of the wound, so that what goes into the instrument does not go in more deeply than it should, and so that it does not harm the patient;
et se li estrumens est plus grans, si covient covrir la parfondesce de la marris de drapelz, si que li estrumens ne li grieve;	and if the instrument is larger, then the depth of the wound should be covered with cloth so that the instrument does not cause pain;et quant tu i vues amenistrer l’estrument de coi ci vient li forme sus la marris, si covient que tu prends li cautere et li mets sur la marris, si qu’il ne se remue, et qu’il soit bien fix;
et covient qu’il mette le cornet de l’estrument au desus, et qu’il teigne l’estrument.	and he must put the horn of the instrument on top, and hold the instrument steady.
Et quant li apostemes apert, et on lou fent a la main mol, si le covient coper au chief, au spatumile leit;	And when the abscess has opened, and they have made an incision in the soft part of the hand, then it must be covered with a bandage, with a light dressing.
et quant li bowe est vuidie, si covient que tu mettes en la plaie tentes moillies en oile roset, ou en oile vert sec;	and when the bowels have been emptied, then you must put in the wound moist bandages soaked in rose oil, or in dry verde oil;
et met la tente fuer de la plaie au parfont de la marris, et met par defuer sus la marris et sus le poignil lainne nette moillie en aigue ou malves soient cuites;	and put the bandage over the wound, down to the bottom of the wound, and put another bandage above the wound, and on the little finger, a clean moist bandage soaked in water or mallows that have been cooked;
puis le cure aprés II jors d’oignement avenant a ceu, tant qu’il soit sanez;	then treat it again after two days of ointment suitable for this, until it is healed;
et aucune fois leve on la marris et la plaie par clistere d’aigue et de miel, et puis d’aigue ou racines de lis et aristologe longe soient cuites;	and sometimes raise the wound and the injury with an enema of water and honey, and then with water or roots of lily and aristology that have been cooked for a long time;
puis reveigne a l’oignement.	then return to the ointment.
Et se li plaie est reponue en la marris, si covient que tu te gardes de cuire de fer, mais cure la si com nos avons dit en la division.	And if the wound is sunken in the injury, then you should beware of cooking with iron, but cure it as we have said in the division.
de l’enfantement	of childbirth
Mestier est premier a la baile qu’elle conoisse la figure de l’enfantement natureil, et li signes si est quant tu vois la femme apresser aval, et desire odorer l’ar:	It is necessary for the midwife to first know the natural signs of childbirth, and the signals that something is wrong when you see the woman push downward, and desire to smell flowers:
adonques se haste li enfes de fuer issir;	therefore the child rushes to be born;
adonc saiches que cil enfantemens est selonc la figure natureil, et est li issue soz son chief, et li secondine avec lui;	then you know that this childbirth is natural, and the baby emerges head first, with the placenta following;
et quant tu vois ces signes, si covient presser legierement son ventre, si que li enfes isse tost;	and when you see these signs, you should gently push on her belly, so that the child is born quickly;
car quant il dessent sus son chief, si ist li secondine avec lui, et est mondee li marris de ses superfluitez par bone mundification;	for when they descend head first, the placenta comes with them, and the mother's excess fluids are cleansed through a good cleaning;
et cist qui vient autrement ne vient mie naturelment.	and those who come differently do not come naturally.
Car il vient aucune fois sus ses piez, et vient fuer li cors ou li chiés, et les mains, ou il vient sus son ventre, ou sovin, et est convertis par aventure sor son col, et par autres figures malvaises;	For sometimes they come out feet first, or outside the body through the chest or arms, or they come out upside down, or they are turned around in some other bad way;
si est mestier a la baile qu’elle soit saige et subtilz en ces choses, et se warse d’error et de decevement, et je vos mostrerai toutes les figures coment on li doit aidier.	If it is necessary at the dance that she be wise and skilled in these things, and beware of error and deception, and I will show you all the ways she should be helped.
Se li enfes vient sus son chief par issue natureil, et li femme enfante griement, et li vertus de li est foible, si la fai seoir sus une selle, ou les femmes la tienent;	If the baby comes out head first through a natural birth, and the woman gives birth with great effort, and her strength is weak, then let her sit on a saddle, or have women hold her.
et arose sa nature d’oile ou fenugreic soit cuit, et puis boute li baile entre ses dois le petit spatumile dont ci est li forme:	And use the natural oil of rose or fenugreek that has been cooked, and then put the baby between her breasts the small spatumile of which there is the shape:
et fende la secondine, et cope a son ungle tant que li moistors qui est ens corre fuers;	and split the afterbirth, and scrape its nail until the fluid that is within flows out;
et preint lou ventre de la femme tant que li enfes dessende, et s’il ne dessent, si covient clisterizer la femme de muscillaige de fenugrec avec oile de sisament;	and press on the woman's belly until the baby descends, and if it does not descend, then one must enema the woman with mucilage of fenugreek with oil of seisment;
puis la fai preindre et esternuer de condisi, et tien sa bouche et son neis une houre:	then have her breathe and sneeze out some of the powder, and hold her mouth and nose for an hour:
si istra maintenant l’enfes.	if she now expels the fetus.
Et se les II mains issent fuer, si covient que tu les ramoinne legierement poc et poc;	And if both hands come out, then you must gently push them back in a little at a time;
et s’elles n’i puent entrer, si met la femme sus I siege, et li lieve les piés en haut;	and if they cannot go in, then put the woman on a chair, and raise her feet up high;
puis deboute le siege sus terre, et teigne on la femme, qu’elle ne chiece au deboutement;	then raise the chair off the ground, and hold the woman so that she does not lean forwards when standing up;Apres que li sieges esteit debout, si covient qu’ele soit en ses sens, et teigne le membre qui est disloie,
et se li mains n’i puet entrer, et li enfes muert, si li cope les mains au couteil qui est ci devant mis, et estrai l’enfant, et ramoine igalment.	After the chair is upright, the woman should be conscious and the dislocated joint should be held in place; if the hands cannot go in and the child is dead, then grasp the hands with a knife at the tip of the fingers as described above, extract the child, and reset the dislocation in the same way.Et s’ele ne vuit pas lasser aller li enfes, si ten le membre en la main dreit et fort, et met le sie
de l’issue de l’enfant sus ses piés	of the child's issue upon its feet
Quant li enfes vient sus ses piez, si lou covient bouter en haut;	When an infant comes onto its feet, it must be pushed upwards.
et puis le torne poc et poc, tant qu’il soit igalz;	Then rock it back and forth gently until it is even;
puis preigne I des piez et l’estende poc et poc.	then hold one foot and stretch it out gently.
Cant il saut jusc’as cuixes, si la comande a preindre, et la fai esternuer de condisi;	If he jumps up to his hips, instruct him to grab hold, and make him sneeze from the stomach;
si saut fuer, se Deus vuet.	if he jumps out, God willing.
Et s’il n’ist fuer si com nos avons dit, si le torne poc et poc, tant qu’il soit selonc la figure natureil.	And if he cannot jump as we have said, then turn him little by little until he is in his natural position.
Car adonques ist il legierement.	For then he is easily cured.
Et s’il ne vient fuer si com nos avons, dit si pren muscillaige de altee, et oile de sisament, et gomme fondue, et broie tout en I mortier;	And if he does not come out as we have described, take mustard and oil and gum, and crush them all in a mortar;
et met sus la nature de la femme dedens et defuer cest oignement, puis la fai seoir en aigue tede jusque desoz les costelz;	and apply this ointment to the mother's abdomen and then make her sit in warm water up to her ribs;
et quant elle est moillifie desoz, se li fai I coliere de mirre, et li met desoz, et li laisse une houre;	and when she is soaked underneath, put the myrrh collar on her and let it stay there for an hour;
puis la fai seoir sus I siege, puis la fai esternuer et estraint sa bouche et son neis, et li preint le ventre legierement, car li enfes saut maintenant.	then have her sit on a chair, then make her sneeze and hold her mouth and nose, and gently press her belly, for the child will soon jump out.
de l’issue de l’enfant sus ses genous	for the child to come out over his knees
Quant li enfes vient en ceste forme, si i mette li baile ses mains poc et poc;	When the child comes in this way, she puts her hands on it little by little;
puis soit sovinee sus son col, et li pendent li piez aval, et soit gisans sor I lit;	then she lies down on her back, and her feet hang down below, and she lies on the bed;
et plie ses mains poc et poc, et puis li preint les mains sus lou ventre, et li oste les cussins desoz, tant qu’elle soit appareillie aval;	and bends her knees little by little, and then she presses her hands on her belly, and takes away the cushions from under her, so that she is exposed below;
et se li enfes ne saut, si pren ses piez et li muef forment, puis li muef lou ventre amont, puis i boute tes mains;	and if the child does not jump out, she takes her feet and moves them about, then she rubs her belly upwards, and then puts in her hands;
et ewe l’enfant poc et poc;	and pushes the child little by little;
et comande a la femme qu’elle se preigne tant que li enfes isse.	and instructs the woman to press until the child comes out.
de l’issue de l’enfant qui vient dou large une main pendant	of the issue of the child which comes out width a hand during
I covient engignier a ramener la main:	We must find a way to return the hand:
s’on ne la puet ramener, si fai lever la femme, et aler;	if we cannot return it, then have the woman stand up and walk.
s’elle ne puet aler, si la fai gesir sus I lit, et li deboute les jambes forment;	If she cannot walk, then have her lie on the bed, and raise her legs straight;
puis amenistre lou muscillaige que j’ai conteit;	then bring the mustard that I described;
et s’elle n’enfante, si la fai seoir sus I siege, puis estudie au rameneir la main;	and if she does not give birth, then have her sit on a chair, and then try to return the hand;
et ewe l’enfant selonc la figure natureil, et la fai esternuer, et li comande qu’elle se preigne tant que li enfes isse fuer.	and hold the child according to its natural position, and make her sneeze, and instruct her to grab it as it comes out.
de l’issue de l’enfant sus son col, et ait espandues ses mains, et sa faice tornee devers lou dos sa mere	from the child's exit at its neck, and spread his hands, and turned his face towards his mother's back
I covient que li baile teigne sa main, puis le torne poc et poc, et l’ewe legierement;	We must have the midwife tug on the hand, then pull it gently bit by bit, and wiggle it lightly;
et quant il est igalz, si met sus la nature muscillaige de altee et oile, si com nos avons dit, puis li comande qu’elle se mueve poc et poc;	and when it's even, put the mustard mixture of arnica and oil as we said before, then instruct her to move it bit by bit;
et quant tu avras ce fait, si la fai seoir sus I siege, et li comande k’elle se preigne;	and when you have done this, make her sit on a chair, and tell her to hold onto it.
et la fai esternuer.	and make her sneeze.
de ceste meisme maniere a tout la secondine	in the same way with all the afterbirth
Quant il vient fuer en ceste maniere a tout la secondine, si cope la secondine a ton ungle, tant que li moistors soit vuidie;	When all the afterbirth has come out in this way, catch the afterbirth with your fingernail so that the fluids are expelled;
et se li enfes pent sus sa faice et sus son col, si la cope des la boude, qu’elle ne soit retenue, et muere li enfes;	and if the child can move its face and neck, catch hold of it so that it does not struggle, and the child will die.
puis boute l’enfant dedens, tant que tu l’aies mis si com il covient, et comande a la femme qu’elle se preigne aucune fois:	Then put the child back inside, positioning it correctly; instruct the woman to hold on several times:
adonques si istra legierement.	then pull gently.
de l’issue des gemelz	of the exit of twins
Saiches que gemeil naissent maintes fois, et aucune fois en naissent III ou IIII;	You should know that twins are born many times, and sometimes three or four are born;
et ceu n’est mie estrainge chose, et poc avient.	and this is not a strange thing, and it happens often.
Dui sont estrainge chose, et ne vivent mie, se poc nom;	These are strange, and do not live long if they do.
je sai ceu, qu’il soient multipliiet, et sont desevrez par lou syfac qui les devise, qui est liiez a la boude;	I know that they will multiply, and are separated by the membrane that divides them, which is attached to the womb.
et aucune fois issent ausi naturelment com uns tous sous, si com nos avons dit.	And sometimes they emerge as naturally as a tail, just as we have said.
Et s’il issent griement, si la cure si com nos avons dit, et soit li baile subtilz, et faice tost et legierement ceu qu’elle fait;	And if they emerge quickly, the midwife should act as we have described, and be quick and skillful in what she does;
et faice ensi com il vaut mues a salut.	and act in such a way that it benefits the mother.
de plusors enfans	of many children
Aucune fois sont formez en la marris I ou II ou III ou IIII ou V ou VI ou VII, ou plusors jusc’a XV, et sont tout formeit en forme d’enfant par le mesurement dou saige glorious, et couvient que li baile saiche tout ceu, car par aventure semblans chose li avient;	Sometimes they are formed in the womb as one, or two, or three, or four, or five, or six, or seven, or more, up to fifteen, and they are all formed in the shape of a child according to the measurement of the wise glorious sage, and the midwife should know all this, because by chance something similar might happen;
si faice selonc ceu qu’il covient.	and she should act accordingly.
de l’enfant mort	of the dead child
Quant tu cures la femme de l’enfant mort ou ventre, si com j’ai dit en la division, et il ne vient fuers, et tu es constrains d’ovraige de mains;	When you are treating a woman for a dead child or abdominal pain, as I have said in the previous chapter, and there is no progress, and you are forced to use manual manipulation;
si covient que tu saiches se li femme est de saine vertut, et n’ait accident ou elle ait paor de mort;	If you need to know whether a woman is of sound health, and has no incident that causes her fear of death.
si covient que li femme soit sovinee sus son dos, et soit ses chiés enclins aval, et les jambes levees;	It is necessary for the woman to be laid on her back, with her hips tilted downward and her legs raised.
et li ministre la teigne de II pars, ou elle soit liie au lit si qu’elle ne soit traite au dessendement de l’enfant;	And if she is tied to the bed so that she does not move, this will aid in delivering the child;
puis frotez la bouche de la marris d’oiles moistes avec muscillaige de altee et de fenugrec et semence de lin, puis oigne li baile ses mains de ces oiles et de ces muscillaiges;	Then rub the mouth of the mother with moist oils mixed with musk, fennel, and flax seed; then anoint the midwife's hands with these oils and musk.
puis les boute en la marris legierement, puis quiere I leu ou elle boute les oncines que soient covenaubles a ceu, et pren warde se li enfes est apparilliez qu’il dessende sus son chief;	Then gently insert them into the mother's privates, taking care not to hurt her; and pay attention to make sure that the child is positioned to come out head first.
si fiche les oncines en ses eulz ou en son col ou en sa bouche ou en som palais ou desoz la barbe ou en la forcele ou pres des costez, et se li dessendemens est sus piez, se li fiche ou poignil et as costes moienes;	If it gets stuck in her throat, or under the beard, or in the navel, or near the ribs, or if it's feet are coming out first, push on its bottom and sides.
et covient qu’il teigne l’oncine a sa main destre, et mette la corbeure entre ses dois de la senestre main, et li boute a tout sa main legierement, et fiche l’oncine en aucun de ces leus que nos avons dit, tant qu’il viegne a la chose vuide;	and he must dye the thread with his right hand, and place the needle between the thumb and forefinger of his left hand, and draw the thread through all his fingers gently, and insert the needle into one of the places we have mentioned, until it reaches the empty space.
et c’est li forme de l’oncine:	and this is the shape of the needle:
puis fiche encontre I autre oncine, ou le tier se tu en as mestier, si que li estractions soit igalz;	then insert another needle, or a third if you need it, so that the extraction is even;
et puis l’estent igalment en movant d’une part et d’autre, por mues issir, et soit li oncines dentez por mues tenir, si com ci est li forme:	and then they are moved evenly from one side to the other, so that they can exit; and the needles must be gripped tightly so that they do not move, as shown in this drawing:
Et s’il en demoure une partie, si oigne li baile aucuns de ses dois d’oile, et les boute en celle partie, et traie l’autre partie;	And if any part remains, he should anoint one of his fingers with oil and insert it into that part, and pull the other part;
et s’il en i demoure point, si met cest oncine ou plus haut leu, et fai ceu tant qu’il s’en isse tout fuers.	and if nothing remains, he should insert this needle or a higher one, and do this until it all comes out completely.
Et se l’une mains vient devant l’autre, et il ne puet ramener por l’estreignement, si covient que tu envoloupes sus I drapeil, tant qu’il isse tote;	And if one hand comes before the other, and he cannot bring it back due to the dislocation, then you must wrap a cloth around it, so that it goes all the way down.
puis la cope en la jointure de la plante ou au coute, et ensi covient que tu faices en l’autre main, et as II piés.	Then, you must cup your hand at the base of the palm or wrist, and you must do the same with the other hand and feet.
Et se li chiés de l’enfant est gros et il est estrois en l’issue, ou il ait ou chief aigue assemblee, si covient que tu boute le spatumile espinous entre tes dois, et fent le chief et estrai l’aigue;	And if the head of the child is large and it is stuck in the birth canal, or if it has a sharp pain gathered at the head, then you must push the spathumile* between your fingers, and press the head, and draw out the sharp pain;
ou tu la ront a l’estrument qui est apelez «almidach», de coi li forme vient avec les estrumens ou chapistre qui est aprés cestui;	or you can use the instrument called 'almidach', from which the mold comes with the instruments or chapter that follows this one;
et ensi meisme faice se li enfes a grant chief naturelment;	and thus you will do if the child has a large natural head;
et puis traie fuer les osses as tenailles, et se li chiés saut fuer et il estraint a la forcele, si soit fendus, tant que li moistors qui est ou pis issue fuer;	and then pull out the bones with tongs, and if the head jumps out and is forced, let it be split, until the moisture that is in the wound comes out.
et s’elle ne puet issir, si le cope par pieces au mues que tu pues;	And if it cannot come out, then cut it into pieces as small as you can.
et s’il est enflez au ventre ou desoz les costez, si covient que tu lou perces tant que li moistors corre.	And if it is swollen in the belly or under the ribs, then you should pierce it so that the moisture runs out.
Et se li enfes est sus ses piez, si est li attraction legiere, et li adrecemens a la bouche de la marris est legier.	And if the swelling is on their feet, the pull is light, and the movement towards the mouth of the wound is easy.
Et s’il est estrois au ventre ou au pis, si couvient que tu l’estraies a I drapeil envoloupeit sus la main;	And if it is bound in the belly or the udder, then you should loosen it with your hand wrapped in a cloth.
et fent le ventre ou le pis, tant que li moistors qui i est corre;	And cut the belly or the udder so that the moisture that is inside runs out.
et se li autre membre sont osteit, et li chiez demoure, si boute li baile sa main em parfont de la marris, et le traie jusc’a la bouche de la marris;	And if any other part is broken, and the head remains, then push the shoulder-bone with your hand into the wound, and pull it out to the mouth of the wound.
puis i boute I oncine ou II, et le trai fuer;	Then put in the hook or two, and pull it out.
et se li bouche de la marris est retrecie por aposteme chaut qui i est venus, si n’i covient mie travillier, ains covient amenistrer choses moistes et grasses;	and if the mouth of the wound is narrowed by a hot abscess that has formed there, one should not work on it, but rather apply moist and fatty substances;
et li amenistre emplaustres, et siece en aigue mollifians et amoistans.	and let the patient use poultices, and wash with warm, softening waters.
Et se li enfes est sus son costeit, et tu le pues mettre igal, si amenistre ceu que nos avons dit en l’enfant vif;	And if the child is on its side, and you can bring it to lie evenly, then administer what we have said for a living child;
et s’on nen ait pooir, si lou trai fuer par pieces, et n’i laissier rien de la secondine.	and if one cannot, then cut it into pieces, and leave nothing of the afterbirth.
Et quant tu avras ce fait, se li amenistre ceu que nos avons dit ens apostemes chaus que vienent en la marris;	And when you have done this, administer what we have said for hot abscesses that come in a wound;
et se decorremens de sanc vient, si soit mise en aigue restraignant, et li amenistre autres cures.	and if there is an discharge of blood, let it be put in restraining waters, and let the patient undergo other treatments.
Et je vis une femme en cui ventre uns enfes avoit esteit mors, puis consut .i. autre sus celui, et refut mors li autres.	And I saw a woman in whose belly a child had died, then another was sewn over it, and the other died too.
Aprés lonc tens li vint uns apostemes en la boude, et enfla tant qu’il ovrit, et comensa a grant porreture.	After a long time she got an abscess in her armpit, which swelled so much that it opened and began to ooze profusely.
je fui apelez a la cure, et i pensai lonc tens, et ne pot soder li plaie.	I was called to the wound, and I thought for a long time, but could not heal it.
Je mis sus emplaustre de fort attraction, et en issit uns os, et aprés aucuns jors uns autres.	I applied a strong attracting plaster, and one bone came out, and after a few days, some others.
Je me mervillai mout, por ceu c’ou ventre n’a point d’os.	I was very amazed, because the belly has no bones.
Si pensai que c’estoit des os d’un enfant mort.	I thought that they were the bones of a dead child.
Je quis la plaie, et en traï mains os, tant que li femme fut em millor point;	I examined the wound, and found bones poking out, until the woman was in a better state;
et vesquit li femme lonc tens ensi, et issoit adés un poc de bowe dou leu;	and the woman wore it for a long time like this, and then suddenly a little bit of bowing from the heat;
et je n’ai recordeit cest chapistre fuer que por ceu que, quant li maistres trueve une estrainge chose, qu’il i saiche mettre aide.	and I haven't recorded this chapter until now because when the master finds a strange thing, he will know how to apply a remedy.
dou ramener la marris a son leu	how to return the dislocated joint to its place
Ci aprés vient li forme dou pressor, a coi on ewe les livres;	Here after comes the form of the press, which is used in books;
et a II tornans as II chiés des II liiens.	and at two turns around the two shoulders.
Toutevoie, li cornes soit plus subtilz dou restrictoire, et soit fais de ebene ou de bux;	Nevertheless, the horns of the press should be more subtle, and they should be made of ebony or boxwood;
et soit li bouche dou fust I doi de large, et li marge des arbres I doit, et de lonc une palme et demi;	and its mouth, two fingers wide, and the margin of the wood, one palm and a half;
et enmi les II liemens soient dui ajostemens de cest meisme fust, qui soient fermeit en l’un et en l’autre, de demi palme de lonc ou un poc plus;	and in between the two limbs there should be two adjustment of this same wood, which are secured in one and the other, half a palm long or a little more;
et cist dui ajostement sont bouteit en la bouche de la marris por ovrir quant on torne les II cornes.	and these two settings are placed at the mouth of the wound to open when one turns the two horns.
Une autre forme, a sa semblance plus subtilz et plus legiere, soit faite de fust de ebene ou de bux, selonc la semblance des tenailles;	A different form, which is more subtle and lighter, should be made from ivory or boxwood, according to the appearance of tweezers;
et ait as II chiés II ajostemens, si com tu vois, d’une palme de lonc, et II dois de large;	and has two settings, as you see, one palm-long, and two fingers wide;
et quant tu vues ovrir la marris a tout l’estrument, si fai seoir la femme sor I lit, les piez pendant et les jambes overtes, puis boute les II ajostemens ajostez ensamble en la marris, et tien le chief de l’estrument desoz entre ses cuixes;	and when you see the wound open with all the instrument, then let the woman lie on the bed, her feet hanging and her legs spread, then insert the two settings together into the wound, and hold the head of the instrument between her thighs;
puis oevre ta main a tout l’estrument, si com tu as fait as tenailles igalment, selonc la quantiteit que tu vues ovrir la bouche de la marris, tant que li baile faice ceu qu’elle vuet.	then work your hand on the whole instrument, just as you did with the tweezers, according to the amount that you want to open the mouth of the wound, until the spouse does what she wants.
Cist estrument sont tuit sormontez, et sont multiplies lor semblances;	All instruments are tipped and their appearances multiplied.
et quant li mires les ait apareilliez, tant est plus hastans li oevre, et plus haute as homes por lor quantiteit.	And when the surgeon has prepared them, the work is quicker and the patients are better for it in terms of quantity.
Si ne despire mie l’estrument que tu ne l’aies apparelliet, car lor necessitez n’est mie escusauble.	Do not despair about the instrument until you have prepared it, for their necessity is unavoidable.
Quant li secondine est retenue a l’enfantement, si covient que tu comandes a la malaide qu’ele reteigne son alaine, et puis la fai esternuer de condisi, et li estraint tes mains a la bouche et au neis;	When the afterbirth is retained in childbirth, you should instruct the patient to hold her breath and then cause her to sneeze with an emetic, and squeeze her hands against her mouth and nose;
et s’elle saut per ceu, bien est.	and if she vomits, all the better.
Se ceu non, si prent I pot, et fai I pertus ou cuvercle, et i met herbes que puissent ovrir la bouche de la marris, si com calament, rue, anis, camomille, cassialigne et centoire;	If not, take a pot and make an emetic with herbs that open the mouth of the womb, such as hellebore, rue, anise, chamomile, cassia, and centaury;
toutes ces herbes, ou aucunes d’eles, soient cuites ou pot en aigue sus le feu;	all these herbs, or some of them, are cooked in water over the fire;
puis met une caine ou pertus dou pot, et l’autre chief en la bouche de la marris, et la teigne tant que li vapors viegne dedens la marris;	then put one end of the pipe into the pot and the other into the mouth of the woman, and hold it there until the steam enters the womb;
puis la fai esternuer, si com nos avons dit.	then make him sneeze, as we have said.
Si saut li secondine hastanment.	Then let the secondine dry quickly.
Et s’elle remaint aprés ceste cure, et n’ist mie fuer, si comande a la baile qu’ele moille sa main senestre en oile de sesement ou en muscillaige de altee, et puis la boute en la nature, et quiere la secondine;	And if it remains after this treatment and is not cured, command the midwife to wet her left hand in oil of sesame or in musk-soaked water, then insert it into the birth canal and push out the afterbirth;
et quant elle l’avra trovee, si la preigne et l’estende poc et poc droitement, si que li marris ne chiece a l’estraction;	and when she has found it, grab it and slowly pull it out straight so that the mother does not feel pain during extraction;
mais la covient movoir legierement a destre et a senestre, et puis traie;	but it must be moved gently to the right and left, and then pulled out;et quant elle l’avra tirée hors de tout, si le veuit mettre sur une toille ne sur un cotte, et la couvrir
si venra et se desaerdra.	and when she has pulled it all out, she should put it on a cloth or shirt and cover it up
Et se li bouche de la marris est jai estrecie, nos avons dit la cure d’esternuer, et de fumigation des herbes;	And if the birth canal of the mother is tight, we have described the cure for sneezing and herbal fomentation;et s’elle deit en son lit et ne peut lever, et le sang lui vait par la ou elle a accouchie, si covient qu’ele soit sur une cotte ou une toille, et li
et s’elle n’ist de tout ceu que nos avons dit, si garde que tu ne foloies au traire;	and if it is not one of those we have described, then beware of following their treatment;
mais il couvient que ceu qui est a la bouche de la marris, que tu le lies a la cuixe de la femme, puis la clisterize d’oignement tetrafarmaçon;	but it is necessary that he who has the mouth of the wound, to tie him to the thigh of the woman, then cauterize with ointment of four drugs;
si la porrira et remettra, et venra fuer;	if she defecates and passes gas, and then goes out;
mais toutevoie, quant elle porrist si en vient male odor au stomac et au chief, et blece la malaide.	but nonetheless, when she defecates, if a foul odor comes from the stomach and head, and causes the illness to flare up.
Si covient donques fumigations covenaubles a ceu:	Then it is necessary to use suitable fumigations:
aucun des anciens ont esproveit fumigation de cresson et de figues seches.	some of the ancients have tried fumeation with watercress and dried figs.
Li forme de l’estrument a coi on fumige la femme a la retenue des flors et de la secondine si est ceste:	The shape of the instrument used to smoke out the woman for the retention of flowers and afterbirth is as follows:
Et est de voirre semblant a une caine, et met on le chief subtil en la nature, et les chiés larges sus le feu;	And it is in the shape of a dog, and one puts the narrow end into the nature, and the wide end above the fire;
et soit li fumigations sus les charbons, et la teigne tant qu’elle soit gastee, et rencomence une autre.	and the fumeation is on the coals, and one fume until it is worn out, then starts again another.Et si le fumee ne tuit pas l’esguile, puis si doit faire le fumigation de sauge;
de percier lou fondement	to pierce the foundation
Maint enfant naissent qui n’ont mie le fondement perciet, ains l’ait estoupeit uns subtilz syfac:	Many children are born who do not have the foreskin pierced, but instead have a thin membrane covering it.
si covient donques a la baile qu’ele perce celui syfac a son doit, et ne lou perce mie de spatumile agut, et garse le lacement qu’elle ne le touche;	Therefore, the midwife must pierce this membrane with her finger, and not with an awl or anything else, and be careful not to touch the foreskin.
puis met sus lainne moillie en vin et en oile, puis la cure d’oignement tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then, she should apply a mixture of wine and oil on it, and then dress the wound with ointment until it is healed.
Et se tu doutes qu’il ne restoupe, si met ou pertus une caine de plonc, et li laisse mains jors, et soit ostee quant li enfes vuet aler en chambres.	And if you doubt that he will be cured, then put a plug of wool in the wound, and leave it for several days, and remove it when the child wants to go to bed.
Et aucune fois vient cist estoupemens de soudement de plaie ou d’aposteme;	Sometimes this membrane comes from a wound or an abscess;
si covient coper celui soudement:	in which case you must cover the wound immediately:
si soit curez, si com nos avons dit de la caine de plonc.	as we have said before regarding the treatment of warts.
de la fistule dou fondement	from the fistula of the fundament
Fistules qui vienent desoz le fondement sont nodation, et groissor que vienent delez lou fondement defuer, ou en l’espaice des II parties, si a une fistule ou plusors;	Fistulas that originate beneath the foreskin are nodules, and they grow larger if they come from underneath the foreskin or in between its two parts, and they can be single or multiple.And if there is a fistula, or more than one:
et quant celle nodation est anciene, si aoeuvre, et encort moistor awouse blainche ou subtilz bowe, et aucune fois sont ces fistule persans;	and when this dislocation is old, it opens and often emits moisture, a white pus or thin fluid, and sometimes these are persistent ulcers.
et sont conues par ceu qu’il en ist ou egestion ou ventositeit quant li malaide fait egestion, et par aventure en saut uns vers.	and they are caused by an ejection or venting of wind when the patient ejects wind, and sometimes a worm comes out.
Et si a fistules que percent jusc’a la vessie, et jusc’a la moitiet de la verge;	And there are ulcers that pierce all the way to the bladder, and halfway down the penis;
et parvienent jusc’a la jointure de la cuixe, et jusc’a nout de la kowe.	and they reach as far as the hip joint, and to the anus.
Et ensi conoist on la fistule persant au fondement, et ne mie persant:	And so one knows a persistent ulcer in the rectum, and one that does not burst:
et est que tu boutes ton doi indice ou fondement, et boute une aguille subtil d’arain ou de fer en la fistule quant il n’i a tortuositeit.	and you should thrust your finger into the rectum, and push in a thin needle made of iron or steel into the ulcer when there is no twisting.
Et s’il ait tortuositeit, si i boute une tente de plonc subtil, ou I poil de cheval, tant que tu sentes la tente ou le poil a ton doit;	And if it has a twist in it, then push in a thin wooden rod, or a horse hair, as far as you can feel the rod or hair with your finger;
et se tu ne le sens, et il ne vient dou pertus egestion ne ventositeit ne ver, si com nos avons dit:	and if you do not feel it, and it does not come out through the orifices as wind or farts or urine, as we have said:
saiches qu’elle ne perce mie;	know that it does not pierce;
si te haste dou curer.	if you want to cure it.
Et quant li fistule est persans jusc’a la vessie ou jusc’a conduit de l’urine, si en saut li urine, et ne puet soudeir par medicines.	And when the fistula has reached the bladder or the urethra, then the urine flows out, and medicine cannot stop it.
S’elle est percie jusc’a la jointure de la cuixe, si est li tente venans jusc’au leu;	If it is pierced up to the hip joint, then the tent will come up to that spot;
s’il n’i a tortuositeit et li invention de la dolor entor, si est qu’il en ist adés bowe, et n’i vaut medicine ne soudement par oignement;	if there is winding and pain throughout the body, then it will go away on its own without medicine or ointments;
et en ces fistules persans n’a point de cure fuer que labor, et vaniteit des folz mires qui s’en entremettent.	and in these weeping sores there is no treatment except effort and the vanity of foolish midwives who interfere.
En celle qui n’est mie persans et n’est mie anciene, a esperance de saniteit par fer, si com j’ai esproveit, et est que li malaides gise entre tes mains sus son dos;	In those that are not weeping and are not old, there is hope of healing through fire, as I have experienced, and the patient should lie on his back between your hands;
et li lieve les jambes jusque sus ses cuixes, et ait ses cuixes enclinees a son ventre;	and raise his legs up to his hips, and let his hips be inclined towards his belly;
puis boute une tente d’arain, ou de plonc s’il i a tortuositeit, tant que tu saiches ou li tente vient.	then put on an iron ring, or a plaster if there is tortuosity, as long as you know where the ring comes from.
Se li malaides la sent entor le fondement, si covient que tu i boutes ton doi indice, se sens adonques que li tente l’ait perciet;	If the patient feels it around the anus, then you should put your index finger in, if without piercing the ring;
et soit descoverte ou tu sens entre ton doit le syfac ou la char, adonques saiches qu’elle est persans;	and uncover where you feel between your finger and the flesh, then you know it is pierced;
si n’i travillier mie c’on ne la puet saner.	if one does not work on it, it cannot be healed.
On dist toutevoie c’on em puet bien saner aucuns, mais ce avient poc;	They still say that some can be healed, but that happens rarely;
et li aide c’on i fait, si est c’on eschaufe le cautere subtil selonc la largesce de la fistule, si com il est devant dit;	and the aid that is done, one burns the cautery subtly according to the width of the fistula, as has been said before;
et le boute tout chaut en la fistule, tant qu’il viegne delez le fondement;	and insert it into the fistula all the way until it comes out from the anus;
et faice ceu II fois ou III, tant que tu saiches que ces chars fautrees soient arses, qui sont semblant a une penne d’oiseil;	And do this two or three times until you know that these charred meats are burnt, which look like an owl's feather;
et puis le cure de tentes moillies em burre, tant que celle chars isse fuer, puis le cure d’oignement enjanrant char et soudant.	and then the cautery of moist tents until the swelling goes down, and then the cautery of ointment binding and sealing.
S’il est ensi sanez, c’est bien.	If it is thus healed, that is good.
Se ceu, nom autrement ne puet estre sanez;	If this is not done, it cannot be healed in any other way;
et se li tente entre, et ne perce jusc’au doit qui est ou fondement, et a entre ton doi et la tente une coverture espesse de char ou de syfac, et tu vois la fistule a ceu qui enseut la coverture dou keur;	and if the tent goes in and does not reach the bone which is in the foundation, and there is between your finger and the tent a thick covering of pus or of syrup, and you see the fistula above the covering of the flesh;
si le cope des l’encomencement de la fistule, et boute adés avant la tente, et pues le cautere aprés, tant qu’il viegne au chief de la tente;	if you cut off the top of the fistula at its beginning, and then plug it with cotton before putting in the tent, and then cauterize after, until it reaches the tip of the tent;
et sera delivré li tente, et cherra;	and the tent will be released, and will fall out;
puis mondefie celles chars fautrees que semblent une penne d’oisel, et n’en remaigne niant.	then clean those swollen areas that look like a bird's feather, and nothing will remain.
Et si li sans te vaint, et cort entre toi et l’uevre, si le cauterize de feu ou de medicine ague.	And if the pus runs out, and goes between you and the wound, then cauterize it with fire or with medicine.
Car li cauteres de feu assemble II bones choses:	For the fire cautery joins two bone things together:
c’est a savoir, l’arsure de ces chars ajostees, et l’esteinchement de sanc et la sechor de la moistor;	that is to say, the scorching of these heated instruments, and the clotting of blood and the drying of moisture;
puis le cure de tentes moillies em burre ou en choz broiez, tant que li leus giete bowe, et isse fuer li chars arse en la bowe;	then the treatment of wet tents with butter or crushed substance, until the liquid flows out and the heated instruments are inserted into the bowels;
puis cure la plaie des oignemens soudans enjanrans dure char, et sont les medicines seches.	then treat the wound of burning-hot iron brands, and they are dry remedies.
Car quant il est restoree, si est sanee et ne revient mie.	For when it is restored, it is healed and does not return.
Et se fistule vient jusc’a parfont dou fondement, et est esloigniez dou cors, se li boute ton doi ou fondement, et enquier ceu.	And if a fistula comes from the depth of the foundation, and is separated from the body, put your finger into it, and explore it.
Se tu sens la tente, et entre II est li toile ou li syfac ou chars, ou il est pres a percier, si n’i ait fuers que voie de fiance et d’esperance, par l’aministrement de l’une des III manieres:	If you feel the tent, and within it is the thread or the silk or the iron, or it is about to pierce, then do not have fear that leads to doubt and despair, but rather have faith and hope through the administration of one of three remedies:
ou tu le cauterizes si com nos avons dit, ou tu le cope jusc’a fons, ou se tu pues si i met tentes et cure si com premier;	either you cauterize it as we have said, or you cut it to the quick, or if you can, insert tents and treat it as before;
et n’aler mie trop em parfont, que tu ne coper le tenement qui tient le fondement, et viegne li egestions par lai sens volenteit;	and do not go too deep, lest you cut the container that holds the foundation, and cause the contents to spill out through that passageway;
puis le cure, si com nos avons dit;	then treat, as we have said;
par aventure si sera sanez, ou tu esloigne celle coverture et la munde puis qu’elle est copee delez lou fondement, ou par tente ou par autre estrument apointé;	by chance you will be healed, or you should remove that covering and clean it after it has been cut away from the foundation, either by scraping or with some pointed instrument;
puis mondefie cele char fautree qui est en la plaie, tant com tu pues;	then probe the wound as deeply as you can;
puis estudie a restorer la plaie, et a demorer la fistule en la partie defuers le fondement:	then examine how to restore the wound and stop the fistula from spreading in the affected area away from the foundation:
si iert plus legiere chose au malaide.	if it is more convenient for the patient.
Et aucune fois sont fistules selonc ceste maniere:	And sometimes they are like this:ou la fistule est entree en la plaie, et alerge vers le fondement, ou le
et est quant tu boutes la tente en la fistule, et elle est ou costeit dou fondement delez lou cuir desus, si pren une tente percie au chief selonc ceste forme:	and it is when you insert the tent into the fistula, and it is by the side of the foundation underneath the skin, then take a tent pierced at the tip in this shape:si la fistule est plus legiere chose que li cuirs ne soit pas trove, si boutes la tente en la plaie au costeit de la fistule, et elle alerge vers le fondement;
Et i boute .i. fil tort en .ij., et boute la tente a tout le fil en la fistule tant qu’il soit au chief.	And he inserts a twisted thread into it, and inserts the tent along the entire thread into the fistula as far as the top.
S’elle est persans en la marge dou fondement dedens, adonc estrai lou fil de celui pertus, ensi que tu boutes ton doi ou fondement;	If it is pushing from the edge of the foundation inside, then pull out the thread of that opening, just as you would push your finger into the fundament.
et trai le chief dou fil, et assemble les II chiés ensamble, et estraint l’un a l’autre, et le laisse I jor ou II;	and pull on the end of the thread, and bring the two heads together, and press them tightly against each other, and leave it for one or two days;
et le restraint aucune fois, tant que li filz cope ces chars que sont entre dous, et chiecent;	and restrain it some time until the threads cut through the flesh between the two, and they separate;
puis cure la plaie tant qu’elle soit soudee et sanee.	then heal the wound so that it is closed and healed.
Se li fistule ne perce, si la fai percier en toutes les manieres que tu pues, s’ele n’est trop em parfont.	If the fistula does not drain, then have it drained in every way you can, if it is not too deep.
Car il ne covient mie faire por le lacement coper si em parfont, et puis le cure, si com nos avons dit, tant qu’il soit sanez.	For it is not appropriate to cover with a bandage immediately after lancing, and then treat the wound, as we have said, until it has healed.
Li forme dou spatumile espinous dont on fent la fistule si est mout agus d’une, part et trenchans;	The form of the spiny spatomyle for making a fistula is sharp at one end and pointed;
et d’autre part non, por ceu c’on ne cope mie ceu c’on ne doit mie copeir, si com tu vois ci:	and on the other part it is not, so that one does not cut what one should not cut, as you see here:
des emorroydes	of hemorrhoids
Emorrydes sont selonc II manieres:	There are two types of hemorrhoids:
ou elles sont dedens le fondement, ausi com grain de resin, et s’en i a petites et grans, et en cort adés sanc, et s’en i a une ou plusors, et sont defuer le fondement et au chief dou fondement;	either they are inside the fundament, like grains of resin, and there can be small or large ones, and they discharge blood constantly, and there can be one or more, and they are located inside the fundament, and at the head of the fundament;
mais celles qui sont defuer si ont poc de moistor, et encort adés ou un poc d’aigue citrine ou un poc de sanc, et ont la color dou cors;	but those which are displaced have a little moisture, and still more or some yellow water or a little blood, and they have the color of the body;
et li cure de ces qui les ont dedens le fondement, si est que tu comandes au malaide qu’il s’espreigne por aleir en chambres, tant que li fondemens li isse fuer, et c’aperent li filz;	and the treatment of those who have them in the anus, is to command the patient to straining to go to the toilet, until the hemorrhoids come out, and they will be seen.
si te haste, et le pent as tenailles, ou tu le tien a ton ungle, puis le cope en ses racines;	If you are in a hurry, and can grab it with tweezers, or your fingernail, then pull it out at the root;
et se li uncine ne les pueent tenir por ses moistors, si les prent a I drapeil, ou a couton, ou d’une piece de chamelot;	and if they cannot be held with tweezers due to moisture, then they can be grabbed with a piece of cloth, or cotton, or a piece of lamb's wool;
et les estrai a tes dois, puis les cope, et poudre desus aucunes chaudes poudres que soient en leu de cautere;	and pull them out with your fingers, then cut them, and powder some hot powdered medicine on top of the cut;
ou tu les cauterize si com il est dit ou chapistre de cautere, pues les cure d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez;	or you can cauterize them as described in the chapter on cautery, then treat the other hemorrhoids until they are healed;
et se li fondemens ne puet issir, si clisterize le malaide de clistere mordant et aspre por laver ceu qui est ou fondement, si qu’il puist issir apertement;	and if the foundations cannot come out, then cleansing the patient with a sharp and harsh enema to wash away what is in the foundations, so that they can come out clearly;
cant li malaides se preint, et se li fil sont fuer dou fondement, si est li cure legiere;	then the patient defecates, and if the thread is loose from the foundations, then the cure is easy;
et est que tu les preignes a ton ungle ou as tenailles, et les cope, puis les cure si com nos avons dit, tant qu’il soit sanez, et qu’il redoute l’incision par fer.	and you should grasp them with your nail or tweezers, and cut them, then cure them as we have said, until they are healed and afraid of incision by iron.
Si covient que tu amenistre la costure selonc ceste maniere:	You should administer the stitch in this way:
pren I fil tort, et le boute en une aguille, et puis trai le fil au desus et fai percier l’aguille d’autre part, et torne les II chiez dou fil desoz l’aguille, et si soit dou large;	take a twisted thread, and insert it into a needle, then pull the thread through from the top, and pierce the needle from the other side, and return both ends of the thread under the needle, and let it be loose;
et estraint le fil forment, puis noe le fil, et estrai l’aguille, et fai ensi de toz les autres, et en laisse I por corre la superfluiteit dou sanc;	and tighten the thread tightly, then tie a knot in the thread, and remove the needle, and do likewise with all the others, and leave one for controlling the flow of blood;
puis met sus le fondement I drapeil moilliet en oile roset ou en cerote, et met sus le fondement, et comande au malaide k’il repose;	then place a damp cloth soaked in rose oil or cerota over the wound, and instruct the patient to rest.
